[page 555]
pañcamaḥ paricchedaḥ |
raso 'bhimāno 'haṃkāraḥ śṛṅa‍gāra iti gīyate | yo 'rthastasyānvayātkāvyaṃ kamanīyatvamaśnute || 1 ||
viśiṣṭādṛṣṭajanmāyaṃ janmināmantarātmasu | ātmasamyagguṇodbhūtereko hetuḥ prakāśate || 2 ||
śṛṅa‍gārī cetkaviḥ kāvye jātaṃ rasamayaṃ jagat | sa eva cedaśṛṅa‍gārī nīrasaṃ sarvameva tat || 3 ||
paśyati strīti vākye hi na rasaḥ pratibhāsate | vilokayati kānteti vyaktameva pratīyate || 4 ||
kanye kāmayamānaṃ māṃ tvaṃ na kāmayase katham | iti grāmyo 'yamarthātmā vairasyāyaiva kalpate || 5 ||
kāmaṃ kandarpacāṇḍālo mayi vāmākṣi nirdayaḥ | tvayi nirmatsaro diṣṭyetyagrāmyo 'rtho rasāvahaḥ || 6 ||
navo 'rthaḥ sūktiragrāmyā śravyo bandhaḥ sphuṭā śrṛtiḥ | alaukikārthā* yuktiśca rasamāhartumīśate || 7 ||
vakroktiśca rasoktiśca svabhāvoktiśca vāṅmayam | sarvāsu* grāhiṇīṃ tāsu rasoktiṃ pratijānate || 8 ||
*bhāvo janmānubandho 'tha* niṣpattiḥ puṣṭisaṃkarau | hrāsābhāsau śamaḥ śeṣo viśeṣaḥ *pariśeṣavān || 9 ||
vipralambho 'tha saṃbhogastacceṣṭāstatparīṣṭayaḥ* | niruktayaḥ prakīrṇāni premāṇaḥ premapuṣṭayaḥ || 10 ||
﻿[page 556]
nāyikānāyakaguṇāḥ pākādyāḥ premabhaktayaḥ | nānālaṃkārasaṃsṛṣṭeḥ prakārāśca rasoktayaḥ || 11 ||
caturviṃśatirityuktā rasānvayavibhūtayaḥ | svarūpamāsāṃ* yo veda sa kāvyaṃ kartumarhati || 12 ||
ālambanavibhāvebhyaḥ svebhyaḥ svebhyaḥ samunmiṣan | raso ratyādirūpeṇa bhāva ityābhidhīyate || 13 ||
ratirhāsaśca śokaśca krodhotsāhau bhayaṃ tathā | jugupsā vismayaścāṣṭau sthāyibhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 14 ||
stambhastanūruhodbhedo* gadgadaḥ svedavepathū | vaivarṇyamaśrupralaya* ityaṣṭau sāttvikāḥ *smṛtāḥ || 15 ||
smṛtirvitarka *utkaṇṭhā cintā capalatā matiḥ | garvaḥ sneho dhṛtirvrīḍāvahitthaṃ mūḍhatā madaḥ || 16 ||
harṣāmarṣāvasūyerṣyā viṣādo dainyamugratā | trāsaḥ śaṅa‍kā gado glānirunmādaḥ saṃbhramaḥ śramaḥ || 17 ||
nirvedo jāḍyamālasyaṃ nidrā suptaṃ prabuddhatā | iti bhāvāstrayastriṃśadvijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ || 18 ||
ciraṃ citte 'vatiṣṭhante saṃbadhyante 'nubandhibhiḥ | rasatvaṃ pratipadyante *prabuddhāḥ sthāyino 'tra te || 19 ||
rajastamobhyāmaspṛṣṭaṃ manaḥ sattvamihocyate | nirvṛttaye 'sya tadyogātprabhavantīti sāttvikāḥ || 20 ||
viśeṣeṇābhitaḥ kāye sthāyinaṃ cārayanti ye |[page 557] anubhāvādihetūṃstānvadanti vyabhicāriṇaḥ || 21 ||
janitvā ye na jāyante te 'thavā vyabhicāriṇaḥ | smṛtyādayo hi premādau bhavanti na bhavanti ca || 22 ||
ratau saṃcāriṇaḥ sarvān garvasnehau *dhṛtiṃ matim | sthāsnūnevoddhatapreyaḥśāntodātteṣu jānate || 23 ||
saṃskārapāṭavādibhyo 'nubhāvaṃ vā nijāśraye | saṃcāriṇaṃ vā janayan sāttvikaṃ vā sa jāyate || 24 ||
uddīpanavibhāvebhyaḥ smṛtihetau paṭīyasi | anubandho 'nubhāvāderanubandho 'sya* kathyate || 25 ||
vibhāvasyānubhāvasya sāttvikavyabhicāriṇoḥ | saṃyoge *tasya niṣpattimātraṃ *niṣpattirucyate || 26 ||
viṣayāśrayasaṃskāraguṇaprakṛtipāṭavaiḥ | dīpanātiśayaiścāsya prakarṣaḥ puṣṭirucyate || 27 ||
tulyakālabalotpattihetau bhāvāntarodaye | saṃsargastasya yastena saṃkaraḥ sa nigadyate || 28 ||
rasāntaratiraskārādanyadrāgācca tasya yaḥ | bhavatyapacayo vṛddhestaddhrāsaṃ taṃ pracakṣate || 29 ||
hīnapātreṣu tiryakṣu nāyakapratiyogiṣu | gauṇeṣveva padārtheṣu tamābhāsaṃ vijānate* || 30 ||
balavatsūpajāteṣu pratikūleṣu hetuṣu | sarvātmanā samucchedaḥ praśamastasya varṇyate || 31 ||
āśrayātprakṛtervāpi *saṃskārasthairyato 'pi vā |﻿[page 558] yo 'syātyantamanucchedaḥ* sa śeṣa iti śabdyate || 32 ||
śṛṅa‍gārādyā rasā ye ca ye ca śāntoddhatādayaḥ | ye ca ratyādibhedāstānviśeṣānasya manvate || 33 ||
vibhāvaścānubhāvaśca saṃcārī *cāśrayaśca yaḥ | ye ca līlādayo yūnāṃ pariśeṣaḥ* sa kīrtyate || 34 ||
āśrayo yasya ratyādiḥ premāderupajāyate | viṣayo yatra yoṣādau so 'sya* janmādhigacchati || 35 ||
ālambanavibhāvaḥ sa jñānakāraṇamucyate | tenādarādirūpeṇa saṃskārastasya jāyate || 36 ||
*ādṛtaḥ paṭurabhyasta āśrayāderguṇena saḥ | tatprabodhāya mālyartucandanendūdayādayaḥ || 37 ||
uddīpanavibhāvāste sa taiḥ smarati vāñchati | dveṣṭi prayatate 'vaiti manyate vakti ceṣṭate || 38 ||
te 'nubhāvāstadā ye syuḥ svedaromodgamādayaḥ | harṣāmarṣādayo ye ca jñeyāḥ saṃcāriṇo 'tra te || 39 ||
smṛtīcchāyatnajanmāno manovākvāyasaṃśrayāḥ | vilāsā ye varastrīṇāṃ jñeyā līlādayastu te || 40 ||
līlā vilāso vicchittirvibhramaḥ kilakiñcitam | moṭṭāyitaṃ kuṭṭamitaṃ vivvoko lalitaṃ tathā || 41 ||
vihṛtaṃ krīḍitaṃ keliriti strīṇāṃ svabhāvajāḥ | helāhāvādayaścānye jñeyāḥ strīpuṃsayorapi || 42 ||
﻿[page 559]
upasaṃkhyānameteṣāmanubhāveṣu manvate | paścādbhāvānubhūtibhyāṃ smaraṇādyanubhāvavat || 43 ||
smṛtyādayo 'nubhāvāśca bhāvāḥ saṃcāriṇaśca ye | nāṭyeṣu* kriyamāṇāste naṭairabhinayāḥ smṛtāḥ || 44 ||
bhāvo yadā ratirnāma prakarṣamadhigacchati | nādhigacchati cābhīṣṭaṃ vipralambhastadocyate || 45 ||
pūrvānurāgo mānaśca pravāsaḥ karuṇaśca saḥ | puruṣastrīprakāṇḍeṣu catuḥkāṇḍaḥ prakāśate || 46 ||
*prāgasaṃgatayoryūnorabhilāṣaḥ pravartate | saṃkalparamaṇīyo 'nurāgaḥ sa prācya ucyate || 47 ||
aheriva gatiḥ premṇaḥ svabhāvakuṭileti saḥ | ahetormeti* netyukterhetorvā *māna ucyate || 48 ||
deśāntarādibhiryūnorvyavadhānaṃ cirāya yat | nave 'nurāge praụdhe vā pravāsaḥ so 'bhidhīyate || 49 ||
lokāntaragate yūni vallabhe vallabhā yadā | bhṛśaṃ duḥkhāyate dīnā* karuṇaḥ sa tadocyate || 50 ||
ratireveṣṭasaṃprāptau puṣṭaḥ saṃbhoga ucyate | so 'pi pūrvānurāgāderānantaryāccaturvidhaḥ || 51 ||
na vinā vipralambhena saṃbhogaḥ puṣṭimaśnute | kaṣāyite hi vastrādau bhūyānrāgo 'nuṣajyate || 52 ||
﻿[page 560]
strīpuṃsayorvipralambhe *vaicittyākalpanādayaḥ | ceṣṭāviśeṣāḥ saṃbhoge cumbanāliṅa‍ganādayaḥ || 53 ||
vipralambhe 'bhiyogādyaiḥ saṃbhoge sādhvasādibhiḥ | mithaḥparīkṣā yāḥ* premṇo nirdiṣṭāstāḥ parīṣṭayaḥ || 54 ||
vipralambhādiśabdānāṃ lokasiddheṣu vastuṣu | prakṛtyādivibhāgena viniveśā niruktayaḥ || 55 ||
saṃśrṛtya vipralambhārthāngṛdhivañcyoḥ pralambhane | ityādijñāpakājjñeyaḥ prapūrvo vañcane labhiḥ || 56 ||
ādānaṃ ca pratiśrutya visaṃvādanameva ca | kālasya haraṇaṃ cāhuḥ pratyādānaṃ ca vañcanam || 57 ||
pūrvānurāgapūrveṣu vipralambheṣu tatkramāt | viśeṣadyotakeneha vyupasargeṇa sūcyate || 58 ||
pratiśravo hi pūrvānurāge* vakrekṣitādibhiḥ | abhīṣṭāliṅa‍ganādīnāmadānaṃ* hrībhayādibhiḥ || 59 ||
māne nivāraṇaṃ teṣāṃ* visaṃvādanamucyate | ayathāvatpradānaṃ vā vyalīkasmaraṇādibhiḥ || 60 ||
pravāse kālaharaṇaṃ vyaktameṣāṃ pratīyate | proṣyāgateṣvihaitāni kāntāḥ kānteṣu yuñjate || 61 ||
pratyādānaṃ punasteṣāṃ karuṇe* ko na manyate | svayaṃ dattāni hi vidhistāni tatrāpakarṣati || 62 ||
﻿[page 561]
*pralambhetyatra yadi vā vañcanāmātravācini | vinā *samāse caturāścaturo 'rthānniyuñjate* || 63 ||
vividhaśca viruddhaśca vyāviddhaśca krameṇa saḥ | viniṣiddhaśca pūrvānurāgādiṣu* viṣajyate || 64 ||
pūrvānurāge vividhaṃ vañcanaṃ vrīḍitādibhiḥ | māne viruddhaṃ tatprāhuḥ punarīrṣyāyitādibhiḥ || 65 ||
vyāviddhaṃ dīrghakālatvātpravāse tatpratīyate* | viniṣiddhaṃ tu karuṇe* karuṇatvena gīyate || 66 ||
rāgo 'nu saha paścādvānurūpo 'nugato 'pi vā | yūnorapūrvaḥ pūrvānurāgaśabdena śabdyate || 67 ||
rājate rañcatervāpi rāgaḥ *karaṇabhāvayoḥ | *ghañānyatkārake bhāve nalopena niyamyate || 68 ||
mānyate preyasā yena yaṃ priyatvena manyate | manute vā mimīte vā premamānaḥ sa kathyate || 69 ||
mahābhāṣyakṛtaḥ ko 'sāvanumāna iti smṛteḥ | lyuḍanto 'pi na puṃliṅa‍go mānaśavdaḥ praduṣyati || 70 ||
yatrāṅa‍ganā yuvānaśca vasate na vasanti ca | sa pravāsaḥ praśabdena pratīpārthena kathyate || 71 ||
*citotkaṇṭhādibhiśceto bhṛśaṃ vāsayatīha yaḥ | pravāsayati vā yūnaḥ sa pravāso nirucyate || 72 ||
﻿[page 562]
prapūrvako vasirjñeyaḥ kāritāntaḥpramāpaṇe* | tūṣṇīṃ pravāsayedenamiti vṛddhānuśāsanāt || 73 ||
abhūtotpādanāyāṃ kṛñ dṛṣṭaḥ kuru ghaṭaṃ yathā | dṛṣṭaścoccāraṇe cauraṃkāramākrośatītivat || 74 ||
dṛṣṭo 'vasthāpane 'śmānamitaḥ kuru yathocyate | abhyañjane 'pi ca yathā *pādau me* *sarpiṣā kuru || 75 ||
mūrcchāvilāpau kurute kurute sāhase manaḥ | karoti *cittaṃ duḥkhena yo 'sau karuṇa ucyate || 76 ||
bhujiḥ pālanakauṭilyābhyavahārānubhūtiṣu | bhunakti bhugno bhūṅkte 'nnaṃ bhūṅkte sukhamitīṣyate || 77 ||
samīcīnārthasaṃpūrvāttato ghañ‌pratyaye sati | bhāve vā kārake vāpi rūpaṃ saṃbhoga iṣyate || 78 ||
sa *pālanārthaḥ pūrvānurāgānantara ucyate | utpannā hi ratistāsminnānukūlyena pālyate || 79 ||
sa mānānantaraṃ prāptaḥ kauṭilyārthaṃ vigāhate | svato 'pi kuṭilaṃ prema kiṃ nu* mānānvaye sati || 80 ||
pravāsānantare tasyābhyavahārārthateṣyate | tatra hyupoṣitairannamiva nirviśyate ratiḥ || 81 ||
karuṇānantaragato 'nubhāvārthaḥ* sa kathyate | *vistrambhavadbhirasminhi *sukhamevānubhūyate || 82 ||
﻿[page 563]
yadi vā bhoga ityasya saṃprayogārthavācinaḥ | samā* samāse *catvāro viśeṣāstamupāsate* || 83 ||
sa saṃkṣipto 'tha* saṃkīrṇaḥ saṃpūrṇaḥ samyagṛddhimān | anantaropadiṣṭeṣu saṃbhogeṣūpapadyate || 84 ||
nave hi saṅa‍game prāyo yuvānaḥ sādhvasādibhiḥ | saṃkṣiptāneva ratyarthamupacārānprayuñjate || 85 ||
mānasyānantare teṣāṃ vyalīkasmaraṇādibhiḥ | roṣaśeṣānusaṃdhānātsaṃkaraḥ kena vāryate || 86 ||
saṃpūrṇaḥ pūrṇakāmānāṃ kāmināṃ proṣyasaṃgame | utkaṇṭhitānāṃ bhūyiṣṭhamupabhogaḥ pravartate || 87 ||
pratyāgate 'pi yatraiṣā ratipuṣṭiḥ priye jane* | sā kimāvarṇyate yūnāṃ tatraiva mṛtajīvite || 88 ||
pūrvānurāgaḥ* pūrvāṇāṃ vyutpattibhirudāhṛtaḥ | anantarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ tatsamāse niruktayaḥ || 89 ||
vṛttistatrājahatsvārthā jahatsvārthāpi vartatām | pradhānamanupaskṛtya na tadartho nivartate || 90 ||
prathamānantare vṛtterajahatsvārthateṣyate | nātyantamajahatsvārthāṃ tāṃ mānānantare viduḥ || 91 ||
pravāsānantare tvīṣadajahatsvārthateṣyate | karuṇārthasya gandho 'pi nāstyeva tadanantare || 92 ||
﻿[page 564]
aṣṭamīcandrakaḥ* *kundacaturthī *suvasantakaḥ | *āndolanacaturthyekaśālmalī* madanotsavaḥ* || 93 ||
*udakakṣveḍikāśo*kottaṃsikā *cūtabhañjikā | puṣpāvacāyikāṃ* cūtalatikā* bhūtamātṛkā* || 94 ||
kadambayuddhāni* navapatrikā* *bisakhādikā | *śakrārcā kaumudī* *yakṣarātrirabhyūṣakhādikā* || 95 ||
*navekṣubhakṣikā toyakrīḍā* *prekṣādidarśanam |﻿[page 565] *dyūtāni *madhupānaṃ ca prakīrṇānīti jānate || 96 ||
﻿[page 566]
nityo naimittikaścānyaḥ* sāmānyo 'nyo viśeṣavān | pracchanno 'nyaḥ prakāśo 'nyaḥ kṛtrimākṛtrimāvubhau || 97 ||
sahajāhāryanāmānau parau yauvanajo 'paraḥ | *vistrambhajaśca premāṇo dvādaśaite maharddhayaḥ || 98 ||
cakṣuḥprītirmanaḥsaṅa‍gaḥ saṃkalpotpattisaṃtatiḥ | pralāpo jāgaraḥ kārśyamaratirviṣayāntare || 99 ||
lajjāvisarjanaṃ vyādhirunmādo mūrcchanaṃ muhuḥ | maraṇaṃ ceti vijñeyāḥ krameṇa premapuṣṭayaḥ || 100 ||
*nāyakaḥ pratipūrvo 'sāvupapūrvo 'nunāyakaḥ | nāyikā pratipurvāsāvupapūrvānunāyikā || 101 ||
nāyikānāyakābhāsāvubhayābhāsa ityapi |﻿[page 567] tiryakṣu ca tadābhāsa* iti dvādaśa nāyakāḥ || 102 ||
teṣu sarvaguṇopetaḥ kathāvyāpī ca nāyakaḥ | anyāyavāṃstaducchedya uddhataḥ pratināyakaḥ || 103 ||
tataḥ kaiścidguṇairhīnaḥ pūjyaścaivopanāyakaḥ | samo nyūno 'pi vā tasya kanīyānanunāyakaḥ || 104 ||
syātkathāvyāpinī sarvaguṇayuktā ca nāyikā | heturīrṣyāyitādīnāṃ sapatnī pratināyikā || 105 ||
tataḥ kaiścidguṇairhīnā pūjyā caivopanāyikā | samā nyūnāpi vā kiṃcitkanīyasyanunāyikā || 106 ||
tadābhāsāstathaiva syurbhedāścaiṣāṃ* guṇādibhiḥ | nāyakastatra guṇata uttamo madhyamo 'dhamaḥ || 107 ||
*prakṛteḥ sāttvikaḥ sa syādrājasastāmasastathā | sādhāraṇo 'nanyajātiḥ* sa vijñeyaḥ parigrahāt || 108 ||
uddhato lalitaḥ śānta udātto dhairyavṛttitaḥ | śaṭho dhṛṣṭo 'nukūlaśca dakṣiṇaśca pravṛttitaḥ || 109 ||
guṇato nāyikāpi syāduttamā madhyamādhamā | mugdhā madhyā pragalbhā ca vayasā kauśalena vā* || 110 ||
dhīrādhīrā ca dhairyeṇa svānyadīyāparigrahāt | ụ̄dhānụ̄dhopayamanātkramājjyeṣṭhā kanīyasī || 111 ||
mānarddheruddhatodāttā śāntā ca lalitā ca sā | sāmānyā ca punarbhūśca svairiṇī ceti vṛttitaḥ || 112 ||
﻿[page 568]
ājīvatastu gaṇikā rūpājīvā vilāsinī | avasthāto 'parāścāṣṭau vijñeyāḥ khaṇḍitādayaḥ || 113 ||
*nidrākulitatāmrākṣo nārīnakhavibhūṣitaḥ | prātareti priyo yasyāḥ *kutaścitseha khaṇḍitā || 114 ||
cāṭukāramapi prāṇanāthaṃ kopādapāsya yā | paścāttāpamavāpnoti kalahāntaritā tu sā || 115 ||
dutīmaharahaḥ preṣya kṛtvā saṃketakaṃ kvacit | yasyā na militaḥ preyānvipralabdheti tāṃ viduḥ || 116 ||
sā tu vāsakasajjā syātsajjite vāsaveśmani | priyamāstīrṇaparyaṅa‍kā* bhūṣitā yā pratīkṣate || 117 ||
svādhīnapatikā sā tu yasyāḥ pārśvaṃ na muñcati | priyaścitraratakrīḍāsukhāsvādanalolupaḥ || 118 ||
puṣpeṣupīḍitā kāntaṃ yāti yā sābhisārikā | priyo deśāntare yasyāḥ sā tu proṣitabhartṛkā || 119 ||
yasyāḥ samucte 'pyahni pravāsī naiti vallabhaḥ | virahotkaṇṭhitā sā tu *dvātriṃśaditi nāyikāḥ || 120 ||
hīnapātrāṇi śeṣāṇi pīṭhamardo vidūṣakaḥ | viṭaceṭau patākāśca sakhyaścaiṣāṃ parigrahaḥ || 121 ||
mahākulīnataudārye mahābhāgyaṃ kṛtajñatā | rūpayauvanavaidagdhya*śīlasaubhāgyasaṃpadaḥ || 122 ||
﻿[page 569]
manitodāravākyatvamadaridrā*nurāgitā | dvādaśeti guṇānāhurnāyakeṣvābhigāmikān* || 123 ||
*mṛdvīkānālikerāmrapākādyāḥ pākabhaktayaḥ | nīlīkusumbhamañjiṣṭhārāgādyā rāgabhaktayaḥ || 124 ||
antarvyājabahirvyājanirvyājā vyājabhaktayaḥ | dharmārthakāmodarkāśca *premasūdarkabhaktayaḥ || 125 ||
vākyavacca prabandheṣu rasālaṃkārasaṃkarān | niveśayantyanaucityaparīhāreṇa sūrayaḥ || 126 ||
caturvṛttyaṅa‍gasaṃpannaṃ* caturodāttanāyakam | caturvargaphalaṃ ko na prabandhaṃ bāndhavīyati || 127 ||
mukhaṃ pratimukhaṃ garbho 'vamarśaśca manīṣibhiḥ | smṛtānirvahaṇaṃ ceti prabandhe pañca saṃdhayaḥ || 128 ||
avistṛtamasaṃkṣiptaṃ śravyavṛttaṃ *sugandhi ca | bhinnasargāntavṛttaṃ ca kāvyaṃ loko 'bhinandati || 129 ||
puropavanarāṣṭrādimudrāśramavarṇanaiḥ | deśasaṃpatprabandhasya rasotkarṣāya kalpate || 130 ||
*ṛturātriṃ*divārkendūdayāstamayakīrtanaiḥ | kālaḥ kāvyeṣu saṃpanno rasapuṣṭiṃ niyacchati || 131 ||
rājakanyākumārastrīsenāsenāṅa‍gabhaṅgibhiḥ |﻿[page 570] *pātrāṇāṃ varṇanaṃ kāvye rasastroto 'dhitiṣṭhati || 132 ||
udyānasalilakrīḍāmadhupānaratotsavāḥ | vipralambhā vivāhāśca ceṣṭāḥ kāvye rasāvahāḥ || 133 ||
mantradūtaprayāṇājināyakābhyudayādibhiḥ | puṣṭiḥ puruṣakārasya rasaṃ kāvyeṣu varṣati || 134 ||
nāvarṇanaṃ nagaryāderdoṣāya viduṣāṃ matam | yadi śailarturātryādervarṇanenaiva *tuṣyati || 135 ||
guṇataḥ prāgupanyasya nāyakaṃ tena vidviṣām | nirākaraṇamityeṣa mārgaḥ prakṛtisundaraḥ || 136 ||
*vaṃśavīryaśrutādīni varṇayitvā riporapi | tajjayānnāyakotkarṣakathanaṃ ca dhinoti naḥ || 137 ||

athaiṣāṃ lakṣaṇodāharaṇāni—

*tatra,

manonukūleṣvartheṣu sukhasaṃvedanaṃ ratiḥ | *asaṃprayogaviṣayā saiva prītirnigadyate || 138 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya bhāvo yathā—

‘harastu kiṃcitpa*rivṛttadhairyaścandroyārambha ivāmburāśiḥ | umāmukhe bimbaphalādharoṣṭhe byāpārayāmāsa vilocanāni || 1 ||’

atra bimboṣṭhatvādibhirmanonukūle pārvatīmukhe vilocanavyāpārānumito maheśvarasyābhilāṣaviśeṣaḥ *sāttvikāderanu*tpādātsukhānubhavasyotpattimātramanumāpayati ||

﻿[page 571]

tadrūpeṇaiva sāttvikotpattau janma yathā—

‘*abhūdvaraḥ kaṇṭakitaprakoṣṭhaḥ khinnāṅa‍guliḥ saṃvavṛte kumārī | *tasmindvaye tatkṣaṇamātmavṛttiḥ samaṃ vibhakteva manobhavena || 2 ||’

atra svedaromodbhedayoḥ* sāttvikayorutpādādrasasya ratirūpeṇāvirbhāvo 'vagamyate |

janmaiva *saṃcāryutpattau yathā—

‘*tayorapāṅa‍gapravicāritāni kiṃcivdya*vasthāpitasaṃhṛtāni | hrīyantraṇāmānaśire manojñāmanyonyalolāni vilocanāni || 3 ||’

atra hrīḥ saṃcāribhāvo jāyamāno rasasya janma jñāpayati |

*tadevānubhāvotpattau yathā—

‘tataḥ sunandāvacanāvasāne lajjāṃ *mṛdūkṛtya narendrakanyā | dṛṣṭyā prasādāmalayā kumāraṃ pratyagrahītsaṃvaraṇasrajeva || 4 ||’

atra dṛṣṭilakṣaṇaḥ śarīrārambho 'nubhāvo* bhavan rasāvirbhāvaṃ lakṣayati | anubhāvāderanekasyaikasya vā punarutpattiranubandhaḥ | so 'nekasya yathā—

‘vivṛṇvatī śailasutāpi bhāvamaṅa‍gaiḥ *kvacidbālakadambakalpaiḥ | sācīkṛtā cārutareṇa tasthau mukhena paryastavilocanena || 5 ||’
﻿[page 572]

atra devyāḥ *smarārau pūrvamutpannā ratiḥ sābhilāṣatadavalokana*viviktavasantādibhiruddīpyamānā romāñcāvahitthalakṣaṇābhyāṃ sāttvikavyabhicāribhyāmanubadhyate ||

ekasyaiva punaḥ *punaryathā—

‘yāntyā muhurvalitakaṃdharamānanaṃ ta- dāvṛttavṛntaśatapattranibhaṃ vahantyā | digdho 'mṛtena ca viṣeṇa ca pakṣmalākṣyā gāḍhaṃ nikhāta iva me hṛdaye kaṭākṣaḥ || 6 ||’

atra mālatyā mādhavaviṣaye pūrvamutpannā ratirvasantāvatāra*tatsaṃnidhiviśeṣapradarśanādibhiruddīpyamānā punaḥ punarutpannena valitagrīvakaṭākṣavikṣepalakṣaṇena śarīrārambhānubhāvenānubadhyate | atraiva* mādhavasya mālatīviṣaye tadaharevotpannā ratistairevoddīpanairuddīpyamānā harṣadhṛtismṛtimativyādhyādibhiḥ saṃcāribhāvairvāgārambheṇa cānubhāvenānubadhyate ||

ratirūpeṇaiva rasaniṣpattiryathā—

‘taṃ vīkṣya vepathumatī sarasāṅa‍gyaṣṭi- rnikṣepa* eva padamuddhṛtamarpayantī* | mārgācalavyatikarākuliteva sindhuḥ śailādhirājatanayā na yayau na tasthau || 7 ||’

atra janmāntarānubhavasaṃskārātpratikūle 'pi śūlini *śailātmajāyāḥ sarvakālamevāvicchinnā ratiści*raviyuktasya duścareṇāpi tapasā prārthanīya﻿[page 573]-saṃgamasya tasyākasmikadarśanenoddīpyamānā sadyaḥsamupajāyamānasāttvikasvedastambhavepathūpalakṣitairharṣa*smṛtyāvegasādhvasādibhirvyabhicāribhāvaiḥ* *padanikṣepalakṣaṇena ca śarīrānubhāvena saṃsṛjyate | so 'yaṃ vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyoge* ratirūpeṇa raso niṣpadyate |

ratirūpeṇaiva *rasapuṣṭiryathā—

‘pīnaśroṇi gabhīranābhi nibhṛtaṃ madhye bhṛśoccastanaṃ pāyādvaḥ parirabdhamabdhiduhituḥ kāntena kāntaṃ vapuḥ | svāvāsānupaghātanirvṛtamanāstatkālamīladdṛśe yasmai so 'cyutanābhipadmavasatirvedhāḥ śivaṃ dhyāyati || 8 ||’

atra sarvadaiva śrīvatsalakṣmaṇo lakṣmīviṣaye mahākulīnataudāryasthirānurāgitārūpayauvanavaidagdhyaśīlasaubhāgyamahābhāgyādibhiḥ samutpannā ratistadavayavaviśeṣakāmanīyakavibhāvanenoddīpanavibhāvātiśayenoddīpyamānāṃ brahmaṇaḥ samakṣamapyāliṅa‍ganalakṣaṇena śarīrārambhānubhāvenānumīyamānāṃ lajjāpraṇāśalakṣaṇāṃ premapuṣṭeraṣṭamīmavasthāmadhyāste | atra cānuktā api sāttvikā vyabhicāriṇo 'nye 'pi cānubhāvaviśeṣāḥ pratīyante | śriyo 'pi ca samagrātmaguṇasaṃpadāśraye śrīvatsalakṣmaṇi tathābhūtā tadabhyadhikā vā* ratiḥ pravṛddhapremapriyatamāliṅa‍ganalakṣaṇenoddīpanavibhāvevoddīpyamānā nayananimīlanānumeyāṃ samastasāttvikānubhāvavyabhicārihetuṃ premapuṣṭeruttamā*mavasthāmāśrayati | so 'yaṃ viṣayasaundaryādāśrayaprakṛteḥ saṃskārapāṭavāduddīpanātiśayācca parāṃ koṭimāvahan rasaḥ puṣṭa ityucyate | atraiva brahmaṇaḥ śriyaṃ prati manoharā mameyaṃ sṛṣṭiriti, ratnākarasyeyamātmajeti, candrā-﻿[page 574]mṛtādīnāmiyaṃ sodaryeti, viṣṇoriyaṃ priyatameti, kāmasyeyaṃ jananītyādibhya ālambanebhyaḥ samutpannā prītiḥ svāvāsānupaghātinā śarīrasaṃniveśena dṛṅmimīlanajanitayā ca tadupaghātaśaṅa‍kayoddīpyamānā tatkṣaṇopajāyamānatayā āvegasmṛtivitarkonmādamohacintādibhirvyabhicāribhāvaistadanumeyaiśca stambhavepathuprabhṛtisāttvikaiḥ śivānudhyānalakṣaṇena budhdyārambhānubhāvena saṃsṛjyamānā paraṃ prakarṣamārohantī* pratīyate ||

ratau bhayādisaṃkaro yathā—

‘rāhoścandrakalāmivānanacarīṃ daivātsamāsādya me dasyorasya kṛpāṇapātaviṣayādācchindataḥ preyasīm | ātaṅa‍kādvikalaṃ drutaṃ karuṇayā vikṣobhitaṃ vismayāt krodhena jvalitaṃ mudā vikasitaṃ cetaḥ kathaṃ vartatām || 9 ||’

atra mādhavasya mālatyāṃ pūrvamutpannā ratistadavasthā*lokanādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānā bhayaśokavismayakrodhaharṣairapi rasāntaraiḥ pṛthakpṛthagvibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyogānniṣpadyamānaiḥ saṃkīryamāṇā manovāgbuddhi*śarīrārambhānubhāvairbhayādyanurūpaiśca sāttvikavyabhicāribhiḥ saṃparke paraṃ prakarṣamārohantī pratīyate | tatra cetaso vaikalyādiparibhāvanaṃ manaārambhaḥ, vākyoccāraṇaṃ vāgārambhaḥ, rāhoriva dasyoścandrakalāmiva preyasīmityādi budhdyārambhaḥ, *ācchindata ityādi śarīrārambhaḥ, bhayādīnāṃ ca pañcānāmapi yathākramaṃ rāhoriti, candrakalāmivānanacarīmiti, daivātsamāsādya me iti, dasyorasya kṛpāṇapātaviṣayāditi, ācchindataḥ preyasīmityālambanavibhāvāstatsvarūpaparibhāvanānyuddīpanavibhāvāḥ, vikalam, ﻿[page 575]drutam, vikṣobhitam, *jvalitam, vikasitaṃ ceta* ityanubhāvāḥ, ātaṅa‍kakaruṇāvismayakrodhamudanurūpāśca kampāśrustambhavaivarṇyaromāñcādayaḥ sāttvikāḥ, mohaviṣādavita*rkogratādhṛtyādayo vyabhicāriṇaścānumīyamānā niṣpattihetavo bhavanti | so 'yaṃ tulyakālabalotpattikāraṇānāṃ bhayādiniṣpattīnāṃ ratau saṃsargaḥ saṃkara ityucyate ||

ratirūpeṇa rasaprakarṣasya hrāso yathā—

‘kopo yatra *bhrukuṭiracanā nigraho yatra maunaṃ yatrānyonya*smitamanunayo dṛṣṭipātaḥ prasādaḥ | tasya premṇastadidamadhunā vaiśasaṃ paśya jātaṃ tvaṃ pādānte luṭhasi na ca me manyumokṣaḥ khalāyāḥ || 10 ||’

atra yoṣiti roṣākhyarasāntaratiraskārātpuruṣe *cānyarāgādratiprakarṣasya *hrāso 'vasīyate |

ratirūpeṇa hīnapātreṣu rasābhāso yathā—

‘vikkiṇaï māhamāsambhi *pāmaro pāraḍiṃ vaïlleṇa | *diṭṭhiṃ samummure sāmalīa thaṇae ṇiacchanto || 11 ||’
[vikrīṇīte māghamāse pāmaraḥprāvarakaṃ balīvardena | dṛṣṭiṃ samurmure śyāmalyāḥ stanake niyacchan ||]
﻿[page 576]

tiryakṣu yathā—

‘*pāaḍiaṃ sohaggaṃ taṃbāe *uaha goṭṭhamajjhammi | duṭṭhavasahassa siṃge acchiuḍaṃ kaṇḍuantīe || 12 ||’
[prakaṭitaṃ saubhāgyaṃ gavā paśyata goṣṭhamadhye | duṣṭavṛṣabhasya śṛṅa‍ge 'kṣipuṭaṃ kaṇḍūyamānayā ||]

nāyakapratiyogiṣu yathā—

‘pulaaṃ *jaṇenti dahakaṃdharassa rāhavasarā sarīrammi | jaṇaasuāphaṃsama*hagghavia *karaalāaṭṭhiavimukkā || 13 ||’
[pulakaṃ janayanti daśakaṃdharasya rāghavaśarāḥ śarīre | janakasutāsparśamahārghā iva karatalākṛṣṭavimuktāḥ ||]

gauṇeṣu yathā—

‘uvvahaï *navataṇaṃkuraromañcapasāhiāiṃ* aṃgāiṃ | *pāusalacchīa paoharehiṃ paḍivelliovijjho* || 14 ||’
[udvahati navatṛṇāṅa‍kuraromāñcaprasādhitānyaṅa‍gāni | prāvṛṭlakṣmyāḥ payodharābhyāṃ pratiprerito vindhyaḥ ||]

*taṃ ete catvāro 'pi rasābhāsā ucyante ||

ratāveva lajjāroṣarūparasāntarayoḥ praśamo yathā—

‘dṛṣṭe locanavanmanāṅyukulitaṃ pārśvasthitevakrava -nnyagbhūtaṃ bahirāsitaṃ pulakavatsparśaṃ samātanvati | ﻿[page 577] nīvībandhavadāgataṃ śithilatāmābhāṣamāṇe tato mānenāpagataṃ hriyeva sudṛśaḥ pādaspṛśi preyasi || 15 ||’

atra balavabhdyāṃ priyapremānunayābhyāṃ hrīroṣayorupaśamaḥ kriyate ||

ratāveva roṣarūparasasya śeṣo yathā—

‘eṣyatyutsukamāgate *vicalitaṃ saṃbhāṣiṇi sphāritaṃ saṃśliṣyatyaruṇaṃ gṛhītavasane kopāñcitabhrūlatam | māninyāścaraṇānativyatikare bāṣpāmbupūrṇaṃ* kṣaṇāccakṣurjātamaho prapañcacaturaṃ jātāgasi preyasi || 16 ||’

atra kasyāścidbalavatā premṇonmūlitasyāpi mānasya *śeṣo 'nuvartate |

ta ete *bhāvādayo daśāpi rasaprakārā hāsādiṣvapi *prāyo dṛśyante | granthagauravabhayātkva*citkvacidudāhriyante ||

tatra

*nyaṅa‍gavrīḍādibhiścetovikāro hāsa ucyate |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya bhāvo yathā—

‘kanakakalaśasvacche rādhāpayodharamaṇḍale navajaladharaśyāmāmātmadyutiṃ pratibimbitām | asitasicayaprāntabhrāntyā muhurmuhurutkṣipan jayati janitavrīḍāhāsaḥ priyāhasito hariḥ || 17 ||’

atra *rādhāyā harinyaṅa‍gād, harestu vrīḍāto hāsasya sattāmātraṃ pratīyate ||

﻿[page 578]
śokaścittasya vaidhuryamabhīṣṭavirahādibhiḥ || 139 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘hṛdayānnāpayāto 'si dikṣu sarvāsu *dṛśyase | vatsa rāma gato 'sīti saṃtāpādanumīyase || 18 ||’

atra daśasthasya rāmaviyogādutpannastadguṇasmaraṇādibhiruddīpitaścintāsaṃtāpādirvāgārambheṇa cānuṣajyamānaḥ śokarūpeṇa raso niṣpadyate ||

pratikūleṣu taikṣṇyasya prabodhaḥ krodha ucyate |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘mayyevamasma*raṇadāruṇacittavṛttau vṛtaṃ rahaḥ praṇayamapratipadyamāne* | bhedādbhuvoḥ kuṭilayoratilohitākṣya bhagnaṃ śarāsanamivātiruṣā smarasya || 19 ||’

atra yadyapi *vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyogalakṣaṇāyā rasaniṣpatteḥ 'adhikamatiruṣātilohitākṣyā’ iti prakarṣanimittamatiśabdopādānaṃ vidyate, tathāpyuttamanāyikāśrayaḥ priyaviṣaye na roṣaḥ prakarṣamāsādayati ||

kāryārambheṣu saṃrambhaḥ stheyānutsāha iṣyate || 140 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘mūrdhnā jāmbavato 'bhivādya caraṇāvāpṛcchya senāpatī- nāśvāsyāśrumukhānmuhuḥ priyasakhīnpreṣyānsamādiśya ca | ārambhaṃ jagṛhe mahendraśikharādambhonidherlaṅa‍ghane raṃhasvī raghunāthapādarajasāmuccaiḥ smaranmārutiḥ || 20 ||’

atrābhivādanapraśnāśvāsanasamādeśanādriśikharārohaṇeṣṭadevatā*smaraṇānāṃ ﻿[page 579]pūrvaraṅa‍gaparyavasāyitvenānuddīpanavibhāvatvādanutsāhānubhāvatvācca nāyamanubandho niṣpattiḥ prakarṣo vā bhavati ||

bhayaṃ cittasya vaiklavyaṃ raudrādijanitaṃ viduḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘mantrānmṛtyujito japadbhirasakṛdhdyāyadbhiriṣṭānsurān śuṣyattālubhirākulākulapadairnirvāgbhirutkampibhiḥ | adhvanyairiha jīviteśamahiṣavyādhūmradhūmāvilā laṅa‍ghyante karimāṃsaghasmara*raṇatkauleyakāḥ pallayaḥ || 21 ||’

atra yadyapi pallīnāmālambanatvam, *tadviśeṣaṇayoruddīpanatvam, mantrajapāderanubhāvatvam, tāluśoṣādīnāṃ vyabhicāritvamiti vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyogo 'sti, tathāpi mantrajapeṣṭadevatānudhyānayorlaṅa‍ghanopāyaparatvānna bhayarūpeṇa *rasasya niṣpattiḥ | adhvanyānāṃ hi tanniṣpattāvalpasattvatayā stambhamohamūrcchāmaraṇādibhirupāyaprayogo na ghaṭate ||

jugupsā garhaṇārthānāṃ doṣasaṃdarśanādibhiḥ || 141 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānugamo yathā—

‘*he hasta dakṣiṇa mṛtasya śiśordvijasya jīvātave visṛja śūdramunau kṛpāṇam | rāmasya gātramasi nirbharagarbhakhinnasītā- pravāsanapaṭoḥ karuṇā kutaste || 22 ||’

atra yadyapi dvijaśiśorjīvanāya munirapi śūdro vadhya iti na rāmasyātmakarmanindā tathāpyanapakāriṇaṃ* jighāṃsato *ghṛṇānuvartata eva | sītā-﻿[page 580]parityāgaviṣayatvenaivātra jugupsānugamo grahītavyaḥ | *śambukaviṣaye punarasyā janmamātrameveti ||

vismayaścittavistāraḥ padārthātiśayādibhiḥ |

tadrūpeṇa *rasaniṣpattiryathā—

‘kṛṣṇenāmba gatena *rantumasakṛnmṛdbhakṣitā svecchayā satyaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ka evamāha *musalī mithyāmba paśyānanam | vyādehīti *vikāsite ca vadane dṛṣṭa‍vā samastaṃ jaga- nmātā yasya jagāma vismayapadaṃ pāyātsa vaḥ keśavaḥ || 23 ||’

atra śiśormuṃkhe jagaddarśanamālambanavibhāvaḥ, tatsāmagryaśaiśavādyā*locanamuddīpanavibhāvaḥ, vismayavaśaṃ jagāmetyanenānupāttā api sarve saṃcā*riṇo 'nubhāvāśca gṛhyante ||

stambhaśceṣṭāpratīghāto bhayarāgāmayādibhiḥ || 142 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya puṣṭiryathā—

‘taṃ tāṇa* haacchāaṃ ṇiccalaloaṇasihaṃ paütthapaāvaṃ | ālekkhapaīvāṇiva ṇiaaṃ paaïcaḍulattaṇaṃ pi vialiaṃ || 24 ||’
[tatteṣāṃ hatacchāyaṃ niścalalocanaśikhaṃ proṣitapratāpam | ālekhyapradīpānāmiva nijakaṃ prakṛticaṭulatvamapi vigalitam ||]

ayaṃ ca puṣṭo 'pi sāttvikatvāt sadaivānyānuyāyīti nānubhāvādibhiranubadhyate ||

harṣādbhutabhayādibhyo romāñco romavikriyā |
﻿[page 581]

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘karimari aālagajjirajalaāsaṇipaüṇapaḍirao eso | païṇo dhaṇuravakaṃkhiṇi romaṃcaṃ kiṃ muhā vahasi || 25 ||’
[bandi akālagarjanajaladāśanipatanapratirava eṣaḥ | patyurdhanūravākāṅa‍kṣaṇaśīle romāñca kiṃ mudhā vahasi ||]

asyāpi sāttvikatvādanyānubandhādayo na jāyante |

madapramadapīḍādervaisvaryaṃ gadgadaṃ viduḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘pipipriya sasasvayaṃ mumumukhāsavaṃ dehi me tatatyaja dududrutaṃ bhabhabhabhājanaṃ kāñcanam | iti skhalitajalpitaṃ madavaśātkuraṅa‍gīdṛśaḥ prage hasitahetave sahacarībhiradhyeyata || 26 ||’

*atrāpi sāttvikatvānniṣpanno nānyairanubadhyate ||

vaprurjalodgamaḥ khedo ratigharmaśramādibhiḥ || 143 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘himavyapāyādviśadādharāṇāmā*pāṇḍurībhūtamukhacchavīnām | khedodgamaḥ kiṃpuruṣāṅa‍ganānāṃ cakre padaṃ *citraviśeṣakeṣu || 27 ||’

atrāpi pūrvavadanyānuṣaṅa‍go na bhavati ||

rāgaroṣabhayādibhyaḥ kampo gātrasya vepathuḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘mā garvamudvaha kapolatale cakāsti kāntasvahastalikhitā mama mañjarīti | ﻿[page 582] anyāpi kiṃ na sakhi bhājanamīdṛśānāṃ vairī na cedbhavati vepathurantarāyaḥ || 28 ||’

ayamapi prāgvadevānyairnānugamyate* |

viṣādamadaroṣādervarṇānyatvaṃ vivarṇatā || 144 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘sahi *sāhasu teṇa samaṃ ahaṃ pi kiṃ ṇiggaā *pahāammi | aṇṇacia dīsaï jeṇa dappaṇe kāvi sā sumuho || 29 ||’
[sakhi sādhaya tena samamahamapi kiṃ nirgatā prabhāte | anyaiva dṛśyate yena darpaṇe kāpi sā sumukhī ||]

ayamapi nānyairanubadhyate ||

aśru netrodgataṃ vāri duḥkhaśokapraharṣajam |

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘utpakṣmaṇornayanayoruparuddhavṛtti bāṣsaṃ kuru sthiratayā śithilānubandham | asminnalakṣitanatonnatabhūmibhāge mārge padāni khalu te viṣamībhavanti || 30 ||’

atra bāṣpaśavdena locanāśrayamaśrūcyate na kaṇṭhādyāśrayo duḥkhāveśaḥ | yathā—‘vilalāpa sa bāppagadgadam', ‘ *muhurmagnaḥ kaṇṭhe taralayati bāṣpaḥ stanataṭīm’ ityādi* ||

pralayastīvraduḥkhāderindriyāstamayo mataḥ || 145 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘tīvrābhiṣaṅa‍gaprabhaveṇa vṛttiṃ mohena saṃstambhayatendriyāṇām | ajñātabhartṛvyasanā muhūrtaṃ kṛtopakāreva ratirbabhūva || 31 ||’
﻿[page 583]

atra mohaśabdena mūrcchocyate, na vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇo mohaḥ ||

smṛtiḥ pūrvānubhūtārthaviṣayaṃ jñānamucyate || 146 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘itaḥ pratyādeśātsvajanamanugantuṃ vyavasitā sthitā tiṣṭhetyuccairvadati guruśiṣye gurusame | punardṛṣṭiṃ *bāṣpaprasarakaluṣāmarpitavatī mayi krūre yattatsaviṣamiva śalyaṃ dahati mām || 32 ||’

atra saviśeṣā smṛtiricchayā vāgārambheṇa cānubadhyate | *niṣpattyādayaḥ punarasyā ratyādiniṣpattiṣveva draṣṭavyāḥ | *ratyādayo 'smṛtimūlatvāttatprakarṣāpakarṣāvanuvartante ||

ūho vitarka ityuktaḥ padārtheṣu yathāmati |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘citte niveśya parikalpitasattvayogā*- n‍rūpoccayena *ghaṭitā manasā kṛtā nu | strīratnasṛṣṭiraparā pratibhāti sā me dhāturvibhutvamanucintya vapuśca tasyāḥ || 33 ||’

so 'yamasatyaḥ satyo vā smṛtijñānacintanādidvāreṇa nirṇayānto niṣpanna ityucyate ||

utkaṇṭheṣṭānavāptau yo 'bhilāṣaḥ syāttadāptaye || 147 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattihrāsau yathā—

‘yāsyatyadya śakuntaleti hṛdayaṃ saṃspṛṣṭamutkaṇṭha‍yā *kaṇṭhaḥ stambhitabāṣpavṛttikaluṣaścintājaḍaṃ darśanam | ﻿[page 584] vaiklavyaṃ mama tāvadīdṛśamidaṃ snehādaraṇyaukasaḥ pīḍyante gṛhiṇaḥ kathaṃ nu* tanayāviśleṣaduḥkhairnavaiḥ || 34 ||’

atra vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyogāt prītirivotkaṇṭhāpi tadanuṣaṅgiṇī niṣpannā uttarārdhapratipādyena *niṣedhenaiva vismayādinābhibhūyamānā hrāsa ityucyate | prakarṣaścāsyā mamāraṇyaukasa ityanena nivāryate ||

prayatnapūrvikārtheṣu smṛtiścinteti *cocyate || 148 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘cintāṇiadaïasamāgamammi kaamaṇṇuāiṃ* mariūṇa | suṇṇaṃ kalahāantī *sahīhiṁ ruṇṇā ṇa* o hasiā || 35 ||’
[cintānītadayitasamāgame kṛtamanyukāni smṛtvā | śūnyaṃ kalahāyamānā sakhībhī ruditā na vā hasitā ||]

atra sakhīrodanena śūnyakalahaḥ, śūnyakalahena sākṣātkāraḥ, sākṣātkāreṇa cintā, cintayā tu mūlabhūtā ratiḥ prakṛṣyate ||

ātmaprakāśanaparā ceṣṭā capalatocyate || 149 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘kaścitkarābhyāmupagūḍhanālamālolapattrābhihatadvirepham | rajobhirantaḥpariveṣabandhi līlāravindaṃ bhramayāṃcakāra || 36 ||’

*atra kaścillīlāravindabhramaṇaceṣṭayā *indumatyai tiṣṭhate ||

śāstroktārthānusaṃdhānādarthanirdhāraṇaṃ matiḥ |
﻿[page 585]

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘asaṃśayaṃ kṣattraparigrahakṣamā yadāryamasyāmabhilāṣi me manaḥ | satāṃ hi saṃdehapadeṣu vastuṣu pramāṇamantaḥkaraṇapravṛttayaḥ || 37 ||’

atra pūrvārdhoktārthanirdhāraṇarūpā matiruttarārdhenānubadhyate ||

garvo 'nyeṣāma*vajñānamātmasaṃbhāvanādibhiḥ || 150 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya puṣṭiryathā—

‘dhṛtāyudho yāvadahaṃ tāvadanyaiḥ kimāyudhaiḥ | yadvā na siddhamastreṇa mama tatkena setsyati || 38 ||’

atra karṇasyātmasaṃbhāvanayāśvatthā* manyavajñā prakṛṣyate ||

aheturanivartī* ca snehaścittārdratā matā |

tadrūpeṇa *rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘anena kasyāpi kulāṅa‍kureṇa spṛṣṭasya gātreṣu sukhaṃ mamaitat | kāṃ nirvṛtiṃ cetasi tasya kuryā- dyasyāyama*ṅa‍gātkṛtinaḥ prarūḍhaḥ || 39 ||’

atra duṣyantasya *sattvadamanadarśanādutpannastadaṅa‍gasparśasukhādibhiruddīpitaḥ spṛhāmativitarkavāgārambhaiḥ saṃsṛjyamānaḥ sneho niṣpadyate ||

abhīṣṭārthasya saṃprāptau spṛhāparyāptatā dhṛtiḥ |
﻿[page 586]

tadrūpeṇa *rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘nīto vikramabāhurātmasamatāṃ prāpteyamurvītale sāraṃ sāgarikā samāgaramahīprāptyekahetuḥ priyā | devī prītimupāgatā ca bhaginīlābhājjitāḥ *kosalāḥ kiṃ nāsti tvayi satyamātyavṛṣabhe *yasminkaromi spṛhām || 40 ||’

atra vatsarājasya sarvātmanā manorathasiddhayo dhṛteḥ prakarṣamāvahanti ||

cetonimīlanaṃ vrīḍā*nyaṅa‍garāgastavādibhiḥ || 151 ||

tadrūpeṇa *rasasya prakarṣe krodha*śokābhyāṃ saṃkaro yathā—

‘akṣudrārikṛtābhimanyunidha*naprodbhūtatīvrakrudhaḥ pārthasyākṛtaśātravapratikṛterantaḥśucā muhyataḥ | kīrṇā bāṣpakaṇaiḥ patanti dhanuṣi vrīḍājaḍā dṛṣṭayo hā vatseti giraḥ sphuranti na punarniryānti kaṇṭhādbahiḥ || 41 ||’

atrārjunasyānyāyenābhimanyuvadhādudbhūtau dīptāveva krodhaśokā*vudbhūtavipratīkārotthayā tathāvidhayaiva vrīḍayā saṃkīryete | tathāhi krodhaśokayoranubhāvabhūtā dṛṣṭayo vācaśca vrīḍājaḍā* iti viśeṣaṇāni saṃbadhyante ||

avahitthaṃ tu lajjāderharṣādyākāragopanam || 152 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘evaṃvādini devarṣau pārśve pituradhomukhī | līlākamalapattrāṇi gaṇayāmāsa pārvatī || 42 ||’
﻿[page 587]

atra—

‘praṇamya śitikaṇṭhāya vibudhāstadanantaram | caraṇau rañjayantvasyāścūḍāmaṇimarīcibhiḥ || 43 ||’

*ityāderdevarṣivākyādudbhūtaḥ* praharṣākāro gurusaṃnidhau lajjitayā līlākamalapatragaṇanavyājena* gauryā gopyate ||

sukhaduḥkhādijanito mohaścittasya mūḍhatā |

tadrūpeṇa *rasaniṣpattiryathā—

‘kānte talpamupāgate vigalitā nīvī svayaṃ bandhanā- dvāso viślathamekhalāguṇadhṛtaṃ kiṃcinnitambe sthitam | etāvatsakhi vedmi kevalamahaṃ tasyāṅa‍gasaṅa‍ge punaḥ *ko 'yaṃ kā vayamatra kiṃ nu surataṃ svalpāpi me na smṛtiḥ 44’

atra sthāyinī ratirmohaniṣpattyā prakṛṣyate ||

saṃmohānandasaṃbhedo madirādikṛto madaḥ || 153 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘ghūrṇamānanayanaṃ skhalatkathaṃ khedabindumadakāraṇasmitam | ānanena na tu tāvadīśvaraścakṣuṣā ciramumāmukhaṃ papau || 45 ||’

atra nayanaghūrṇanākāraṇasmitādayaḥ saṃmohānandasaṃbhedā*dudbhavanto madaṃ niṣpādayanti |

manaḥprasādo harṣaḥ syādiṣṭāvāptistavādibhiḥ |
﻿[page 588]

tadrūpeṇa *rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘jātasya te piturapīndrajito nihantu- rvatsasya vatsa kati nāma dinānyamūni | tasyāpyapatyamadhitiṣṭhati *vīradharme diṣṭyā gataṃ daśarathasya kulaṃ pratiṣṭhām || 46 ||’

atra *daśarathasuhṛdaḥ sumanttrasāratheḥ *prabhukulasya pratiṣṭhāmāśaṃsatastatsūnumindrajito hantāraṃ paśyato manorathāvāptyā harṣo niṣpannastadapatye 'pi vīradharmamācariṣṇau prakṛṣṭo diṣṭyetyavyayena sūcyate ||

krodhaḥ *kṛtāparādheṣu sthiro 'marṣatvamaśnute || 154 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘lākṣāgṛhānalaviṣānnasabhāpraveśaiḥ prāṇeṣu vittanicayeṣu ca naḥ *prahṛtya | ākṛṣṭapāṇḍavavadhūparidhānakeśāḥ svasthā bhavanti mayi jīvati dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ || 47 ||’

atra *bhīmasenasya dhārtarāṣṭreṣu svasthā iti nāmno 'pya*sahanāt lākṣāgṛhādyapakārajanmāmarṣaḥ *pratīyate ||

asūyānyaguṇarddhīnāmauddhatyādasahiṣṇutā |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘vandyāste na vicāraṇīyacaritāstiṣṭhantu huṃ vartate sundastrīnidhane 'pyakhaṇḍayaśaso loke mahānto hi te | ﻿[page 589] yāni trīṇi *kutomukhānyapi padānyāsankharāyodhane yadvā kauśalamindrasūnudamane* tatrāpyabhijño janaḥ || 48 ||’

atra yadyapi solluṇṭhadoṣakīrtanādibhirjugupsā niṣyadyate tathāpi na tayā svaniṣpattiheturasūyā saṃkīryate ||

īrṣāmāhuḥ samāneṣu mānadānādyamarṣaṇam* || 155 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘huṃ* ṇillajja samosara taṃ ccia* aṇuṇesu jāi de eaṃ | *pāaggaṃguṭṭhālattaeṇa tilaaṃ viṇimmaviaṃ || 49 ||’
[huṃ nirlajja samapasara tāmevānunaya yasyāsta etat | pādāgrāṅa‍guṣṭhālaktakena tilakaṃ vinirmitam ||]

atra kasyāścit preyasi sapatnīṃ prasādayituṃ gate tanmānamamṛṣyamāṇāyāḥ samutpannerṣyā priyānunayādibhirbhṛśāyamānatayā niṣpannālaktakatilakānumeyaistatpādapatanādibhiruddīptā huṃkārākṣepabhartsanapratibhedāvinābhūtairbhrūbhaṅa‍gatāḍanāṅa‍gakṣepavepathusvedagadgadādibhiḥ saṃsṛjyamānā prakṛṣyate ||

viṣādaścetaso glānirupāyābhāvanāśayoḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘vyarthaṃ yatra kapīndrasakhyamapi me kleśaḥ* kapīnāṃ vṛthā prajñāṃ jāmbavato 'pi yatra na gatiḥ putrasya vāyorapi | mārgaṃ yatra na viśvakarmatanayaḥ kartuṃ nalo 'pi kṣamaḥ saumitrerapi pattriṇāmaviṣayastatra priyā kvāpi me || 50 ||’
﻿[page 590]

atra sītāsamāgamaviṣaye rāmasya dṛṣṭāvadānasugrīvasakhyāderupāyasyābhāvādviṣādaḥ prakṛṣyate ||

sattvatyāgādanutkarṣo vākyāderdainyamucyate || 156 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘asmānsādhu vicintya saṃyamadhanānuccaiḥ kulaṃ cātmana- stvayyasyāḥ kathamapyabāndhavakṛtāṃ bhāvapravṛttiṃ ca tām | sāmānyapratipattipūrvakamiyaṃ dāreṣu dṛśyā tvayā bhāgyādhīnamataḥ paraṃ na khalu tadvācyaṃ vadhūbandhubhiḥ || 51 ||’

atra snehaprabhavaṃ pādatrayoktamarthitādainyaṃ turīṃyapādopakṣiptayācñādainyāntareṇānubadhyate ||

vidurvāgdaṇḍapāruṣyamugratāmapakāriṣu |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘praṇayisakhīsalīlaparihāsarasādhigatai- rlalitaśirīṣapuṣpahananairapi tāmyati yat | vapuṣi vadhāya tatra tava śastramupakṣipataḥ patatu śirasyakāṇḍayamadaṇḍa ivaiṣa bhujaḥ || 52 ||’

atra mādhavasya prakṛṣṭāpakāriṇyaghoraghaṇṭe viṣaye prakṛṣṭameva vākpāruṣyaṃ daṇḍapāruṣyaṃ ca jāyate ||

trāsaścittacamatkāra ākasmikabhayādibhiḥ || 157 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘parisphuranmīnavighaṭṭito ravaḥ surāṅa‍ganāsrāsaviloladṛṣṭayaḥ | upāyayuḥ kampitapāṇipallavāḥ sakhījanasyāpi vilokanīyatām 53’
﻿[page 591]

atra loladṛṣṭitā karābadhūnanaṃ ca strīṇāṃ svabhāvabhīrutvavilāsitvābhyāmapi bhavatīti trāsāvirbhāve 'pyasamarthamiti nānubangho bhavati ||

aniṣṭābhyāgamotprekṣāṃ śaṅa‍kāmācakṣate budhāḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya prakarṣo yathā—

‘sahasā mā sāhijjaü piāgamo tīa virahakisiāe | accaṃtapahariseṇa vi jā a muā sā muā ccea || 54 ||’
[sahasā mā sādhyatāṃ priyāgamastayā virahakṛśayā | atyantapraharṣeṇāpi yā ca mṛtā sā mṛtaiva ||]

atra virahiṇyāḥ kārśyātiśayamudvīkṣamāṇāyāḥ kasyāścidvayasyāyāḥ snehātiśayāt 'prema paśyati bhayānyapade 'pī'ti priyāgamapraharṣātiśayabhāve 'pyasahiṣṇutayā tanmaraṇaśaṅa‍kā prakṛṣyate ||

virahādermanastāpaḥ *śarīrātaṅa‍kado gadaḥ || 158 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘sthitamurasi viśālaṃ padminīpattrametat kathayati na tathāntarmanmathotthāmavasthām | atiśayaparitāpaglāpitābhyāṃ yathāsyāḥ stanayugapariṇāhaṃ maṇḍalābhyāṃ bravīti || 55 ||’

atra sāgarikāyāḥ stananihitasarojinīdalaglāpanena vapuḥsaṃtāpo niṣpadyate ||

balasyāpacayo glānirādhivyādhiprakarṣabhūḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘kisalayamiva mugdhaṃ *banghanādvipralūnaṃ hṛdayakusumaśoṣī dāruṇo dīrghaśokaḥ | ﻿[page 592] glapayati paripāṇḍukṣāmamasyāḥ śarīraṃ śaradija iva gharmaḥ ketakīgarbhapattram || 56 ||’

atra prakṛṣṭaśokānubandhinī glānirvaivarṇyakṣāmatābhyāmanubadhyate ||

utkaṇṭhāharṣaśokāderunmādaścittaviplavaḥ || 159 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya janma yathā—

‘*kvākāryaṃ kva kalādharasya ca kulaṃ bhūyo 'pi dṛśyeta sā doṣāṇāmupaśāntaye śrutamaho kope 'pi śāntaṃ mukham | kiṃ vakṣyantyapakalmaṣāḥ kṛtadhiyo rekhaiva* sānyādṛśī cetaḥ svāsthyamupaihi kaḥ khalu yuvā dhanyo 'dharaṃ dhāsyati 57’

atra virahiṇaḥ purūravasa utkaṇṭhādibhiḥ premaprakarṣādasatpralāparūpa unmādo niṣpadyate ||

ādarātiśayāccetasyāvegaḥ saṃbhramo mataḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya saṃkaro yathā—

‘alamalamatimātraṃ sāhasenāmunā te tvaritamapi vimuñca tvaṃ latāpāśamenam | calitamiva niroddhuṃ jīvitaṃ jīviteśe kṣaṇamiha mama kaṇṭhe bāhupāśaṃ nidhehi || 58 ||’

atra ratijanmā saṃbhramātiśayo ratijanmanaiva matiprakarṣeṇa saṃkīryate ||

manaḥśarīrayoḥ khedaḥ kriyātiśayataḥ śramaḥ || 160 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya saṃkaro yathā—

‘skhalayati vacanaṃ te saṃśrayatyaṅa‍gamaṅa‍gaṃ janayati mukhacandrodbhāsinaḥ khedabindūn | ﻿[page 593] mukulayati ca netre sarvathā subhru khedastvayi vilasati tulyaṃ *vallabhālokanena || 59 ||’

atra mālatyāḥ puṣpāvacayajanmā śramaḥ, mādhavāvalokanajā ca ratiḥ, svedagadgadāṅa‍gasādanayanamukulaistulyadharmiṇau mithaḥ saṃkīryete ||

cittasya khedo nirvedastattvajñānodayādibhiḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya śeṣo yathā—

‘jarāmaraṇadaurgatyavyādhayastāvadāsatām | manye janmaiva dhīrāṇāṃ bhūyobhūyasttrapākaram || 60 ||’

atra mokṣāyotsahamānasya kasyacinnirvedāvadamo gamyate ||

kriyāsvapāṭavaṃ jāḍyaṃ cintotkaṇṭhābhayādibhiḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasya* niṣpattiryathā—

‘śithilaśithilaṃ nyasya svairaṃ dhanuḥśikhare śiro nayanasalilaiḥ kurvanmaurvīlatāmaparāmiva | ahaha vikalaḥ śrutvā śrutvā ghanastanitadhvaniṃ kimapi kimapi dhyāyannāryo na yāti na tiṣṭhati || 61 ||’

atra virahiṇo rāmasya kriyāsvapāṭavaṃ niṣpādyate ||

kriyāvidveṣa ālasyaṃ sukhasaṃvinmadādibhiḥ || 161 ||

tadrūpeṇa rasasya niṣpattiryathā—

‘ghariṇighaṇatthaṇa*pellaṇasuhelli*paḍiassa honta*pahiassa | *avasaüṇaṅa‍gāraavāraviṭṭhidiahā* suhāventi || 62 ||’
[gṛhiṇīghanastanapreraṇasukhakelipatitasya bhaviṣyatpathikasya | apaśakunāṅa‍gārakavāraviṣṭidivasāḥ sukhayanti ||]
﻿[page 594]

atra ratisukhānubhavājjigamiṣorapyagacchata ālasyaṃ niṣpadyate ||

nidrā vyāpāravaimukhyamindriyāṇāṃ śramādibhiḥ |

tadrūpeṇa *rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘ṇiddālasapari*ghummirataṃsavalantaddha*tāraāloā | kāmassa vi duvvisahā diṭṭhiṇivāā sasimuhīe || 63 ||’
[nidrāla*saparighūrṇanaśīlatiryagvaladardhatārakālokāḥ | kāmasyāpi durviṣahā dṛṣṭinipātāḥ śaśimukhyāḥ ||]

atra ratiśramajāgarādijanitanidrālasā* dṛṣṭinipātāstā*rakāghūrṇanatryasravalanādibhiranubadhyante ||

nidrādijanitaṃ suptamindriyādinimīlanam || 162 ||

tadrūpeṇa *rasaprakarṣo yathā—

‘osuaï diṇṇa*paḍivakkhaveaṇaṃ pasịdhilehiṁ aṅa‍gehiṁ | ṇivvattiasuraarasāṇubaṃdhasuhaṇibbharaṃ* soṇhā || 64 ||’
[avasvapiti dattapratipakṣavedanaṃ praśithilairaṅa‍gaiḥ | nirvartitasuratarasānubandhasukhanirbharaṃ snuṣā ||]

atra nirbharapadenaiva prakarṣaḥ pratipādyate ||

nidrāpagamahetubhyaḥ prabodhaścetanāgamaḥ |

tadrūpeṇa rasasyānubandho yathā—

‘pratyagronmeṣajihmā kṣaṇamanabhimukhī ratnadīṃpaprabhāṇāmātmavyāpāragurvī janitajalalavājṛmbhaṇaiḥ sāṅa‍gabhaṅa‍gaiḥ | ﻿[page 595] *nāgāṅa‍kaṃ moktumicchoḥ śayanamuruphaṇācakravālopadhānaṃ nidrācchedābhitāmrā* ciramavatu harerdṛṣṭirākekarā vaḥ || 65 ||’

atra dṛṣṭeḥ pratyagronmeṣajihmatādibhiḥ prabodho nādyāpi niṣpadyata iti pratīyate ||

uktā bhāvādibhedena te 'mī ratyādayo rasāḥ | athaiteṣveva keṣāṃcidviśeṣānabhidadhmahe || 163 ||

tatra

śṛṅa‍gāravīrakaruṇaraudrādbhutabhayānakāḥ | bībhatsahāsyapreyāṃsaḥ śāntadāntoddhatā rasāḥ || 164 ||
ratirnisargasaṃsargaupamyādhyātmābhiyogajā | saṃprayogābhimānotthā viṣayotthā ca kathyate || 165 ||
prītirapyevameva syānna tvasyāṃ sāṃprayogikī | *ābhyāsikī tu tatsthāne tadudāhṛtayo yathā || 166 ||
‘mṛteti pretya saṃgantuṃ yayā me maraṇaṃ matam | saivāvantī mayā labghā kathamatraiva janmani || 66 ||’

atra sthāyino vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyogādrasaniṣpattiriti ratireva śṛṅa‍gārarūpeṇa niṣpadyate | atrāvantyā vāsavadattāyā ālambanavibhāvabhūtāyāḥ sakāśādutpanno vatseśvarasya ratisthāyibhāvaḥ, tasyāḥ punarjīvanādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamāno mṛtetyādinā vāgārambhānubhāvenānumīyamānairharṣadhṛtiprabhṛtibhiḥ sukhātmakairvyabhicāribhiḥ saṃsṛjyamānaḥ karuṇānantaraḥ saṃbhogaḥ śṛṅa‍gārākhyāṃ labhate ||

﻿[page 596]
‘ajitvā sārṇavāmurvīmaniṣṭa‍vā vividhairmakhaiḥ | adattvā cārthamarthibhyo bhaveyaṃ pārthivaḥ katham || 67 ||’

atra vasudhāvijayāderālambanavibhāvādutpannaḥ sthāyyutsāhabhāvaḥ sthairyadhairyādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaiḥ samutpanneṣu vāgārambhānumīyamāneṣu smṛtimativitarkādiṣu niṣpanno vīrarasasaṃjñayā vyavahriyate ||

‘yasyāḥ kusumaśayyāpi komalāṅa‍gyā rujākarī | sādhiśete kathaṃ devī hutāśanavatīṃ citām || 68 ||’

atra cālambanavibhāvabhūtadevīmaraṇādutpannaḥ śokaḥ sthāyibhāvaścitāniveśanahutāśanāṅa‍gajvālādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamāno vāgārambhānumeyairnirvedaglānivaivarṇyādibhirvyabhicāribhiḥ saṃsṛjyamānaḥ karuṇa iti jñāyate ||

‘nigṛhya keśeṣvākṛṣṭā kṛṣṇā yena mamāgrataḥ | so 'yaṃ duḥśāsanaḥ pāpo lavdhaḥ kiṃ jīvati kṣaṇam || 69 ||’

atra duḥśāsanālambanavibhāvāya krudhyato bhīmasenasya pūrvamutpannaḥ krodhaḥ sthāyibhāvastadavāpteḥ smaryamāṇasamakṣakṛtadraupadīnigrahakeśakarṣaṇādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ samutpanneṣu vāgārambhānumīyamāneṣvasūyāvegavepathuśramādiṣu duḥkhātmakeṣu vyabhicāriṣu *nippadyamāno raudra iti niṣpadyate ||

‘aṃśukāni pravālāni puṣpaṃ hārādibhūṣaṇam | phalaṃ madhūni harmyāṇi śākhā nandanaśākhinām || 70 ||’

atra śākhināṃ pravālapuṣpaphalaśākhāsaṃpannaṃ nijaṃ rūpaṃ nandanaśākhināṃ punaḥ pravālādisthāne*ṣvaṃśukahāramadhumandirāṇi tadetadāścaryam | ataścaitebhya ālambanavibhāvebhyaḥ kasyaciddevabhūyaṃgatasya samutpanno vismayaḥ*﻿[page 597] sthāyibhāvastadīyāvayavadarśanādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ samutpanneṣu vāgārambhānumeyeṣu harṣaromodgamakhedagadgadādiṣu vyabhicāriṣu niṣpadyamāno 'dbhuta ityucyate ||

‘idaṃ maghonaḥ kuliśaṃ dhārāsaṃnihitānalam | smaraṇaṃ yasya daityastrīgarbhapātāya kalpate || 71 ||’

atra mahendrakuliśāddhārāsaṃnihitānalādālamba*navibhāvātsmaryamāṇādapi daityastrīṇāmutpanno *bhayasthāyibhāvastadvidīrṇadānavamaraṇasmaraṇādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ *svagarbhapātādibhiranubhāvādibhistadanumitaiśca svedastambhavepathuprabhṛtibhirvyabhicāribhiḥ saṃsṛjyamāno bhayānakarasarūpeṇa niṣpannaḥ kenacidākhyāyamāno 'pi bhayānaka ityākhyāyate ||

‘pāyaṃ pāyaṃ tavārīṇāṃ śoṇitaṃ *pāṇisaṃpuṭaiḥ | kauṇapāḥ saha nṛtyanti kabandhairanttrabhūṣaṇāḥ || 72 ||’

atrālambanavibhāvabhūtebhyaḥ kauṇapebhyaḥ kasyaci*dripujayaśaṃsinaḥ puṃsa utpanno jugupsāsthāyibhāvaḥ śiraśchedavigaladrudhiraghārāparipluta*praṇartitakabandhakauṇapānttrabhūṣaṇaśoṇitapānādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ samutpanneṣu *vāgārambhānumeyeṣu bhayāveśaśaṅa‍kāvahitthādiṣu vyabhicāriṣu niṣpanno bībhatsa iti nigadyate ||

‘idamamlānamānāyā lagnaṃ stanataṭe tava | chādyatāmuttarīyeṇa navaṃ nakhapadaṃ sakhi || 73 ||’
﻿[page 598]

atra kācit sakhīṃ pūrvaṃ bhartari *gṛhītamānāṃ tenaiva nakha*padāṅkitastanīmālambanavibhāvabhūtāmupalabhamānāyāḥ kasyāścitsakhyā utpanno hāsaḥ sthāyibhāvastadīyamānaparigrahasmaraṇādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ samutpanneṣu vāgārambhānumiteṣu śaṅa‍kāvahitthagadgadādivyabhicāriṣu *niṣpadyamāno hāsyaśabdenābhidhīyate ||

‘yadeva rocate mahyaṃ tadeva kurute priyā | iti vetti na *jānāti *tatpriyaṃ yatkaroti sā || 74 ||’

atra vatsalaprakṛterdhīratayā lalitanāyakasya *priyālambanavibhāvādutpannaḥ *snehasthāyibhāvo viṣayasaukumāryātmaprakṛtyādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ samupajāyamānairmoha*dhṛtismṛtyādibhirvyabhicāribhāvairanubhāvaiśca* saṃsṛjyamāno niṣpannaḥ preyāniti pratīyate ||

ratiprītyorapi cāyameva mūlaprakṛtiriṣyate | yaditthamāhuḥ—

‘ahetuḥ pakṣapāto yastasya nāsti pratikriyā | sa hi snehātmakastanturantarmarmāṇi sīvyati || 75 ||
sarvāḥ saṃpattayastasya saṃtuṣṭaṃ yasya mānasam | upānadgṛḍhapādasya nanu *carmāstṛtaiva bhūḥ || 76 ||’

atra kasyacidupaśāntaprakṛterdhīraśā*ntanāyakasya yathopanatamanonukūladārādisaṃpatterālambanavibhāvabhūtāyāḥ samutpanno dhṛtisthāyibhāvo vastutattvālocanādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ samupajāyamāna*smṛtyādibhirvyabhi-﻿[page 599]cāribhāvairvāgārambhādibhiranuṣajyamāno niṣpannaḥ śānta ityabhigīyate* ||

anye punarasya śamaṃ prakṛtimāmananti sa tu dhṛtereva viśeṣo bhavati ||

‘sādhāraṇyānnirātaṅa‍kaḥ kanyāmanyo 'pi yācate | kiṃ punarjagatāṃ jetā prapautraḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ || 77 ||’

atra rāmasyodāttaprakṛternisargata eva tattvābhiniveśinī matirnākṛtyaviṣaye pravartate, na ca pravṛttopāramati, sā ca sīteyaṃ mama svīkārayogyetyevaṃrūpeṇa *pravṛttā rāvaṇaprārthanālakṣmaṇaprotsāhanābhyāmuddīpyamānā samupajāyamānacintāvitarkavrīḍāvahitthasmṛtyādibhiḥ kālocitottarānumīyamānaiśca vivekacāturyaudāryadhairyādibhiḥ *saṃsṛjyamānodāttarasarūpeṇa niṣpadyate ||

‘apakartāhamasmīti mā te manasi bhūdbhayam | vimukheṣu na me khaṅa‍gaḥ prahartuṃ jātu vāñchati || 78 ||’

atra mayāsyāpakāraḥ kṛta iti *yaccetasi bhayaṃ tanmābhūt ‘*parāṅyukheṣu me khaṅa‍gaḥ kadācidapi na prahartumutsahate’ iti sarvadaiva rụ̄dho 'haṃkāraḥ pratīyate | so 'yaṃ garvaprakṛtiruddhato nāma rasaḥ | kecit punaḥ—

‘āsthāmālambya nīteṣu vaśaṃ kṣudreṣvarātiṣu | vyaktimāyāti mahatāṃ māhātmyamanukampayā || 79 ||’

ityevamūrjakhītyudāttapakṣe nikṣipantaḥ pūrvoktameva garvaprakarṣodāharaṇaṃ dhṛtāyudho yāvadahamityādyuddhataniṣpattau varṇayanti ||

rativiśeṣeṣu naisargikī yathā—

‘iyaṃ mahendraprabhṛtīnadhiśriyaścaturdigīśānavamanya* māninī | arūpahāryaṃ madanasya nigrahātpinākapāṇiṃ patimāptumicchati || 80 ||’
﻿[page 600]

atra janmāntaravāsanayā nisargata iyaṃ bhavati ||

sāṃsargikī yathā—

‘bhittvā sadyaḥ kisalayapuṭān devadārudrumāṇāṃ ye tatkṣīrasrutisurabhayo dakṣiṇena pravṛttāḥ | āliṅgyante guṇavati mayā te tuṣārādrivātāḥ pūrvaspṛṣṭaṃ* yadi kila bhavedaṅa‍gamebhistaveti || 81 ||’

atra śaityasaurabhādibhirvirahija*nodvejanīyā api vāyavaḥ priyatamāṅa‍gasaṃsargasaṃbhāvanayā *samāśliṣyanta iti saṃsargata iyaṃ bhavati ||

aupamānikī yathā—

‘api janakasutāyāstacca taccānurūpaṃ sphuṭamiha śiśuyugme naipuṇonneyamasti | nanu punariva tanme gocarībhūtamakṣṇo- rabhinavaśatapattraśrīmadāsyaṃ* priyāyāḥ || 82 ||’

seyaṃ sītāviṣayiṇī ratistadupamānadarśanena rāmaṃ *ramayati ||

ādhyātmikī yathā—

‘kāmaṃ* pratyādiṣṭāṃ smarāmi na parigrahaṃ munestanayām | balavattu dūyamānaṃ pratyāyayatīva me cetaḥ || 83 ||’

atra seyaṃ durvāsasaḥ śāpādvismṛtavivāhādivṛttāntasya duṣyantasya śakuntalāyāṃ ratiradhyātmaṃ bhavati ||

[page 601]

ābhiyogikī yathā—

‘alasavalitamugdhasnigghaniṣpandamandairadhikavikasadantarvismayasmeratārai; | hṛdayamaśaraṇaṃ* me pakṣmalākṣyāḥ kāṭākṣairapahṛtamapaviddhaṃ pītamunmūlitaṃ ca || 84 ||’

seyamanurāgātiśayasūcakamālatīkaṭākṣābhiyoge mādhavasya *ratiratīvotpadyate ||

sāṃprayogikī yathā—

‘unnamayya sakacagrahamāsyaṃ cumbati priyatame haṭhavṛttyā | huṃhuṁ muñca mamameti ca mandaṃ jalpitaṃ jayati mānadhanāyāḥ || 85 ||’

atra tarjanārtha—mokṣārtha—vāraṇārthānāṃ mandaṃ mandaṃ prayogānmānavatyāḥ saṃprayoge ratyutpattiḥ pratīyate ||

ābhimānikī yathā—

‘iyaṃ gehe lakṣmīriyamamṛtavartirnayanayo- rasāvasyāḥ sparśo vapuṣi *bahalaścandanarasaḥ | ayaṃ bāhuḥ kaṇṭhe śiśiramasṛṇo* mauktikasaraḥ kimasyā na preyo yadi paramasahyastu virahaḥ || 86 ||’

atra ruciviśeṣo 'bhimānastata evaṃprāyā ratayo bhavanti ||

[page 602]

*vaiṣayikīṣu śabde yathā—

‘vilāsamasṛṇollasanmusalaloladoṣkandalīparasparapariskhaladvalayaniḥkhanodbandhurāḥ | lasanti kalahuṃkṛtiprasabha*kampitoraḥsthala*truṭadgamakasaṃkulāḥ *kalamakaṇḍanīgītayaḥ || 87 ||’

sparśe yathā—

‘badhnannaṅa‍geṣu romāñcaṃ kurvanmanasi nirvṛtim | netre nimīlayanneṣa priyāsparśaḥ pravartate || 88 ||’

rūpe yathā—

‘tā rāghavaṃ dṛṣṭibhirāpibantyo nāryo na jagmurviṣayāntarāṇi | tathā hi śeṣendriyavṛttirāsāṃ sarvātmanā cakṣuriva praṃviṣṭā 89’

rase yathā—

‘kasya no kurute *mugdhe pipāsākulitaṃ manaḥ | ayaṃ te vidrumacchāyo marumārga ivādharaḥ || 90 ||’

*gandhe yathā—

‘randhaṇakammaṇiuṇie mā jūrasu* rattapāḍalasuandham | muhamāruaṃ pianto dhūmāi sihī ṇa pajjalaï || 91 ||’
[randhanakarmanipuṇike mā *kradhyasva raktapāṭalasugandham | mukhamārutaṃ piban dhūmāyate śikhī na prajvalati ||]
[page 603]

prītiviśeṣeṣu naisargikī yathā—

‘ālakṣya dantamukulāna*nimittahāsā- navyaktavarṇaramaṇīyavacaḥphrvṛttīn | aṅa‍kāśrayapraṇayinastanayānvahanto dhanyāstadaṅa‍garajasā *malinībhavanti || 92 ||’

*atra yadā yadā ratirjāyate tadā tadā putreṣu snihyati putrarūpeṇa vā jāyata iti janmāntaravāsanārūpo nisargaḥ saṃgacchate ||

sāṃsargikī yathā—

‘viśvaṃbharā bhagavatī bhavatīmasūta rājā prajāpatisamo janakaḥ pitā te | teṣāṃ vadhūstvamasi nandini pārthivānāṃ yeṣāṃ *kule ca savitā ca gururvayaṃ ca || 93 ||’

atra viśvaṃbharādisaṃsargāt sītāyāṃ vasiṣṭhamiśrāḥ snihyanti |

aupamānikī yathā—

‘kuvalayadalasnigdhaśyāmaḥ śikhaṇḍakamaṇḍano baṭupariṣadaṃ puṇyaśrīkaḥ śriyaiva sabhājayan | punariva śiśurbhūtvā vatsaḥ sa me raghunandano jhaṭiti kurute dṛṣṭaḥ ko 'yaṃ dṛśoramṛtāñjanam || 94 ||’

atra rāmaupamyāllave janakaḥ prīyate ||

ādhyātmikī yathā—

‘paritastaṃ pṛthāsūnuḥ snehena paritastare | avijñāte 'pi bandhau hi balātprahlādate* manaḥ || 95 ||’
[page 604]

atrāvijñāto 'pi vāsavaḥ svasūnumarjunaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ prīṇayati ||

ābhiyogikī yathā—

‘*ajñātabandhurayamṛkṣaharīśvaro me paulastya eṣa samareṣu puraḥ prahartā | ityādṛtena kathitau raghunandanena *vyutkrāntalakṣmaṇamubhau bharato vavande || 96 ||’

atra sītānveṣaṇāderabhiyogādrāmasya sugrīvabibhīṣaṇayoḥ prītirudayate* | sāṃprayogikīsthāne ābhyāsikī yathā—

‘iti vismṛtānyakaraṇīyamātmanaḥ sacivāvalambitadhuraṃ narādhipam | parivṛddharāgamanubaddhasevayā mṛgayā jahāra catureva kāminī || 97 ||’

atra

‘śabdādibhyo bahirbhūtā yā karmābhyāsalakṣaṇā | prītiḥ sābhyāsikī jñeyā mṛgayādiṣu karmasu ||’

iti lakṣaṇaṃ ghaṭate ||

ābhimānikī yathā—

‘dattendrābhayadakṣiṇairbhagavato vaivasvatādāmano- rdṛptānāṃ dahanāya dīpitanijakṣāttrapratāpāgnibhiḥ | ādityairyadi vigraho nṛpatibhirdhanyaṃ mamaitattato dīptāstrasphuradugra*dīdhitiśikhānīrājitajyaṃ dhanuḥ || 98 ||’
[page 605]

atrābhimatapratidvandvilābhāllavānupadī kuśastuṣyati ||

*vaiṣayikīṣu śabde yathā—

‘lāvaṇyaiḥ kṣaṇadāvirāmamadhurāḥ kiṃcidvinidrālasa*śrotraiḥ savraṇamugdhacāraṇavadhūdantacchadāvāsinaḥ | pīyante mṛdutrakrapītamarutaḥ paurāṇarītikrama*vyālolāṅa‍guliruddhaśukta*suṣiraśreṇīravā* veṇavaḥ || 99 ||’

sparśe yathā—

‘praśāntagharmābhibhavaḥ śanairvivānvilāsinībhyaḥ parimṛṣṭapaṅa‍kajaḥ | dadau bhujālambamivāttaśīkarastaraṅa‍gamālāntaragocaro 'nilaḥ || 100 ||’

rupe yathā—

‘ayamabhinavameghaśyāmalottuṅa‍gasānu- rmadamukharamayūrīmu*ktasaṃsaktakekaḥ | śakuniśabalanīḍānokahasnigdhavarṣmā vitarati bṛhadaśmā parvataḥ prītimakṣṇoḥ || 101 ||’

rase yathā—

‘ikṣudaṇḍasya maṇḍasya dadhnaḥ piṣṭakṛtasya* ca | *varāhasya ca māṃsasya so 'yaṃ gacchati phālgunaḥ || 102 ||’

gandhe yathā—

‘kapolakaṇḍūḥ karibhirvinetuṃ vighaṭṭitānāṃ saraladrumāṇām | yatra *srutakṣīratayā prasūtaḥ sānūni ganghaḥ surabhīkaroti || 103’

upalakṣaṇaṃ caitat | tenotsāhasya yuddhadānadayāvīrādayaḥ, krodhasya [page 606]*bhāmamanyūtprāsādayaḥ, hāsasya smitahasitavihasitādayaḥ, *suptapralayamatyādīnāṃ tu* svapnamaraṇaśamādayo bhedā jāyante | tatra yadyapi ‘ajitvā sārṇavāmurvīm’ ityanena yuddhavīraḥ, ‘aniṣṭa‍vā vividhairmakhaiḥ’ ityanena dānavīraḥ, ‘adattvā cārthamarthibhyaḥ’ ityanena dayāvīraścotsāharūpeṇa niṣpattau varṇitaḥ*, *tathāpyekaśo 'pyete rasaniṣpattyai prabhavantīti pradarśyante ||

teṣu yuddhavīro yathā—

‘etāṃ paśya *puraḥsthalīmiha kila krīḍākirāto haraḥ kodaṇḍena kirīṭinā sarabhasaṃ cūḍāntare tāḍitaḥ | ityākarṇya kathādbhutaṃ himanidhāvadrau subhadrāpate- rmandaṃ mandamakāri yena nijayordordaṇḍayormaṇḍanam 104’

dānavīro yathā—

‘dadhikṣīraghṛtāmbhodhivyañjanaspṛhaṇīyayā | mahādānotsave yasya hantakārāyitaṃ bhuvā || 105 ||’

dayāvīro yathā—

‘sa tvaṃ madīyena śarīravṛttiṃ dehena nirvartayituṃ yatasva | dināvasānotsukabālavatsā vimucyatāṃ dhenuriyaṃ maharṣeḥ || 106 ||’

krodhasya yadyapi *bhāmādayo *mānabhedāścaturviṃśatiḥ saṃbhavanti tathāpi lalitālalitobhayabhedena rūpeṇa krameṇa sarvasaṃgrahāttatra traya eva prakārāḥ pradarśyante ||

[page 607]

teṣu strīṇāṃ *lalitakopo bhāmo yathā—

‘bhrūbhedibhiḥ prakampauṣṭhairlalitāṅa‍gulitarjanaiḥ | yatra kopaiḥ kṛtā srīṇāṃ saṃprasādārthinaḥ priyāḥ || 107 ||’

priyāparādhajanmā duḥkhotpīḍo manyuryathā—

‘dhaṇuovappaṇavallariviraïakaṇṇāvaaṃsaduppecche | vāhaguruā* *ṇisammaï vāhīea bahumuhe diṭṭhī || 108 ||’
[dhanudhanvapanavallarīviracitakarṇāvataṃsaduṣprekṣye | bāṣpagurukā niśāmyati bādhyā vadhūmukhe dṛṣṭiḥ ||]

nanviyamīrṣyā kasmānna bhavati, nātra *mānadānāmarṣamātraṃ vivakṣitamapi tu tajjanito duḥkhātiśaya iti ||

priyādiṣu vyājanindotprāso yathā—

‘pahavaṃti ccia* purisā mahilāṇaṃ kiṃ *tha suhaa vihiosi | *aṇurāaṇolliāe ko doso *āhijāīe || 109 ||’
[prabhavantyeva puruṣā mahilānāṃ kimatra subhaga vihito 'si | anurāganoditāyāḥ ko doṣa ābhijātyāyāḥ ||]

hāsasya yadyapyupahāsādayo bhedāḥ saṃbhavanti tathāpi vihasitena teṣāṃ *saṃgrahādīṣannyūnādhikamiti *trayastadbhedā udāhriyante—

tatreṣaddhasitaṃ smitaṃ yathā—

‘puṣpaṃ pravālopahitaṃ yadi syānmuktāphalaṃ vā sphuṭavidrumastham |’[page 608] tato 'nukuryādviśadasya tasyāstāmrauṣṭhaparyastarucaḥ smitasya || 110 ||’

dṛṣṭadaśanakānti hasitaṃ yathā—

‘timiraniruddhabhīmarajanīmukhacandrikayā *gaṇapatitāṇḍavābhinayadarśanadīpikayā | abhibhavasi tvamadya śaśinaḥ *śriyamutkaṭayā daśanamayūkhamañjaritayā hasitaprabhayā || 111 ||’

tadeva saviśeṣaṃ *hasitaṃ yathā—

‘cyutāmindorlekhāṃ ratikalahabhagnaṃ ca valayaṃ dva‍yaṃ cakrīkṛtya prahasitamukhī* śailatanayā | avocadyaṃ paśyetyavatu sa śivaḥ sā ca girijā sa ca krīḍācandro daśanakiraṇāpūritatanuḥ || 112 ||’

suptaviśeṣaḥ svapno yathā—

‘jāne kopaparāṅmukhī priyatamā svapne 'dya dṛṣṭā mayā mā mā saṃspṛśa pāṇineti rudatī gantuṃ pravṛttā puraḥ | no yāvatparirabhya cāṭukaśatairāśvāsayāmi priyāṃ* bhrātastāvadahaṃ śaṭhena vidhinā nidrādaridrīkṛtaḥ || 113 ||’

mūrcchāviśeṣo maraṇaṃ yathā—

‘kṣaṇamātrasakhīṃ sujātayoḥ stanayostāmavalokya vihvaṃlā | nimimīla narendrasundarī hṛtacandrā tamaseva śarvarī || 114 ||’
[page 609]

mativiśeṣaḥ *śamo yathā—

‘yadāsīdajñānaṃ smaratimirasaṃskārajanitaṃ tadā dṛṣṭaṃ nārīmayamidamaśeṣaṃ jagaditi | idānīmasmākaṃ paṭutaravivekāñjanajuṣāṃ samībhūtā dṛṣṭistribhuvanamapi brahma manute || 115 ||’
evamanye 'pi vijñeyā *rasabhāvādisaṃśrayāḥ | viśeṣāḥ prāptakālo 'tha *pariśeṣo *nidarśyate || 167 ||

tatrāśrayastridhā—pumān—strī—tiryagādayaḥ ||

teṣu pumān yathā—

‘āścaryamutpaladṛśo vadanāmalendu- sāṃnidhyato mama muhurjaḍimānametya | jātyena* candramaṇineva mahīdharasya saṃdhāryate dravamayo manasā vikāraḥ || 116 ||’

strī yathā—

‘tenātha nātha durudāharaṇātapena* saumyāpi nāma paruṣatvamabhiprapannā | jajvāla tīkṣṇaviśadāḥ sahasodgirarantī* vāgarciṣastapanakāntaśileva sītā || 117 ||’

tiryagādiṣu yathā—

‘utkūjati śvasiti muhyati yāti tīraṃ tīrāttaruṃ tarutalātpunareti* vāpīm | [page 610] vāpyāṃ na rajyati na cātti mṛṇālakhaṇḍaṃ cakraḥ kṣapāsu virahe khalu cakravākyāḥ || 118 ||’

viṣayastridhā—cetanaḥ, tiryagū, acetanaśca ||

teṣu cetano yathā—

‘iyaṃ sā lolākṣī tribhuvanalalāmaikavasatiḥ sa cāyaṃ duṣṭātmā svasurapakṛtaṃ yena mama tat | itastīvraḥ kāmo gururayamitaḥ krodhadahanaḥ kṛto veṣaścāyaṃ kathamidamiti bhrāmyati manaḥ || 119 ||’

tiryagū yathā—

‘āyāte dayite marusthalabhuvāṃ *saṃcintya durlaṅa‍ghyatāṃ *gehinyā paritoṣabāṣpataralāmāsajya dṛṣṭiṃ *mukhe | dattvā pīluśamīkarīrakavalān *svenāñcalenādarā- dunmṛṣṭaṃ karabhasya kesarasaṭābhārāgralagnaṃ* rajaḥ || 120 ||’

acetano yathā—

‘kṣiptaṃ puro na jagṛhe muhurikṣukāṇḍaṃ nāpekṣate sma nikaṭopagatāṃ kareṇum | sasmāra vāraṇapatiḥ parimīlitākṣa- micchāvihāravanavāsamahotsavānām* || 121 ||’

jñānaṃ tridhā—dṛṣṭam, śrutam, anumānajaṃ ca ||

[page 611]

teṣu dṛṣṭaṃ yathā—

‘sarasijamanuviddhaṃ śaivalenāpi ramyaṃ malinamapi himāṃśorlakṣma lakṣmīṃ tanoti | iyamadhikamanojñā valkalenāpi tanvī kimiva hi madhurāṇāṃ *maṇḍanaṃ nākṛtīnām || 122 ||’

śrutaṃ yathā—

‘kiṃ rūpaṃ sphuṭameva sā śaśimukhī dhatte tadatyadbhutaṃ māmutsāhayituṃ parāpakaraṇe cittaṃ kimasmatsvasuḥ | ityantarvikasadvitarkavidhuraṃ cetastathā vartate svalpo 'pyeṣa mama prayāti purataḥ panthā yathā dīrghatām 123’

anumānaṃ yathā—

‘śāntamidamāśramapadaṃ sphurati ca bāhuḥ kutaḥ phalamihāsya | athavā bhavitavyānāṃ dvārāṇi bhavanti sarvatra || 124 ||’

saṃskārastridhā—ādṛtaḥ, paṭuḥ, abhyastaśceti* | tatrāśrayaguṇenādarapratyayādutpanna* ādṛto yathā—

‘kanyāratnamayonijanma bhavatāmāste vayaṃ cārthino ratnaṃ yatkvacidasti* tatpariṇamatyasmāsu śakrādapi | kanyāyāśca parārthataiva hi matā tasyāḥ pradānādahaṃ bandhurvo bhavitā pulastyapulahapraṣṭhāśca saṃbandhinaḥ || 125 ||’

viṣayaguṇena paṭupratyayādutpannaḥ paṭuryathā—

‘utpattirdevayajanādbrahmavādī nṛpaḥ pitā | suprasannojjvalā mūrtirasyāḥ* snehaṃ karoti me || 126 ||’
[page 612]

jñānapaunaḥ*punyenābhyāsapratyayādutpanno 'bhyastaḥ ||

sa yathā—

‘bhūyo bhūyaḥ savidhanagarīrathyayā paryaṭantaṃ dṛṣṭa‍vā dṛṣṭa‍vā bhavanavalabhītuṅa‍gavātāyanasthā | sākṣātkāmaṃ navamiva ratirmālatī mādhavaṃ yadgạ̄dhotkaṇṭhālulitalulitairaṅa‍gakaistāmyatīti || 127 ||’

atra yadyapi viṣayaguṇāt paṭuḥ, āśrayaguṇādāhato 'pi* pratyayaḥ, paṭumāhataṃ ca* saṃskāraṃ *prasūte tathāpyabhyāsātpaṭīyānāhatatamaśca jāyamāno 'bhyasta ityucyate ||

uddīpanavibhāveṣu mālyavastravibhūṣaṇādayo mālyādayaḥ ||

teṣu mālyaṃ yathā—

‘aśokanirbhartsitapadmarāgamākṛṣṭahemadyutikarṇikāram* | muktākalāpīkṛtasindhuvāraṃ vasantapuṣpābharaṇaṃ vahantī || 128 ||’

vastraṃ yathā—

‘āvarjitā kiṃcidiva stanābhyāṃ vāso vasānā taruṇārkarāgam | sujātapuṣpastabakāvanamrā* saṃcāriṇī pallavinī lateva || 129 ||’

vibhūṣaṇaṃ yathā—

‘kaṇṭhasya tasyāḥ stanabandhurasya muktākalāpasya ca *nistalasya | anyonyaśobhājananādbabhūva sādhāraṇo bhūṣaṇabhūṣyabhāvaḥ 130’

*ṛtuvayomadādaya ṛtvādayaḥ |

[page 613]

teṣu ṛturyathā—

‘idamapulabhavastu prārthanādunirvāraṃ prathamamapi mano me pañcabāṇaḥ kṣiṇoti | kimuta malayavātonmūlitāpāṇḍupattrai- rupavanasahakārairdarśiteṣvaṅa‍kureṣu || 131 ||’

vayo yathā—

‘māmūmuhatkhalu bhavantamananyajanmā mā te malīmasavikāraghanā matirbhūt | ityādi nanviha nirarthakameva yasmā- tkāmaśca jṛmbhitaguṇo navayauvanaṃ ca || 132 ||’

mado yathā—

‘tatkṣaṇaṃ viparivartitahriyorneṣyatoḥ* śayanamiddharāgayoḥ | sā babhūva vaśavartinī *dvayoḥ śūlinaḥ suvadanā madasya ca 133’

candanasnānadhūpādayaścandanādayaḥ |

teṣu candanaṃ yathā—

‘candanaṃ viṣadharāśrayaḥ śaśī vāruṇī ca viṣasodarāvubhau | tāpayanti virahe kimucyate mārayanti na yadetadadbhutam 134’

snānaṃ yathā—

‘āambaloaṇāṇaṃ *ollaṃsuapā*aḍorujahaṇāṇaṃ | *avaraṇhamajjirīṇaṃ kae ṇa kāmo *dhaṇuṃ vahaï || 135 ||’
[ātāmralocanānāmārdrāṃśukaprakaṭorujaghanānām | aparāhṇamajjanaśīlānāṃ kṛte na kāmo dhanurvahati ||]
[page 614]

dhūpo yathā—

‘snānārdramukteṣva*nudhūpavāsaṃ vinyastasāyantanamallikeṣu | kāmo *vasantātyayamandavīryaḥ keśeṣu lebhe balamaṅa‍ganānām 136’

candrodayo ghanadhvanirupakārasmaraṇamityādyāścandrodayādayaḥ |

teṣu candrodayo yathā—

‘*vilimpatyetasminmalayajarasārdreṇa* mahasā diśāṃ vaktraṃ candre sukṛtamatha tasyā mṛgadṛśaḥ | dṛśorbāṣpaḥ pāṇau vadanamasavaḥ kaṇṭhakuhare hṛdi tvaṃ hrīḥ pṛṣṭhe vacasi ca guṇā eva bhavataḥ || 137’

ghanadhvaniryathā—

‘ajja mae teṇa viṇā *aṇuhūasuhāiṁ saṃmaraṃtīe | *ahiṇavamehāṇaṁ ravo ṇisāmio *vajjhapaḍaho vva || 138 ||’
[adya mayā tena vinānubhūtasukhāni saṃsmarantyā | abhinavameghānāṃ ravo niśāmito vadhyapaṭaha iva ||]

upakārasmaraṇaṃ yathā—

‘tanme manaḥ kṣipati yatsarasaprahāramālokya māmagaṇitaskhaladuttarīyā | trastaika*hāyanakuraṅa‍gaviloladṛṣṭirāśliṣṭavatyamṛtasaṃvalitairivāṅa‍gaiḥ || 139 ||’
[page 615]

anubhāveṣu *smarati yathā—

‘khaṇamettaṃ pi* ṇa phiṭṭaï aṇudiahaṃ *diṇṇagaruasaṃtāvā | *pacchaṇṇapāvasaṃkavva sāmalī majjha *hiaāhiṁ || 140 ||’
[kṣaṇamātramapi nāpagac‍chatyanudivasaṃ dattagurukasaṃtāpā | pracchannapāpaśaṅa‍keva śyāmalāṅa‍gī mama hṛdayāt ||]

vāñchati* yathā—

‘emea *akaaüṇṇā appattamaṇorahā vivajjisaṃ | jaṇavāo vi ṇa jāo teṇa samaṃ haliaütteṇa* || 141 ||’
[evamevākṛtapuṇyāprāptamanorathā vipatsye | janavādo 'pi na jātastena samaṃ halikaputreṇa ||]

dveṣṭi* yathā—

‘gottakkhalaṇaṃ soūṇa piaame ajja *māmi *chaṇadiahe | vajjhamahisassa mālavva maṃḍaṇaṃ se ṇa *paḍihāi || 142 ||’
[gotraskhalanaṃ śrutvā priyatame 'dya sakhi *kṣaṇadivase | vadhyamahiṣasya māleva maṇḍanamasyā na pratibhāti ||]

prayatate yathā—

‘anugacchanmunitanayāṃ sahasā vinayena vāritaprasaraḥ | svasthānādacalannapi gatveva punaḥ pratinivṛttaḥ || 143 ||’
[page 616]

*avaiti yathā—

‘candasarisaṃ muhaṃ se sariso amaassa muharaso tissā | sakaaggaharahasujjalacuṃbaṇaaṃ kassa sarisaṃ se || 144 ||’
[candrasadṛśaṃ mukhamasyāḥ sadṛśo 'mṛtasya mukharasastasyāḥ | sakacagraharabhasojjvalacumbanakaṃ kasya sadṛśamasyāḥ ||]

manyate yathā—

‘*parivaṭṭaṃtiva ṇisaṃsa(ma)i maṃḍaliakusumāuhaṃ va aṇaṃgaṃ | virahammi maṇṇaï harīṇahe* aṇatthapaḍiuṭṭhiaṃ va miaṃkam || 145’
[parivartamāneva(?) niśāmyate maṇḍalitakusumāyudhamivānaṅa‍gam | virahe manyate hārinakhe anarthapratyutthitamiva mṛgāṅa‍kam ||]

vakti yathā—

‘ālāo mā dijjaü loaviruddhatti ṇāma kāūṇa | samuhāvaḍie ko verie vi diṭṭhiṃ ṇa pāḍei || 146 ||’
[ālāpo mā dīyatāṃ lokaviruddha iti nāma kṛtvā | saṃmukhāpatite ko vairiṇyapi dṛpṭiṃ na pātayati ||]

ceṣṭate yathā—

‘ajja mae gaṃtavvaṃ ghaṇaṃdhaāre vi tassa suhaassa | ajjā ṇimīliacchī paaparivāḍiṃ ghare kuṇaï || 147 ||’
[adya mayā gantavyaṃ ghanāndhakāre 'pi tasya subhagasya | āryā nimīlitākṣī padaparipāṭīṃ gṛhe karoti ||]
[page 617]

saṃcāriṣu svedaromāñcavepathavo yathā—

‘diṭṭhe jaṃ pulaïjjasi *tharaharasi piammi jaṃ samāsaṇṇe | tuha saṃbhāsaṇa*seulliphaṃsaṇe kiṃ vi *ṇijjihisi || 148 ||’
[dṛṣṭe yatpulakāyase tharaharāyase priye yatsamāsanne | tava saṃbhāṣaṇasvedārdrīkṛtasparśe kimapi nīyase ||]

aśru yathā—

‘*ṇaaṇabbhaṃtaragholaṃtabāhabharamaṃtharāi* diṭṭhīe | puṇaruttapechirīe* vālaa kiṃ jaṃ ṇa bhaṇio si || 149 ||’
[nayanābhyantaraghūrṇamānabāṣpabharamantharayā dṛṣṭayā | punaruktaprekṣaṇaśīlayā bālaka kiṃ yanna bhaṇito 'si ||]

harṣo yathā—

‘savvassammi vidaddhe(ḍ̣dhe)* taha vi hu hiaassa ṇivvudi ccea | jaṃ teṇa gāmaḍāhe hatthāhatthiṃ kuḍo gahio || 150 ||’
[sarvasve 'pi dagdhe tathāpi khalu hṛdayasya nirvṛtireva | yattena grāmadāhe hastāhasti kuṇḍo gṛhītaḥ ||]

amarṣo yathā—

‘katto saṃpaḍaï *maha pi piasahi piasaṃgamo paose vi | jaṃ jiajaï* gahia*karaṇiara khiṃkhirī* caṃdacaṃḍālo’ ||
[kutaḥ saṃpatati mamāpi priyasakhi priyasaṃgamaḥ pradoṣe 'pi | yajjīvati gṛhītakaranikarakhiṃkhirī candracaṇḍālaḥ ||]
[page 618]

līlādiṣu priyajanaceṣṭānukṛtilīṃlā yathā—

‘jaṃ jaṃ karesi jaṃ jaṃ jappasi jaṃ* jaṃ ṇiacchesi | taṃ tamaṇusikkharīe* dīho diaho ṇa saṃpaḍaï || 152 ||’
[yadyatkaroṣi yadyajjalpasi yadyannirīkṣase | tattadanuśikṣaṇaśīlāyā dīrgho divaso na saṃpadyate ||]

netrabhrūvaktrakarmaṇāṃ viśeṣaṇe lasanaṃ vilāso yathā—

‘sabhrūvilāsamatha so 'yamitīrayitvā sapratyabhijñamiva māmavalokya tasyāḥ | anyonyabhāvacatureṇa sakhījanena muktāstadā smitasudhāmadhurāḥ kaṭākṣāḥ || 153 ||’

vibhūṣaṇādīnāmanādaravinyāso vicchittiryathā—

‘aṅa‍gāni candanarajaḥparidhūsarāṇi tāmbūlarāgasulabho 'dharapallavaśca | acchāñjane ca nayane vasanaṃ tanīyaḥ kāntāsu bhūṣaṇamidaṃ vibhavaśca śeṣaḥ || 154 ||’

vibhūṣaṇādīnāmasthānaprayogo vibhramo yathā—

‘cakāra kācitsitacandanāṅa‍ke kāñcīkalāpaṃ stanabhārapṛṣṭhe | priyaṃ prati preṣitacittavṛtti- rnitambabimbe ca *babhāra hāram || 155 ||’
[page 619]

smitaruditahasitādīnāṃ harṣādasakṛdekīkaraṇaṃ kilakiñcitaṃ yathā—

‘pāṇipallavavidhūnanamantaḥsītkṛtāni *nayanārdhanimeṣāḥ | yoṣitāṃ rahasi gadgadavācāmastratāmupayayurmadanasya || 156 ||’

dṛṣṭajanakathāyāṃ tadbhāvabhāvanotthitavikāro moṭṭāyitaṃ yathā—

‘tava sā kathāsu parighaṭṭayati śravaṇaṃ yadaṅa‍gulimukhena muhuḥ | ghanatāṃ dhruvaṃ nayati tena bhavadguṇapūgapūritamatṛptatayā || 157 ||’

keśastanādharādigrahaṇādduḥkhe 'pi sukhabuddhiceṣṭā kuṭṭamitaṃ yathā—

‘hnībharādavanataṃ parirambhe rāgavānavaṭujeṣvavakṛṣya | arpitoṣṭhadalamānanapadmaṃ yoṣito mukulitākṣamadhāsīt || 158 ||’

abhīṣṭaprāptāvabhimānagarvasaṃbhāvanānādarakṛto viṃkāro *vivvoko yathā—

‘nirvibhujya daśanacchadaṃ tato vāci bharturavadhīraṇāparā | śailarājatanayā samīpagāmālalāpa vijayāmahetukam || 159 ||’

sukumāratayā karacaraṇāṅa‌‍ganyāso lalitaṃ yathā—

‘gurutarakala*nūpurānunādaṃ* salalitanartitavāmapādapadmā | itaradanatilolamādadhānā padamatha manmathamantharaṃ jagāma 160’

vaktavyasamaye 'pi vacasābhibhāṣya kriyānuṣṭhānaṃ vihṛtaṃ yathā—

‘patyuḥ śiraścandrakalāmanena spṛśeti sakhyā parihāsapūrvam | sā rañjayitvā caraṇau kṛtāśīrmālyena tāṃ nirvacanaṃ jaghāna || 161 ||’

bālyakaumārayauvanasādhāraṇo vihāraviśeṣaḥ krīḍitaṃ yathā—

‘mandākinīsaikatavedikābhiḥ sā kandukaiḥ kṛtrimaputrakaiśca | [page 620] reme muhurmadhyagatā sakhīnāṃ krīḍārasaṃ nirviśatīva bālye || 162 ||’

krīḍitameva *priyatamaviṣaye keliryathā—

‘vyapohitaṃ locanato mukhānilai- rapārayantaṃ kila puṣpajaṃ rajaḥ | payodhareṇorasi kācidunmanāḥ priyaṃ jaghānonnatapīvarastanī || 163 ||’

helādiṣu rāgataḥ sahasā pravṛttihetuścittollāso helā | sā striyāṃ yathā—

‘rehaï piaparirambhaṇapasāriaṃ suraamaṃdiraddāre | *helāhalahaliathorathaṇaharaṃ bhualaājualaṃ || 164 ||’
[rājate priyaparirambhaṇaprasāritaṃ suratamandiradvāre | vegakautukitasthūlastanabharaṃ bhujalatāyugalam ||]

saiva puruṣe yathā—

‘uttiṣṭhantyā ratānte bharamuragapatau pāṇinaikena kṛtvā dhṛtvā cānyena vāso vigalitakavarībhāramaṃse vahantyāḥ | bhūyastatkālakāntidviguṇitasurataprītinā śauriṇā vaḥ śayyāmāliṅa‍gya nītaṃ vapuralasalasadbāhu lakṣmyāḥ punātu || 165 ||’

helaiva savacanavinyāso hāvaḥ | sa striyāṃ yathā—

‘jaï ṇa chivasi pupphavaïṃ purao tā kīsa* vārio ṭhāsi | chittosi culuculantehiṁ *pahāviūṇa maha hatthehiṃ || 166 ||’
[yadi na spṛśasi puṣpavatīṃ puratastatkiṃ vāritastiṣṭhasi | spṛṣṭo 'si culuculāyamānaiḥ dhāvitvāsmākaṃ hastābhyām ||]
[page 621]

sa eva puruṣe yathā—

‘loo jūraï *jūraü vaaṇijjaṃ hoi hou taṃ ṇāma | ehi *ṇimajjasu* pāse pupphavaï ṇa ei me ṇiddā || 167 ||’
[lokaḥ khidyate khidyatu vacanīyaṃ bhavati bhavatu tannāma | ehi nimajja pārśve puṣpavati naiti me nidrā ||]

ādigrahaṇena bhāvādayo gṛhyante | teṣu bhāvāḥ striyāṃ yathā—

‘tāvaccia raïsamae mahilāṇaṃ vibbhamā virāaṃti | jāva ṇa kuvalaadala*sacchahāiṁ maüleṃti ṇaaṇāiṃ || 168 ||’
[tāvadeva ratisamaye mahilānāṃ vibhramā virājante | yāvanna kuvalayadalasacchāyāni mukulībhavanti nayanāni ||]

vyājaḥ puṃso yathā—

‘aliapasuttaviṇimīliaccha de suhaa majjha oāsaṃ | gaṃḍapariuṃbaṇāpulaïaṃga ṇa puṇo cirāissaṃ || 169 ||’
[*alīkaprasuptavinimīlitākṣa he subhaga mamāvakāśam | gaṇḍaparicumbanāpulakitāṅa‍ga na punaścirayiṣyāmi ||]

visrambhabhāṣaṇaṃ striyā yathā—

‘jāo so vi vilakkho mae vi hasiūṇa gāḍhamuvagụ̄dho | paḍhamosariassa ṇiaṃsaṇassa gaṃṭhiṃ vimagganto || 170 ||’
[jātaḥ so 'pi vilakṣo mayāpi hasitvā gāḍhamupagūḍhaḥ | *prathamāpasṛtasya nivasanasya granthiṃ vimārgayamāṇaḥ ||]
[page 622]

cāṭu strīpuṃsayoryathā—

‘ekkaṃ *paharuvviṇṇaṃ hatthaṃ muhamāruṇṇaṃ eṇa vīaṃto | so vi hasaṃtīeĕ mae gahio vīeṇa kaṃṭhammi || 171 ||’
[ekaṃ prahārodvignaṃ hastaṃ mukhamārutena bījayan | so 'pi hasantyā mayā gṛhīto dvitīyena kaṇṭhe ||]

premābhisaṃdhānaṃ puṃso yathā—

‘kelīgottakkhalaṇe varassa papphullaïṃ dihiṃ dehi | bahuvāsaavāsahare bahue vāholliā diṭṭhī || 172 ||’
[kelīgotraskhalane varasya praphullāṃ dhṛtiṃ dadhāti | bahuvāsakavāsagṛhe vadhvā bāṣpārditā dṛṣṭiḥ ||]

parihāsaḥ striyāṃ(yā) yathā—

‘aï diara kiṃ ṇa *pecchasi āāsaṃ kiṃ muhā paloesi | jāāi bāhumūlaṃ mi *addhaandāṇaṁ paḍivāḍiṃ || 173 ||’
[ayi devara kiṃ na prekṣasa ākāśaṃ kiṃ mudhā pralokayasi | jāyāyā bāhumūle 'rdhacandrāṇāṃ paripāṭīm ||]

kutūhalaṃ puṃso yathā—

‘asamattamaṃḍaṇaccia* vacca gharaṃ se sakouhallassa | *bolāviahalahalassaa[assa]putti citte ṇa *laggihisi ||’
[asamāptamaṇḍanaiva vraja gṛhaṃ tasya sakautūhalasya | vyatikrāntautsukyasya putri citte na lagiṣyasi ||]
[page 623]

cakitaṃ striyā yathā—

‘*ṇavalaï pahāratuṭhṭhāi* taṃ kaaṃ kiṃ pi haliasoṇhāe | jaṃ ajja vi juaïjaṇo ghare ghare sikkhiuṃ bhamaï || 175 ||’
[patināmapraśnapūrvakaprahāratuṣṭayā tatkṛtaṃ kimapi hālikasnuṣayā | yadadyāpi yuvatijano gṛhe gṛhe śikṣituṃ bhramati ||]
helā *hāvaśca bhāvaśca vyājo visrambhabhāṣaṇam | cāṭu premābhisaṃdhānaṃ parihāsaḥ kutūhalam || 168 ||
cakitaṃ ceti nirdiṣṭāśceṣṭāḥ kāścidvilāsinām | śeṣāṇāṃ vipralambhādau rūpamāvirbhaviṣyati || 169 ||

tatra nāyakayoḥ prāgasaṃgatayoḥ, saṃgatayośca, saṃgataviyuktayorvā, mithodarśanaśravaṇābhyāmavasthitābhimānajanmā parasparānurāgo 'nyatarānurāgo vābhilaṣaṇīyāliṅa‍ganādīnāmanavāptau satyāṃ samupajāyamānaistaistairutkaṇṭhādibhirvyabhicāribhāvairmanovāgbuddhiśarīrārambhajanmabhiścānubhāvairanubaddhaḥ prāptaprāpyaprakarṣāvastho vipralambhaśrṛṅa‍gārākhyāṃ labhate | sa caturdhā—pūrvānurāgo, mānaḥ, pravāsaḥ, karuṇaśca ||

teṣu prāgasaṃgatayoḥ pūrvānurāgaḥ puruṣaprakāṇḍe yathā—

‘dūraṃ muktālatayā bisasitayā vipralobhyamāno me | haṃsa iva darśitāśo mānasajanmā tvayā nītaḥ || 176 ||’

atra puṇḍarīkasya mahāśvetāyāṃ prāgasaṃgatāyāṃ samutpannaḥ saṃkalparamaṇīyo 'bhilāṣastadanāptāvuktaprakāreṇa prakṛṣyamāṇastvayā me *mānasajanmā dūraṃ nīta ityuttarakāmāvasthayā prakāśyate ||

[page 624]

sa eva strīprakāṇḍe yathā—

‘dullahajaṇānurāo lajjā garuī paravaso appā | piasahi visamaṃ pemmaṃ maraṇaṃ saraṇaṃ *ṇavari ekkaṃ || 177 ||’
[durlabhajanānurāgo lajjā gurvī paravaśa ātmā | priyasakhi viṣamaṃ prema maraṇaṃ śaraṇamanantaramekam ||]

atrāpi prāgvadeva sāgarikāyā vatsarāje 'nurāgaḥ prakṛṣyamāṇo maraṇaṃ śaraṇamityuttarayaiva kāmāvasthayā kathyate ||

saṃgatayormānaḥ sa nirheturyathā—

‘atthakkarūsaṇaṃ* khaṇapasijjaṇaṃ aliavaaṇaṇibbandho | *ummaccharasaṃtāvo puttaa paavī siṇehassa || 178 ||’
[akasmādroṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇaprasādanamalīkavacananirbandhaḥ | unmatsarasaṃtāpaḥ putraka padavī snehasya ||]

atra premagateḥ svabhāvakauṭilyāddhetumantareṇopajāyamāno nirheturucyate sa eva saheturyathā—

‘*paḍiucchiā ṇa jaṃpaï gahiā vi pphuraï cumbiā rusaï | tuṇhiṃkā* ṇavabahuā *kaāvarāheṇa daïeṇa || 179 ||’
[paripṛṣṭā na jalpati gṛhītāpi sphurati cumvitā ruṣyati | tūṣṇīṃbhūtā navavadhūkā kṛtāparādhena dayitena ||]

atra yadyapyāliṅa‍ganāderneti netyādeḥ pratiṣedho na vidyate tathāpi tadartho 'styeveti mānalakṣaṇaṃ ghaṭate ||

[page 625]

saṃgataviyuktayoḥ pravāsaḥ | sa navānurāgo yathā—

‘priyamādhave kimasi mayyavatsalā nanu so 'hameva yamanandayatpurā | *ayamāgṛhītakamanīyakaṅa‍kaṇaḥ *sakhi mūrtimāniva mahotsavaḥ karaḥ || 180 ||

atra vivāhānantarameva mālatyāḥ kapālakuṇḍalayāpahārānmādhavamālatyorayaṃ navānurāgaḥ pravāsa ucyate ||

sa eva praụdhānurāgo yathā—

‘tvāmālikhya praṇayakupitāṃ dhāturāgaiḥ śilāyāmātmānaṃ te caraṇapatitaṃ yāvadicchāmi kartum | asraistāvanmuhurupacitairdṛṣṭirālupyate me krūrastasminnapi na sahate saṃgamaṃ nau kṛtāntaḥ || 181 ||’

atra prācīnapraṇayaprasādanābhiranurāgasya praụdhiravagamyate ||

saṃgatayorevānyataravyapāye karuṇaḥ | sa strīvyapāye puruṣasya yathā—

‘dhruvamasmi śaṭhaḥ śucismite kalitaḥ kaitavavatsalastvayā | paralokamasaṃnivṛttaye yadanāmantrya* gatāsi māmitaḥ || 182 ||’

atrendumatīvyapāyādajasya duḥkhātiśayaḥ karuṇa ucyate ||

sa eva puruṣasya vyapāye striyā yathā—

‘hṛdaye vasasīti matpriyaṃ yadavocastadavaimi kaitavam | upacārapadaṃ na cedidaṃ tvamanaṅa‍gaḥ kathamakṣatā ratiḥ || 183 ||’

atrānaṅa‍gaviṣaye rateḥ *śokaprakarṣaḥ karuṇa ityākhyāyate ||

[page 626]

*hīnapātrādiṣu caitadābhāsā bhavanti | tatra hīnapātreṣu puṃsi premānurāgo yathā—

‘kaalīgabbhasaricche ūrū daṭṭhūṇa haliasoṇhāe | ullalaï ṇaharaṃjaṇaṃ caṃdilassa* seulliakarassa || 184 ||’
[kadalīgarbhasadṛkṣe ūrū dṛṣṭa‍vā hālikasnuṣāyāḥ | ārdrībhavati nakharañjanaṃ nāpitasya svedārditakarasya ||]

atraiva striyāṃ māno yathā—

‘paḍhamaghariṇīa samaaṃ *ua piṃḍāre* daraṃ kuṇantammi | ṇavabahuāi sarosaṃ savva ccia vacchalā mukkā || 185 ||’
[prathamagṛhiṇyā samakaṃ paśyābhīre bhayaṃ kurvati | navavadhvā saroṣaṃ sarve 'pi ca vatsakā muktāḥ ||]

tiryakṣu pakṣiṇi pravāso yathā—

‘āpṛcchāmi vyathayati mano durbalā vāsaraśrīre- hyāliṅa‍ga kṣapaya rajanīmekikā cakravāki | nānyāsakto na khalu kupito nānurāgacyuto vā daivādhīnaḥ sapadi bhavatīmasvatastrastyajāmi || 186 ||’

atraiva kariṇi* karuṇo yathā—

‘nāntarvartayati dhvanatsu jaladeṣvāmandramudgarjitaṃ nāsannātsarasaḥ karoti kavalānāvarjitaiḥ śaivalaiḥ | dānajyāniviṣaṇṇamūkamadhupavyāsaṅa‍gadīnānano nūnaṃ prāṇasamāviyogavidhuraḥ* stamberamastāmyati || 187 ||’

atha saṃbhogaḥ | tatra nāyakayoḥ prāgasaṃgatayoḥ saṃgataviyuktayorvā [page 627]mithaḥ samāgame prāgutpannastadānīṃtano vā ratyākhyaḥ sthāyibhāvo 'bhilaṣaṇīyāliṅa‍ganādīnāmavāptau satyāṃ samupajāyamānairharṣa-dhṛti-smṛti-matiprabhṛtibhirvyabhicāribhāvaiḥ saṃsṛjyamānaḥ, ṛtūdyānopagamajalakrīḍāparvatopadeśaprasādhanagṛha*madhupānendūdayādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamānaḥ, savibhramabhrūkaṭākṣavikṣepālāpasaṃbhramasmitādibhiranubhāvairabhivyajyamāna īpsitamāsādayan, jihāsitaṃ vā jihānaḥ, prāptaprāpyaprakarṣārambhaḥ saṃbhogaśrṛṅa‍gārākhyāṃ labhate | sa caturdhā—prathamānurāgānantaraḥ, mānānantaraḥ, pravāsānantaraḥ, karuṇānantara iti ||

teṣu prathamānurāgāntaro yathā—

‘pāṇiggahaṇe ccia* pavvaīa ṇāaṃ sahīhiṃ sohaggam | pasuvaïṇā vāsuikaṃkaṇammi osārie dūram || 188 ||’
[pāṇigrahaṇa eva pārvatyā jñātaṃ sakhībhiḥ saubhāgyam | paśupatinā vāsukikaṅa‍kaṇe 'pasārite dūram ||]

mānāntaro yathā—

‘uvvahaï dahaagahiāharoṭṭhajhijjantarosapaḍirāam | pāṇosarantamaïraṃ *casaaṃ va ṇiaṃ muhaṃ bālā || 189 ||’
[udvahati dayitagṛhitādharauṣṭhakṣīyamāṇaroṣapratirāgam | pānāpasaranmadiraṃ caṣakamiva nijaṃ sukhaṃ bālā ||]

pravāsānantaro yathā—

‘maṃgalavalaaṃ jīaṃ va rakkhiaṃ jaṃ paütthavaïāi* | pattapiadaṃsaṇūsasiabāhulaïāiṃ taṃ* bhiṇṇam || 190 ||’
[maṅa‍galavalayaṃ jīvitamiva rakṣitaṃ yatproṣitapatikayā | prāptapriyadarśanocchvasitabāhulatikāyāṃ tadbhinnam ||]
[page 628]

karuṇānantaro yathā—

‘ṇa muammi* mue vi pie diṭṭho uṇa piṃaamo jiaṃtīe | ia lajjā a *pahariso tīe hiae ṇa saṃmāi || 191 ||’
[na mṛtāsmi mṛte 'pi priye dṛṣṭaḥ punaḥ priyatamo jīvantyā | iti lajjā ca praharṣastasyā hṛdaye na saṃmāti ||]

te 'mī catvāro 'pi saṃbhogāścaturbhireva vipralambhaiḥ prakarṣamāpadyante ||

teṣu prathamānurāgeṇa yathā—

‘induryatra na nindyate na madhuraṃ dūtīvacaḥ śrūyate *nocchvāsā hṛdayaṃ dahantyaśiśirā nopaiti kārśyaṃ vapuḥ | svādhīnāmanukūlinīṃ svagṛhiṇīmāliṅa‍gya yatsupyate tatkiṃ prema gṛhāśramavratamidaṃ kaṣṭaṃ samācaryate || 192 ||’

mānena yathā—

‘raïviggahammi* kuṇṭhīkaāo dhārāo pemmakhaggassa | aṇamaāiṃ vva sijjhanti māṇasāiṃ ṇāi* mihuṇāṇam 193’
[rativigrahe kuṇṭhīkṛtā dhārāḥ premakhaṅa‍gasya | annamayānīva svidyanti mānasāni jñāyante mithunānām ||]

pravāsena yathā—

‘śāpānto me bhujagaśayanādutthite śārṅa‍gapāṇau' māsānetān gamaya caturo locane mīlayitvā | paścādāvāṃ virahaguṇitaṃ taṃ tamātmābhilāṣaṃ* nirvekṣyāvaḥ pariṇataśaraccandrikāsu kṣapāsu || 194 ||’
[page 629]

karuṇena yathā—

‘na martyalokastridivātprahīyate mriyeta nāgre yadi vallabho janaḥ | nivṛttameva tridivaprayojanaṃ mṛtaḥ sa cejjīvata eva jīvati 195’

tiryagādiṣu caitadābhāsā bhavanti ||

teṣu sarīsṛpamṛgayoryathā—

‘madhu dvirephaḥ kusumaikapātre papau priyāṃ svāmanuvartamānaḥ | śrṛṅa‍geṇa saṃsparśanimīlitākṣīṃ mṛgīmakaṇḍūyata kṛṣṇasāraḥ 196’

paśupakṣiṇoryathā—

‘dadau saraḥpaṅa‍kajareṇugandhi gajāya gaṇḍūṣajalaṃ kareṇuḥ | ardhopabhuktena bisena jāyāṃ saṃbhāvayāmāsa rathāṅa‍ganāmā || 197 ||’

kiṃnareṣu yathā—

‘gītāntareṣu śramavārileśaiḥ *kiṃcitsamuccha‍vāsitapattralekham | puṣpāsavādhūrṇitanetraśobhi priyāmukhaṃ kiṃpuruṣaścacumbe || 198 ||’

taruṣu yathā—

‘paryāptapuṣpastabakastanībhyaḥ sphuratpravāloṣṭhamanoharābhyaḥ* | latāvadhūbhyastaravo 'pyavāpurvinamraśākhābhujabandhanāni || 199 ||’

vipralambhaceṣṭāsu prathamānurāge striyā yathā—

‘pecchaï *aladdhalakkhaṃ dīhaṃ ṇīsasaï suṇṇaaṃ hasaï | jaï jaṃpaï aphuḍatthaṃ taha se hiaaṭṭhiaṃ kiṃ vi || 200 ||’
[prekṣate 'labdhalakṣyaṃ dīrghaṃ niḥśvasiti śūnyaṃ hasati | yathā jalpatyasphuṭārthaṃ tathāsyā hṛdayasthitaṃ kimapi ||]
[page 630]

puṃso yathā—

‘so tuha* kaeṇa suṃdari taha *jhīṇo sumahilo haliaütto | jaha se macchariṇīa vi doccaṃ jāāe paḍibaṇṇam 201’
[sa tava kṛtena sundari tathā kṣīṇaḥ sumahilo hālikaputraḥ | yathāsya matsariṇyāpi dautyaṃ jāyayā pratipannam ||]

māne striyā yathā—

‘*kaṇṇujjuā varāī sā ajja tae kaāvarāheṇa | *jaṃbhāiarukkhapaloaïāiṃ diaheṇa sikkhiviā* || 202 ||’
[karṇarjukā varākī sādya tvayā kṛtāparādhena | jṛmbhāyitarūkṣapralokitāni divasena śikṣitā ||]

puṃso yathā—

‘avibhāviaraaṇimuhaṃ tassa a saccariavimalacandujjoam | jāaṃ piāvirohe baḍhaṃtāṇuamūḍhalakkhaṃ hiaama || 203 ||’
[avibhāvitarajanīmukhaṃ tasyāśca saccaritavimalacandroddayotam | jātaṃ priyāvirodhe vardhamānānuśayamūḍhalakṣyaṃ hṛdayam ||]

pravāse striyā yathā—

‘piyasaṃbharaṇapalloṭṭa*tavāhadhārāṇi*vāabhiāe | dijjaï vaṃkaggīvāi* dīvao pahiajāāe || 204 ||’
[priyasaṃsmaraṇapraluṭhadbāṣpadhārānipātabhītayā | dīyate vakragrīvayā dīpakaḥ pathikajāyayā ||]
[page 631]

puṃso yathā—

‘majjhaṇṇapatthiassa vi gimhe pahiassa haraï saṃtāvam | hiaaṭṭhiajāāmuhamiaṃkajoṇhājalappavaho* || 205 ||’
[madhyāhnaprasthitasyāpi grīṣme pathikasya harati saṃtāpam | hṛdayasthitajāyāmukhamṛgāṅa‍kajyotsnajalapravāhaḥ ||]

karuṇe striyā yathā—

‘ṇavari a pasāriaṃgī raabhariuppahapaïṇṇaveṇībaṃdhā | paḍiā urasaṃdāṇiamahialacakkalaï*atthaṇī jaṇaasuā 206’
[anantaraṃ ca prasāritāṅa‍gī rajobharitotpathaprakīrṇaveṇībandhā | patitoraḥsaṃdānitamahītalacakrīkṛtastanī janakasutā ||]

puṃso yathā—

‘*aṃtohuṃtaṃ ḍajjhaï jāāsuṇṇe dhare haliaütto | ukkhittaṇihāṇāiṃ va ramiaṭhṭhāṇāiṃ pecchaṃto* || 207 ||’
[antarabhimukhaṃ dahyate jāyāśūnye gṛhe hālikaputraḥ | utkṣiptanidhānānīva ramitasthānāni paśyan ||]

*evamanyā api ||

karuṇavarjaṃ striyā yathā—

‘saudhādudvijate tyajatyupavanaṃ dveṣṭi prabhāmaindavīṃ dvārāttrasyati citrakelisadaso* veṣaṃ viṣaṃ manyate | āste kevalamabjinīkisalayaprastāraśayyātale saṃkalpopanatatva*dākṛtirasāyattena cittena sā || 208 ||’
[page 632]

striyā eva prathamānurāgavarjaṃ yathā—

‘tiṣṭhaḥ dvāri bhavāṅa‍gaṇe vraja bahiḥ *sadmeti vartmekṣate śālāmañca tamaṅa‍gamañca valabhīmañceti veśmāñcati | dūtīṃ saṃdiśa saṃdiśeti bahuśaḥ saṃdiśya sāste tathā talpe kalpamayīva nirghṛṇa yathā nāntaṃ niśā gacchati 209’

prathamānurāgavarjaṃ puṃso yathā—

‘ramyaṃ dveṣṭiṃ pusa yathā prakṛtibhirna pratyahaṃ sevyate śayyo pāntavivartanaurviṃgamayatyunnidra eva kṣapāḥ | dākṣiṇyena dadāti vācamucitāmantaḥpurebhyo yadā gotreṣu skhalitastadā bhavati sa* vrīḍāvanamraściram 210’

puṃsa eva pravāsakaruṇayoryathā—

‘sītāveśma yato nirīkṣya harate dṛṣṭiṃ jhaṭityākulā manyonyārpitacañcudattakavalaiḥ pārāvatairdūyate* || indordūrata eva naśyati viśatyantargṛhaṃ duḥkhitaḥ pracchādyānanamañcalena rajanīpvastatrapaṃ roditi || 211 ||’

saṃbhogaceṣṭāsu pūrvānurāgāntare cumbanaṃ yathā—

‘āarapaṇāmioṭṭhaṃ aghaḍiaṇāsaṃ *asaghaḍiaṇilāḍam | *vaṇṇagghaalippamuhīa tīa pariuṃbaṃṇaṃ marimo || 212 ||’
[ādarapraṇāmitauṣṭhamaghaṭitanāsamasaṃghaṭitalalāṭam | varṇadhṛtaliptamukhyāstasyāḥ paricumbanaṃ smarāmaḥ ||]
[page 633]

atraivāliṅa‍ganaṃ yathā—

‘tāvamavaṇei ṇa tahā caṃdaṇapaṃko vi kāmimihuṇāṇam | jaha dūsahe vi* gimhe aṇṇoṇṇāliṃgaṇasuhellī* || 213 ||’
[tāpamapanayati na tathā candanapaṅa‍ko 'pi kābhimithunānām | yathā duḥsahe 'pi grīṣme 'nyonyāliṅa‍ganasukham ||]

mānānantare cumbanaṃ yathā—

‘jaha jaha se pariuṃbaï* maṇṇubhariāiṃ’ ṇihuvaṇe daïo | acchīiṃ uvari uvari taha taha bhiṇṇāiṃ vigalaṃti || 214 ||’
[yathā yathāsyāḥ paricumbati manyubharitāni nidhuvane dayitaḥ | akṣīṇyuparyupari tathā tathā bhinnāni vigalanti ||]

atraivāliṅa‍ganaṃ yathā—
