‘*māṇadumaparusapavaṇassa māmi savvaṃgaṇibbudiarassa | *uvaūhaṇassa bhaddaṃ raïṇāḍaapuvvaraṃgassa || 215 ||’
[mānadrumaparuṣapavanasya mātulāni sarvāṅa‍ganirvṛtikarasya | upagūhanasya bhadraṃ ratināṭakapūrvaraṅa‍gasya ||]

pravāsānantare* cumbanaṃ yathā—

‘kenacinmadhuramulbaṇarāgaṃ bāṣpataptamadhikaṃ viraheṣu | oṣṭhapallavamapāsya muhūrtaṃ subhruvaḥ sarasamakṣi cucumbe || 216 ||’

karuṇānantaramāliṅa‍ganaṃ yathā—

‘candrāpīḍaṃ sā ca jagrāha kaṇṭhe kaṇṭhasthānaṃ jīvitaṃ ca prapede | tenāpūrvāṃ sā samullāsalakṣmīminduṃ spṛṣṭa‍vā sindhuveleva bheje 217’
[page 634]

*prathamānurāgānantare dantakṣataṃ yathā—

‘ṇāsaṃ va sā kavole ajja vi tuha daṃtamaṃḍalaṃ bālā | ubbhiṇṇapulaabaī*veḍhaparigaaṃ rakkhaï varāī || 218 ||’
[nyāsamiva sā kapole 'dyāpi tava dantamaṇḍalaṃ bālā | udbhinnapulakavṛtiveṣṭaparigataṃ rakṣati varākī ||]

tadeva mānānantare yathā—

‘pavaṇuvvelliasāhuli* *ṭhaesu ṭhiadaṃtamaṃḍale ūrū | *caḍuāraaṃ païṃ mā hu putti *jaṇahāsiaṃ kuṇasu || 299 ||’
[pavanodvellitavastrāñcale sthagaya sthitadaṇḍamaṇḍale ūrū | caṭukārakaṃ patiṃ mā khalu putri janahasitaṃ kuru ||]

pravāsānantare dantakṣatādayo yathā—

‘daṃtakkhaaṃ kavole kaaggahuvvelio a dhammillo | *parighummirā a diṭṭhī piāgamaṃ sāhaï vahūe || 220 ||’
[dantakṣataṃ kapole kacagrahodvellitaśca dhammillaḥ | parighūrṇanaśīlā ca dṛṣṭiḥ priyāgamaṃ sādhayati vadhvāḥ ||]

*prathamānurāgānantare nakhakṣataṃ yathā—

‘ajjāi *ṇavaṇahakkhaaṇirikkhaṇe garuajovvaṇuttuṃgam | paḍimāgaaṇiaṇaaṇuppalacciaṃ* hoi thaṇavaṭṭham || 221 ||’
[āryāyā navanakhakṣatanirīkṣaṇe gurukayauvanottuṅa‍gam | pratimāgatanijanayanotpalārcitaṃ bhavati stanapṛṣṭham ||]
[page 635]

atraiva puruṣāyitaṃ yathā—

‘daravevirorujualāsu maüliacchīsu luliaciurāsu* | *purisāiasīrisu kāmo piāsu sajjāuho vasaï || 222 ||’
[īṣadvepanaśīloruyugalāsu mukulitākṣīṣu lulitacikurāsu | puruṣāyitaśīlāsu kāmaḥ priyāsu sajjāyudho vasati ||]

sarvaṃ sarvatra yathā—

‘poḍhamahilāṇaṃ jaṃ suṭṭhu sikkhiaṃ taṃ rae suhāvei* | *jaṃ jaṃ asikkhiaṃ ṇavavahūṇaṃ taṃ taṃ *dhiiṃ deṭṭha || 223 ||’
[prauḍhamahilānāṃ yatsuṣṭhu śikṣitaṃ tadrate sukhayati | yadyadaśikṣitaṃ navavadhūnāṃ tattaddhṛtiṃ dadāti ||]

vipralambhaparīṣṭiṣvabhiyogataḥ premaparīkṣā yathā—

‘haṃho kaṇṇullīṇā bhaṇāmi re suhaa kiṃ pi mā jūra* | ṇijjaṇapāraddhīsu* tue kahiṃ* vi puṇṇehiṃ laddhosi || 224 ||’
[haṃho karṇollīnā bhaṇāmi re subhaga kimapi mā khidyasva | nirjanarathyāsu tvaṃ kathamapi puṇyairlabdho 'si ||]

pratyabhiyogato yathā—

‘golāvisamoāracchaleṇa appā urammi se mukko | aṇuaṃpāṇiddosaṃ teṇa vi sā *gāḍhamuvaụ̄dhā || 225 ||’
[godāvarīviṣamāvatāracchalenātmā urasi tasya muktaḥ | anukampānirdoṣaṃ tenāpi sā gāḍhamupagụ̄dhā ||]
[page 636]

viṣahaṇena yathā—

‘ajja vi seaṃjalollaṃ pavvāi ṇa tīa haliasoṇhāe | phaggucchaṇa*cikkhi(kkha)llaṃ jaṃ taï diṇṇaṃ thaṇucchaṅa‍ge 226’
[adyāpi svedajalārdritaḥ pramlāyate na tasyā hālikasnuṣāyāḥ | phalgūtsavakardamo yastasyā dattāḥ stanotsaṅa‍ge ||]

vimarśena yathā—

‘tatto ccia ṇenti* kahā *viasaṃti tarhi *samappanti | kiṃ maṇṇe māucchā ekkajuāṇo imo gāmo || 227 ||’
[tata eva niryānti kathā vikasanti tatra tatra samāpyante | kiṃ manye mātṛṣvasaḥ ekayuvako 'yaṃ grāmaḥ ||]

bahumānena yathā—

‘teṇa ira ṇavalaāe diṇṇo paharo imīa thaṇavaṭṭhe | gāmataruṇīhiṃ ajja vi diahaṃ parivāliā bhamaï || 228 ||’
[tena kila dolāvilāse daktaḥ prahāra etasyāḥ stanapṛṣṭhe | grāmataruṇībhiradyāpi divasaṃ pratipālitā bhramati ||]

ślāghayā yathā—

‘sā taï sahatthadiṇṇaṃ phaggucchaṇakaddamaṃ thaṇucchaṃge | parikuviā iva* sāhaï *salāhirī gāmataruṇīṇam || 229 ||’
[sā tvayā svahastadattaṃ phalgūtsavakardamaṃ stanotsaṅa‍ge | parikupiteva sādhayati ślāghanaśīlā grāmataruṇīnām ||]
[page 637]

iṅgitena yathā—

‘jaï so ṇa *vallaha ccia ṇāmaggahaṇena tassa sahi kīsa | hoi muhaṃ te raviaraphaṃsavisaṭṭaṃ* va tāmarasam || 230 ||’
[yadi sa na vallabha eva nāmagrahaṇena tasya sakhi kimiti | bhavati mukhaṃ te ravikarasparśavikasitamiva tāmarasam ||]

dūtasaṃpreṣaṇena yathā—

‘seulliasavvaṃgī *ṇāmaggahaṇena tassa suhaassa | *dūiṃ *appāheṃtī tasse a gharaṃgaṇaṃ pattā || 231 ||’
[svedārdrīkṛtasarvāṅa‍gī nāmagrahaṇena tasya subhagasya | dūtīṃ saṃdiśantī tasyaiva gṛhāṅa‍gaṇaṃ prāptā ||]

*dūtapreśne yathā—

‘kaha ṇu gaā kaha diṭṭhā* kiṃ bhaṇiā kiṃ ca teṇa paḍivaṇṇaṃ* | eaṃ cia ṇa samappaï punaruttaṃ *jaṃpamāṇīe || 232 ||’
[kathaṃ nu gatā kathaṃ dṛṣṭā kiṃ bhaṇitā kiṃ ca tena pratipannam | evameva na samāpyate punaruktaṃ jalpamānāyāḥ ||]

lekhavidhānena yathā—

‘*vevirasiṇṇakaraṅa‍guli*pariggahakkhalialehaṇīmagge | sotthi ccia* ṇa samappaï piasahi lehammi kiṃ lihino || 233 ||’
[vepanaśīlasviṃnnakarāṅa‍guliparigrahaskhalitalekhanīmārge | svastyeva na samāpyate priyasakhi lekhe kiṃ likhāmaḥ ||]
[page 638]

lekhavācanena yathā—

‘prītyā svastipadaṃ vilokitavatī sthānaṃ stutaṃ* tuṣṭayā paścājjñātamanukrameṇa puratastattāvakaṃ nāmakam | tanvyā saṃmadanirbhareṇa manasā tadvācayantyā muhurna prāpto ghanabāṣpapūritadṛśā lekhe 'pi kaṇṭhagrahaḥ || 234 ||’

saṃbhogaparīṣṭiṣu prathamānurāgānantare sādhvasena puṃso yathā—

‘līlāio ṇiasaṇe rakkhiu taṃ rāhiāi thaṇavaṭṭhe | hariṇo paḍhamasamāgamasajjhasavasarehiṃ* veviro hattho || 235 ||’
[līlāyito nivasane rakṣatu tvāṃ rādhikāyāḥ stanapṛṣṭhe | hariṇaḥ prathamasamāgamasādhvasaprasarairvepanaśīlo hastaḥ ||]

atraiva dohadena mugdhāyā yathā—

‘kiṃ kiṃ de paḍihāsaï sahīhiṁ ia pucchiāi* muddhāiṁ | paḍhamullaadohaliṇīa* *ṇavari daïaṃ gaā diṭṭhī || 236 ||’
[kiṃ kiṃ te pratibhāsate sakhībhiriti pṛṣṭāyā mugdhāyāḥ | prathamodgatadohadinyāḥ kevalaṃ dayitaṃ gatā dṛṣṭiḥ ||]

atraiva pragalbhāyāḥ priyavākyavarṇanena* yathā—

‘huṃhuṃ *he bhaṇasu puṇo ṇa suaṃti karei kālavikkheaṃ | ghariṇī hiaamuhāiṃ païṇo kaṇṇe bhaṇaṃtassa || 237 ||’
[huṃhuṃ he bhaṇa punarna svapanti karoti kālavikṣepam | gṛhiṇī hṛdayasukhāni patyuḥ karṇe bhaṇataḥ ||]
[page 639]

mānānantare striyāḥ *kaitavasmaraṇena yathā—

‘bharimo se saaṇaparammuhīa vialaṃtamāṇapasarāe | *keavasuttuvvattaṇathaṇaharapellaṇasuhellim || 238 ||’
[smarāmastasyāḥ śayanaparāmukhyā vigalanmānaprasarāyāḥ | kaitavasuptodvartanastanabharapreraṇasukhakelim ||]

striyā eva sakhīvākyasyokṣepeṇa yathā—

‘bhiuḍīa* puloissaṃ ṇivbhacchissaṃ* parammuhī hossam | jaṃ bhaṇaha taṃ karissaṃ sahio jaï taṃ ṇa pecchissam 239’
[bhrakuṭyā pralokayiṣye nirbhartsye parāṅa‍makhībhaviṣyāmi | yadbhaṇata tatkariṣye sakhyo yadi taṃ na prekṣiṣye ||]

tasyā eva tadanuṣṭhānavighnena yathā—

‘granthimudgrathayituṃ hṛdayeśe vāsasaḥ spṛśati mānadhanāyāḥ | bhrūyugena sapadi pratipede romabhiśca samameva vibhedaḥ || 240 ||’

*pravāsānantaraṃ striyā yathā—

‘*acchakkāgaahiae bahuā *daïammi gurupurao | *jūraï vialaṃtāṇaṃ harisavisaṭṭāṇa* valaāṇam || 241 ||’
[akasmādāgatahṛdaye vadhūkā dayite gurupurataḥ | krudhyati vigalabhdyo harṣavikasabhdyo valayebhyaḥ||]
[page 640]

atraiva strīpuṃsayoryathā—

‘ramiūṇa *paammi gae (o)jāhe avaūhiuṃ paḍinivṛtto* | ahaaṃ *paütthapaïavva takkhaṇaṃ so pavāsivva || 242 ||’
[ratvā padamapi gato yadopagūhituṃ pratinivṛttaḥ | ahaṃ proṣitapatikeva tatkṣaṇaṃ sa pravāsīva ||]

sāmānyata eva pravāsasādhvasena striyā yathā—

‘hoṃtapahiassa jāā *āucchaṇajīaadhāraṇarahassam | pucchantīṃ bhamaï gharaṃ ghareṇa piavirahasahirīo* || 243 ||’
bhaviṣyatpathikasya jāyā āpṛcchanajīvadhāraṇarahasyam | pṛcchantī bhramati gṛhaṃ gṛheṇa priyavirahasahanaśīlāḥ ||]

*pravāsavilambena puṃso yathā—

‘ekko vi kālasāro ṇa dei gaṃtuṃ paāhiṇa valanto* | kiṃ uṇa bāhāuliaṃ loaṇajualaṃ miacchīe* || 244 ||’
[eko 'pi kṛṣṇasāro na dadāti gantu pradakṣiṇaṃ valan | kiṃ punarbāṣpākulitaṃ locanayugalaṃ mṛgākṣyāḥ ||]

parihāre svedādibhiḥ striyā yathā—

‘ullāaï se aṃgaṃ ūrū vevanti *kūvalo galaï | *ucchucchulei hiaaṃ piāame pupphavaïāi* || 245 ||’
[ārdrībhavatyasyā aṅa‍gamūrū vepete jaghanavasanaṃ galati | utkampate hṛdayaṃ priyāgame puṣpavatyāḥ ||]
[page 641]

karuṇānantaraṃ puṃso yathā—

‘*karasparśārambhātpulakitapṛthūrojakalaśe śramāmbho vāmārdhe vahati madanākūtasubhagam | vibhorvāraṃvāraṃ kṛta*samadhikoddhūlanavidhe- stanau bhasmasnānaṃ kathamapi samāptaṃ vijayate || 246 ||’

vipralambhaniruktiṣu prathamānurāge pratiśrutyādānaṃ yathā—

‘*kiṃ bhaṇiosi ṇa vālaa gāmaṇidhūāi* guruaṇasamakkham | *aṇimisavaṃkavalaṃtaaāṇaṇa*ṇaaṇaddhadiṭṭhehiṃ || 247 ||’
[kiṃ bhaṇito 'si na bālaka grāmaṇīduhitrā gurujanasamakṣam | animiṣavakravaladānananayanārdhadṛṣṭaiḥ ||]

atra *vakrekṣitādibhiḥ pratiśrutyāliṅa‍ganādayo hrībhayādibhirna dīyante || māne visaṃvādanaṃ yathā—

‘aṇṇua ṇāhaṃ kuviā uvaūhasu* kiṃ muhā pasāemi | tuha maṇṇusamuppaṇṇeṇa majjha māṇeṇa* viṇa kajjam || 248 ||’
[ajña nāhaṃ kupitā upagūhasva kiṃ mudhā prasādayāmi | tava manyusamutpannena mama mānenāpi na kāryam ||]

atra māninī pūrvamāliṅa‍ganādīnniṣidhya paścādayathāvatprayacchati yathā kaścidaṣṭau *śatāni pradāsyāmīti pratiśrutyāṣṭabhira*dhikaṃ śataṃ praya-[page 642]cchati na tvaṣṭau śatānīti | tadetavdyalīka*vipriyādibhirāliṅa‍ganādīnāṃ nirākaraṇamayathāvatpradānatvādvisaṃvādanamevocyate ||

pravāse kālaharaṇaṃ yathā—

‘*ehii so vi* paüttho *ahaaṃ kuppejja so vi* aṇuṇejja | *ia kassa vi phalaï *maṇorahāṇaṁ mālā piaamammi || 249 ||’
[eṣyati so 'pi proṣito 'haṃ kupiṣyāmi so 'pyanuneṣyati | iti kasyāpi phalati manorathānāṃ mālā priyatame ||]

atrāliṅa‍ganādīnāṃ vyaktaiva kālaharaṇapratītiḥ ||

karuṇe pratyādānaṃ yathā—

‘*samasokkhadukkhaparivaḍ̣dhiāṇaṁ kāleṇa rūḍhapemmāṇaṃ* | *mihuṇāṇaṁ maraï jaṃ taṃ khu jiaï iaraṃ muaṃ hoi || 250 ||’
[samasaukhyaduḥkhaparivardhitayoḥ kālena rūḍhapremṇoḥ | mithunayormriyate yattatkhalu jīvatītaranmṛtaṃ bhavati ||]

atra—

‘suhṛdiva prakaṭayya sukhapradaḥ prathamamekarasāmanukūlatām | punarakāṇḍavivartanadāruṇaḥ *praviśinaṣṭi vidhirmanaso rujam 251’

ityayamarthaḥ saṃbadhyate | tasya ca pratyādānamevārtho bhavati ||

[page 643]

prathamānurāge *vañcanamātraṃ vividhaṃ yathā—

‘diṭṭhāi* jaṃ ṇa diṭṭho* ālaviāe vi jaṃ ṇa ālatto | uvaāro jaṃ ṇa kao taṃ cia* kaliaṃ chaïllehiṃ || 252 ||’
[dṛṣṭayā yanna dṛṣṭa ālapitayā yannālāpitaḥ | upakāro yanna kṛtastadeva kalitaṃ vidagdhaiḥ ||]

atra vrīḍādibhi*radarśanādibhirvañca*nādibhirvaividhyaṃ pratīyate ||

māne viruddhaṃ yathā—

‘ṇa muaṃti *dīhasāse ṇa ruaṃti *ṇa honti virahakisiā o | dhaṇṇāŏ tāŏ jāṇaṃ bahuvallaha vallaho ṇa tumam || 253 ||’
[na muñcanti dīrghaśvāsān na rudanti na bhavanti virahakṛśāḥ | dhanyāstā yāsāṃ bahuvallabha vallabho na tvam ||]

atrerṣyāyitādibhirvallabhāliṅa‍ganādiviruddhairmānavatī vañcyate ||

pravāse vyāviddhaṃ yathā—

‘kaïā gao pio ajja putti ajjeṇa kaï diṇā hoṃti | ekko eddahamette *bhaṇie mohaṃ gaā kuṃvarī* || 254 ||’
[kadā gataḥ priyo 'dya putri adyeti kati dināni bhavanti | eka etāvanmātre bhaṇite mohaṃ gatā kumārī ||]

atraikasyāpi divasasya *varṣāyamāṇatayā *viśeṣato dairghyaṃ pratīyate ||

[page 644]

karuṇe niṣiddhaṃ yathā—

‘āvāabhaaaraṃ cia* ṇa hoi dukkhassa dāruṇaṃ *ṇivvahaṇam | ṇāha jiantīa mae diṭṭhaṃ sahiaṃ a tuha imaṃ avasāṇam ||’
[āpātabhayaṃkarameva na bhavati duḥkhasya dāruṇaṃ nirvahaṇam | nātha jīvantyā mayā dṛṣṭaṃ soḍhaṃ ca tavedamavasānam ||]

tadetadrāmaviṣaye sītāyāścirāśaṃsitasamāgamasukhāvāptivyapāyarūpaṃ vacanaṃ karuṇe niṣidhyate ||

prathamānurāgeṇa saha rāgo yathā—

‘sā mahaï tassa ṇhāuṃ aṇusotte sovi se samuvvahaï | thaṇavaṭṭabhiḍaṇaviluliakallolamahagghie salile || 256 ||’
[sā vāñchati tasya snātumanusrotasi so 'pyasyāḥ samudvahati | stanapṛṣṭamilanavilulitakallolamahārghite salile ||]

atra dvayorapyekakālamanyo 'nyānurāgaḥ pratīyate tatraikā lāvaṇyādinā rajyate 'nyaḥ snehādineti ||

tatraiva paścādyathā—

‘māmi hiaaṃ va pīaṃ teṇa juāṇeṇa majjamāṇāe* | ṇhāṇahaliddā*kaḍuaṃ aṇusottajalaṃ piaṃteṇa || 257 ||’
[mātulāni hṛdayameva pītaṃ tena yūnā majjamānāyāḥ | snānaharidrākaṭukamanusrotojalaṃ pibatā ||]

atraikasyānurāgaṃ dṛṣṭa‍vā paścāddvitīyo rajyate ||

[page 645]

tatraivānurūpo* yathā—

‘saccaṃ jāṇaï daṭa‍ṭhuṃ sarisammi jaṇammi jujjae rāo | maraü ṇa tumaṃ bhaṇisyaṃ maraṇaṃ vi* salāhaṇijjaṃ se || 258 ||’
[satyaṃ jānāti draṣṭuṃ sadṛśe jane yujyate rāgaḥ | mriyatāṃ na tvāṃ bhaṇiṣyāmi maraṇamapi ślāghanīyamasyāḥ ||]

atra na kevalaṃ lāvaṇyādinaiva rajyate kiṃ tarhyanurūpaviṣayiṇābhilāṣeṇāpīti pratīyate ||

tatraivānugato yathā—

‘gahavaïsueṇa samaaṃ saccaṃ aliaṃ va kiṃ viāreṇa* | dhaṇṇāi haliakumāriāi* jaṇammi jaṇavāo* || 259 ||’
[gṛhapatisutena samakaṃ satyamalīkaṃ vā kiṃ vicāreṇa | dhanyāyā hālikakumārikāyā jane janavādaḥ ||]

atra yadyapi saubhāgyādiprasiddhikṛtasārūpyaṃ* na vidyate tathāpi striyā uttamaprārthanamagarhitatvādanugatameva bhavati | so 'yaṃ *karaṇasādhanotpattipakṣe uktaḥ | bhāvasādhanapakṣe tu sahārthādiviśiṣṭā ratirdīptirvānurāgaśabdenocyate | *prathamaṃ copajāyamānatvādayaṃ prathamānurāga iti *prathate ||

māne *mānyate yeneti yathā—

‘pāapaḍaṇāṇaṁ muddhe rahasavalāmoḍia*cciavvāṇam | daṃsaṇametta*pasijjiri cukkā *bahuāṇa sokkhāṇaṁ || 260 ||’
[page 646]
[pādapatanānāṃ mugdhe rabhasabalātkṛtārcitavyānām | darśanamātraprasādanaśīle bhraṣṭā bahūnāṃ saukhyānām ||]

atra 'māna pūjāyām’ iti dhātoḥ *svārthikaṇijantāṇṇici ghañi ca māna iti rūpam | *sa hi preyāṃsamasyāḥ pādapatanādipūjāyāṃ prayojayati ||

yaṃ priyatvena manyate yathā—

‘kāraṇagahio vi mae māṇo emea jaṃ samosario | atthakkapphulla*aṃkolla tujjha taṃ matthae paḍaü || 261 ||’
[kāraṇagṛhīto 'pi mayā māna evameva yatsamupasṛtaḥ | akasmātphullitāṅa‍kolla tava tanmastake patatu ||]

atra ‘mana jñāne’ iti dhātuḥ | tathā hi mānaṃ priyatvena manyamānā tadapahāriṇe 'ṅa‍kollāya kāpi māninī *kupyati ||

yaḥ prema manute yathā—

‘jattha ṇa ujjāgarao jattha ṇa īsāvisūraṇaṃ māṇam | *sabbhāvacāṭuaṃ jattha ṇatthi ṇeho tahiṃ ṇatthi || 262 ||’
[yatra nāstyujjāgarako yatra nerṣyākhedī mānaḥ | sadbhāvacāṭukaṃ yatra nāsti snehastatra nāsti ||]

atra 'manu avabodhane’ iti dhātuḥ | mānena hi janaḥ premāsti nāsti veti budhyate* | tasya ca karaṇabhūtasyāpi prādhānyādatra kartṛtvopacāraḥ | tadyathā 'prajñā paśyati no cakṣurdṛṣṭiḥ sārasvatī hi sā |’ iti ||

[page 647]

prema mimīte yathā—

‘*kuviā a saccahāmā* same vi bahuāṇa ṇavara māṇakkhalaṇe | pāaḍiahiaasāro pemmāsaṃghasariso paaṭṭaï maṇṇū || 263 ||’
[kupitā ca satyabhāmā same 'pi bandhūnāṃ kevalaṃ mānaskhalane | prakaṭitahṛdayasāraḥ premāśvāsasadṛśaḥ pravartate manyuḥ ||]

atra ‘māṅ māne’ iti dhātoḥ ‘kṛtyalyuṭo bahulam 3|3|113’ iti kartari lyuṭ | ‘ko 'sāvanumāna’ iti bhāṣyaprayogāt | tena ca yadyapi karaṇabhūtenaivātmani rukmiṇyāṃ ca priyapremṇaḥ parimāṇaṃ satyabhāmā pratyāyayati tathāpi pūrvavadihāpyayaṃ *pūrvavatkartṛtvenopacaryate ||

pravāse vasata ityupalakṣaṇenātmānamaṅa‍ganā na bhūṣayanti* yathā—

‘sāhīṇe vi piaame patte vi khaṇe ṇa maṇḍio appā | *dukkhiapaütthavaïaṃ saajjiaṃ* saṃṭhavaṃtīe || 264 ||’
[svādhīne 'pi priyatame prāpte 'pi kṣaṇe na maṇḍita ātmā | duḥkhitaproṣitapatikāṃ prativeśinīṃ saṃsthāpayantyā ||]

atra ‘vasa ācchādane’ ityasya 'prasmarati’ ityādivanniṣedhārthakaprapūrvasya *ghañi *pravāsa iti rūpaṃ nirūpyate ||

yuvānaḥ priyāsaṃnidhau na vasanti yathā—

‘virahāṇalo sahijjaï āsābaṃdheṇa vallahajaṇassa* | ekkaggāmapavāso māe maraṇaṃ visesei || 265 ||’
[virahānalaḥ sahyata āśābandhena vallabhajanasya | ekagrāmapravāso mātarmaraṇaṃ viśeṣayati ||]
[page 648]

atra dūrasthayorivāntikasthayorapi saṃnikarṣābhāvātpravāso bhavati ||

utkaṇṭhādibhiśceto vāsayati yathā—

‘āloaṃta* disāo sasaṃta jaṃbhaṃta* gaṃta roanta | *mujjhaṃta *paḍaṃta hasaṃta pahia kiṃ te paüttheṇa || 266 ||’
[ālokayan diśaḥ śvasan jṛmbhamāṇo gāyan rudan | muhyan patan hasan pathika kiṃ tena proṣitena ||]

atrotkaṇṭhādibhirvāsite* cetasi śūnyāvalokanādayo 'nubhāvā jāyante ||

pramāpayati yathā—

‘saṃjīvaṇosahimmiva* suassa* rakkhaï aṇaṇṇavāvārā | sāsū ṇavambhadaṃsaṇakaṃṭhāgaajīviaṃ soṇham || 267 ||’
[saṃjīvanauṣadhimiva sutasya rakṣatyananyavyāpārā | śvaśrūrnavābhradarśanakaṇṭhāgatajīvitāṃ snuṣām ||]

atra prasādaṃ karotītyādivatpramāpaṇopakramo 'pi pramāpaṇamucyate ||

karuṇe *karoterbhūtopādanārthatve kurute mūrcchāṃ yathā—

‘*vialiavioaviaṇaṃ takkhaṇa*pabbhaṭṭharāmamaraṇāāsam | jaṇaataṇaāi ṇavaraṃ laddhaṃ mucchāṇimīliacchīa suhaṃ 268’
[vigalitaviyogavedanaṃ tatkṣaṇaprabhraṣṭarāmamaraṇāyāsam | janakatanayayā kevalaṃ labdhaṃ mūrcchānimīlitākṣyā sukham ||]

atra sītāyāḥ patiśokaprakarṣeṇābhūtā* mūrcchotpadyate ||

[page 649]

uccāraṇārthatve kurute vilāpaṃ yathā—

‘puhavīa *hohii paī bahupurisavisesacaṃcalā rāasirī | kaha tā mahaccia* imaṃ ṇīsāmaṇṇaṃ *uvaṭhṭhiaṃ vehavvam || 269 ||’
[pṛthivyā bhaviṣyati patirbahupurūṣaviśeṣacañcalā rājyalakṣmīḥ | kathaṃ tanmamaivedaṃ niḥsāmānyamupasthitaṃ vaidhavyam ||]

*atra rāmaduḥkhena vilapantī *sītedamuccarati ||

*avasthāpanārthe kurute sāhase mano yathā—

‘*iyametya pataṅa‍gavartmanā punaraṅa‍kāśrayiṇī bhavāmi te | caturaiḥ surakāminījanaiḥ priya yāvanna *vilupyase divi || 270 ||’

atra rateḥ kāmaśokena maraṇasāhase mano 'vasthāpyate ||

abhyañjanārthatve karoti cittaṃ duḥkhena yathā—

‘dalati hṛdayaṃ gạ̄dhodvegaṃ dvidhā* tu na bhidyate* vahati vikalaḥ kāyo mohaṃ na muñcati cetanām | jvalayati tanūmantardāhaḥ karoti na bhasmasāt praharati vidhirmarmacchedī na kṛntati jīvitam || 271 ||’

atra *rāmāderduḥkhena cittamabhyajyate ||

saṃbhoganiruktiṣu prathamānurāgānantare pālanārtho* yathā—

‘dṛṣṭā dṛṣṭimadho dadāti kurute nālāpamābhāṣitā śayyāyāṃ parivṛtya tiṣṭhati balādāliṅgitā vepate | [page 650] niryāntīṣu sakhīṣu vāsabhavanānnirgantumevehate bālā vāmatayaiva *saṃprati mama prītyai navọdhā priyā || 272 ||’

atrāprāgalbhyavāmatābhyāmanukūlāyāmapi navọdhāyāmicchānuvṛttyā ratiḥ pālyate ||

mānānantare kauṭilyārtho yathā—

‘pāde mūrdhani tāmratāmupagate karṇotpale cūrṇite chinne hāralatāguṇe karatale saṃpātajātavraṇe | aprāptapriyatāḍanavyatikarā hantuṃ punaḥ kopitā vāñchantī muhureṇaśāvanayanā paryākulā* roditi || 273 ||’

atra premṇaḥ svabhāvakuṭilatvānmānavatyāḥ kacagrahaṇena yatpādatāḍanādirūpāḥ kuṭilā* eva saṃbhogā jāyante ||

pravāsānantare 'bhyavahārārtho yathā—

‘vasiṣṭhadhenoranuyāyinaṃ tamāvartamānaṃ vanitā vanāntāt | papau nimeṣālasapakṣmapaṅktirupoṣitābhyāmiva locanābhyām || 274 ||’

atra *uttarārdhenopoṣitasyānnopayoga iva priyālokajanmā pibaterabhyavahāraḥ *kathyate ||

karuṇānantare 'nubhavārtho yathā—

‘aṇumaraṇapatthiāe paccāgaajīvie* piaamammi | vehavvamaṃḍaṇaṃ kulavahūa sohaggaaṃ jāam || 275 ||’
[anumaraṇaprasthitāyāḥ pratyāgatajīvite priyatame | vaidhavyamaṇḍanaṃ kulavadhvāḥ saubhāgyakaṃ jātam ||]
[page 651]

atra yatheyaṃ matprāṇabhūtaivamasyā ahamapi jīvitameveti patyā visrambhajo 'nurāgaḥ* patnyāḥ punaḥ pretyāpi yatsaṃgamo mayābhilaṣitaḥ so 'yaṃ jīvantyaiva jīviteśvaraḥ samāsādita iti visrambhādatisukhamevānubhūyate ||

atra prathamānurāgānantare saṃbhogaḥ saṃkṣipto yathā—

‘apetavyāhāraṃ *dhutavividhaśilpavyatikaraṃ *karasparśārambhapragalitadukūlāntaśayanam | muhurbaddhotkampaṃ diśi diśi muhuḥ preritadṛśo- rahalyāsutrāmṇoḥ kṣaṇikamiha tatsaṃgatamabhūt || 276 ||’

atra saṃkṣepo nigadenaiva vyākhyāyate ||

sa eva mānānantare saṃkīrṇo yathā—

‘aṇuṇiakhaṇaladdhasuhe puṇo vi saṃbhariamaṇṇudūmiavihale* | hiae māṇavaīṇaṃ cireṇa *paṇaagaruo pasammaī roso 277’
[anunītakṣaṇalabdhasukhe punarapi saṃsmṛtamanyudūnitavihvale | hṛdaye mānavatīnāṃ cireṇa praṇayagurukaḥ praśāmyati roṣaḥ ||]

atrāvasthitā prakṛṣṭā ca ratirvyalīkasmaraṇādibhiḥ saṃkīryate ||

pravāsānantare saṃpūrṇo* yathā—

‘śāpānto me bhujagaśayanādutthite śārṅgapāṇau māsānetāngamaya* caturo locane mīlayitvā | paścādāvāṃ virahaguṇitaṃ taṃ tamātmābhilāṣaṃ nirvekṣyāvaḥ pariṇataśaraccandrikāsu kṣapāsu || 278 ||’
[page 652]

atrāmunā virahivākyenāpi nirvekṣyāva iti bhaviṣyatkālopādheḥ *pravāsānantare 'pyavirudhyamānena taṃ tamātmābhilāṣamityādinā tadānīntanasaṃbhogasya* saṃpūrṇatvaṃ varṇyate ||

karuṇānantare samṛddho yathā—

‘tīrthe toyavyatikarabhave jahnukanyāsarayvordehatyāgādamaragaṇanālekhyamāsādya sadyaḥ | pūrvākārādhikatararucā* saṃgataḥ kāntayāsau līlāgāreṣvaramata punarnandanābhyantareṣu || 279 ||’

atrottarārdhenendumatyajayorlokāntarapratyujjīvanena saṃbhogasamṛddhiḥ pratipādyate ||

prathamānurāgānantare sahārthānvayo yathā—

‘muhapecchao paī se *sāvi hu piarūadaṃsaṇummaïā | do vi kaatthā puhaviṃ* *apurisamahilaṃ tti maṇṇaṃti || 280 ||’
[mukhaprekṣakaḥ patistasyāḥ sāpi khalu priyarūpadarśanonmattā | dvāvapi kṛtārthau pṛthivīmapuruṣamahileti manyete ||]

atra pūrvārdhe rañjayatyartha uttarārdhe rājatyarthaḥ prathamānurāge saha *bhāvena siddhastadanantare 'pi tathaivānuvartate ||

tatraiva paścādarthānvayo yathā—

‘adya prabhṛtyavanatāṅgi tavāsmi dāsaḥ krītastapobhiriti vādini candramaulau | [page 653] ahvāya sā niyamajaṃ klamamutsasarja kleśaḥ phalena hi punarnavatāṃ vidhatte || 281 ||’

atra rañjayatyarthaḥ prathamānurāge puṃsi paścādbhāvena siddhastadanantare 'pi tathaivānuvartate ||

atraivānurūpārthānvayo yathā—

‘śaśinamupagateyaṃ kaumudī meghamuktaṃ jalanidhimanurūpaṃ jahnukanyāvatīrṇā | iti samaguṇayogaprītayastatra paurāḥ śravaṇakaṭu nṛpāṇāmekavākyaṃ vivavruḥ || 282 ||’

atra rājatyarthaḥ prathamānurāge strīpuṃsayorapyānurūpyeṇa siddhastadanantare 'pi tathaivānuvartate ||

tatraivānugatārthānvayo yathā—

‘sthāne tapo duścarametadarthamaparṇayā pelavayābhitaptam* | yā dāsyamapyasya labheta nārī sā syātkṛtārtha kimutāṅa‍kaśayyām || 283 ||’

atra pūrvārdhe rañjayatyarthaḥ *prathamānurāge 'nugatārthatvena siddhastadanantare tathaivānuvartate | so 'yaṃ *karaṇasādhanaḥ pratyayotpattipakṣa uktaḥ | bhāvasādhanapakṣe tu sarvatra sahārthādiviśiṣṭā ratirdīptirvānurāgaśabdenocyamānā tadanantare 'pi samāsasāmarthyādanuvartate | kaḥ punaratra samāsaḥ | ṣaṣṭhīlakṣaṇastatpuruṣaḥ | prathamānurāgasyānantaraḥ* prathamānurāgānantara iti | kā ca vṛttiḥ | ajahatsvārthā na hyatra nāyakau mithaḥ samāgatāvapi prathamānurāgamutsṛjataḥ | yuktaṃ punaryadajahatsvārthā parārthābhidhānarūpā vṛttiḥ syāt, [page 654]avaśyaṃ hyanena parasyārthamabhidadhātā svārtha utsraṣṭavyaḥ | bāḍhaṃ yuktam | evaṃ hi dṛśyate loke bhikṣuko dvitīyā* bhikṣāmāsādya pūrvāṃ na jahāti saṃcayāyaiva yatate, evaṃ tārhi dvayordvivacanamiti dvivacanaṃ prāpnoti | kasyā vibhakteḥ | ṣaṣṭhyāḥ | na ṣaṣṭhīsamartho 'nantaraḥ | tarhi prathamāyāḥ | na prathamāsamarthaḥ prathamānurāgaḥ saṃbandhādhikyāt | abhihitaḥ so 'rtho 'nantarbhūtaḥ* prātipadikārthaḥ saṃpanna iti sāmarthyaṃ bhaviṣyati | maivam | iha prathamānurāgānantara *ityetasmātsamudāyādvibhaktyā utpattavyam | tena ca samudāyenaiko 'rthapiṇḍo* mṛtpiṇḍa ivāvibhāgāpanna*pāṃsūdakavibhāgo 'vayavārthaśaktyānugṛhītaḥ pṛthagavyapadeśyāvayavaśaktirabhidhīyate | tasmiṃśca samudāyārtha ekatvaṃ samavetamato vidyamānāyāmapyavayavasaṃkhyāyāṃ tadāśrayā subutpattirna bhaviṣyati ||

mānānantare pūjārthānvayo yathā—

‘na spṛṣṭo 'pi tridaśasaritā dūramīrpyānubandhā- nnāpyunmṛṣṭo* bhujagapatinā tarjanābhirjayāyāḥ | mānasyānte nayanasalilaiḥ kṣālitaḥ śailaputryā patyurmaulau natiyuji jayatyātmanaḥ pādapāṃsuḥ || 284 ||’

atra pādapatanādipūjā mānasiddhā tadanantare 'pyanuvartate ||

atraiva mānaṃ prati priyatvābhimānārthānvayo* yathā—

‘vihāyaitanmānavyasanamanayoruccakucayo- rnidheyaḥ* preyāṃste yadi vayamanullaṅghyavacasaḥ | [page 655] sakhībhyaḥ snigdhābhyo *giramiti niśamyaiṇanayanā nivāpāmbho datte nayanasalilairmānasuhṛde || 285 ||’

atra mānaṃ prati priyatvābhimāno mānānantare 'pyanuvartate ||

atraiva premāvarodhārthānvayo yathā—

‘dūmeṃti je muhuttaṃ kuviaṃ dāsavva je* pasāeṃti* | te ccia mahilāṇa piā sesā sāmi ccia varāā* 286’
[dūnayanti ye muhurtaṃ kupitāṃ dāsā iva ye prasādayanti | ta eva mahilānāṃ priyāḥ śeṣāḥ svāmina eva varākāḥ ||]

atrāsyāmapi premāsti *nāsti veti jijñāsuḥ *priyaḥ priyāṃ kelīgotraskhalanādinā dunoti | sā ca premavatyavaśyamasmai kupyati | sa copalabdhapremā *dāsavadenāṃ prasādayati | athaiṣātmani premāstitvamavabudhyate* | so 'yaṃ mānasiddho 'rthastadanantare 'pyanuvartate ||

tatraiva premapramāṇārthānvayo* yathā—

‘surakusumehiṃ kalusiaṃ jaï tehiṃ cia puṇo pasāemi tumaṃ | to pemmassa kisoari avarāhassaṃ a ṇa me kaaṃ aṇurūaṃ* 287’
[surakusumaiḥ kaluṣitāṃ yadi taireva punaḥ prasādayāmi tvām | tataḥ premṇaḥ kṛśodari aparādhasya ca na me kṛtamanurūpam ||]

atra rukmiṇyāḥ surakusumamañjarī dattā mama tu suratarureva preyasā pratipannastadahamasyāḥ *sahasraguṇatvena priyatameti satyabhāmā svapremāṇaṃ-[page 656]mimīte* | sa cāyamartho *mānena siddhastadanantare 'pi samāsamāmarthyādanuvartate | kaḥ punaratra samāsaḥ | ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣa eva | kā vṛttiḥ | *prathamānurāgānantaravadajahatsvārthaiva | yuktaṃ tatra visrambhaṇādāvapi prathamānurāgasya vidyamānatvāt | iha tu mānanivṛttau mānāpagamādayo jāyante | anvayādviśeṣaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | tadyathā—ghṛtaghaṭastailaghaṭa iti niṣikte 'pi ghṛte taile vā ghṛtaghaṭo 'yaṃ* tailaghaṭo 'yamityanvayātpūrvapadārtho viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati | *bhavati tatra yā ca yāvatī *cārthamātrā ihāpi tattulyameva ||

tathā hi—

‘sakaaggahataṃsuṇṇāmiāṇaṇā* piaï piaamaviiṇṇam* | *thoaṃ thoaṃ rososadhaṃ* va māṇaṃsiṇa* maïram || 288 ||’
[sakacagrahatrastāvanāmitānanā pibati priyatamavitīrṇam | stokaṃ stokaṃ roṣauṣadhamiva māninī madirām ||]

sakaṣāyaireva vākyairnāyakaṃ nistudantī śayanīyaṃ gacchediti mānaśeṣānvayo dṛśyate ||

pravāsānantare priyā na vasata ityarthasyānvayo yathā—

‘vasane paridhūsare vasānā *niyamakṣāmatanuḥ kṛtaikaveṇiḥ | atiniṣkaruṇasya śuddhaśīlā mama dīrghaṃ virahavrataṃ* bibharti 289’
[page 657]

atra duṣyantena śakuntalāyāḥ pravāse vibhūṣaṇādyagrahaṇaṃ yadavagataṃ *tattadanantare 'pyanuvartamānaṃ premaprakarṣāya bhavati ||

tatraiva* yuvānaḥ priyasaṃnidhau na vasantītyarthasyānvayo yathā—

‘samarthaye yatprathamaṃ priyāṃ prati kṣaṇena tanme parivartate 'nyathā | ato vinidre sahasā vilocane karomi na sparśavibhāvitāpriyaḥ* 290’

atra purūravāḥ pravāsānmatta urvaśībudhdyā latādikaṃ *yadyadāsasāda *tattadānekaśo 'nyathā babhūva | *tatsaṃskārāccāyaṃ yasyā latārūpaparivartanaṃ pratyeti so 'yaṃ priyāsaṃnidhau yūnāmavāsaḥ* saṃsiddhastadanantare 'pyanuvartate ||

atraivotkaṇṭhādibhiśceto vāsayatītyarthasyānvayo yathā—

‘*abbo dukkaraāraa puṇo vi tartti karesi gamaṇassa | ajja vi ṇa hoṃti saralā veṇīa taraṃgiṇo ciurā* 291’
[he duṣkarakāraka punarapi cintāṃ karoṣi gamanasya | adyāpi na bhavanti saralā veṇyāstaraṅgiṇaścikurāḥ ||]

atra *pravāsānubhūtabhṛśotkaṇṭhādicittavāsanāḥ* pravāsānantare 'pi tasyā *nopaśāmyantīti veṇikāvarṇanādinā sūcyate ||

atraiva pramāpayatītyarthasyānvayo yathā—

‘tvadviyogodbhave caṇḍi mayā tamasi majjatā | diṣṭyā pratyupalabdhāsi cetaneva gatāsunā || 292 ||’
[page 658]

atrorvaśī*virahātpurūravā uttarāṃ *kāmāvasthāṃ prapannaḥ priyāprāptau pretyeva pratyujjīvitastadevānusaṃdhatte | so 'yaṃ pramāpaṇārthaḥ pravāsasiddhastadanantare 'pi samāsasāmarthyādanuvartate | kaḥ punaratra samāsaḥ | ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣa eva | kā vṛttiḥ* | na tāvadanutsṛṣṭasvārthā, nahi proṣyasamāgatayoḥ pravāsasaṃbandho 'pi vidyate | utsṛṣṭasvārthā tadiha bhavatu | yuktaṃ punaryadutsṛṣṭasvārthā nāma vṛttiḥ syāt | bāḍhaṃ yuktam | evaṃ hi dṛśyate lokepuruṣo 'yaṃ parakarmaṇi pravartamānaḥ svakarmotsṛjati | tadyathā takṣā rājakarmaṇi pravartamānastakṣakarmotsṛjati | nanvevaṃ sati rājapuruṣamānayetyukte puruṣamātrasyānayanaṃ prāpnoti | naiṣa doṣaḥ | utsṛjannapyayaṃ svārthaṃ nātyantāyotsṛjati, yaḥ parārthavirodhī svārthastamevotsṛjati | tadyathā takṣā rājakarmaṇi pravartamānastakṣakarmotsṛjati na tu sthitavihasitakampitādīni | na cāyamarthaḥ parārthavirodhī viśeṣaṇaṃ nāma | tasmānnotsrakṣyati ||

karuṇānantare 'nubhūta*prādurbhāvānvayārtho yathā—

‘jayanti jāyāśliṣṭasya śambhorambhodhimanthane | magnāmṛtaviṣāsvādamadamūrcchā manomudaḥ || 293 ||’

atra *dākṣāyaṇyā haimavatītvena karuṇānantaratvam | tatra karuṇaduḥkhena mūrcchādayaḥ prādurāsan | iha tvānandena te prādurbhavanti ||

tatraivoccāraṇānvayārtho yathā—

‘klāmyantī yadupekṣitāsi purataḥ kāmo yadagre hataḥ kliṣṭaṃ yattapasā vapuryadapi ca proktā baṭucchadmanā | tatsarvaṃ praṇatasya me 'dya dayite dākṣāyaṇi kṣamyatāmityuktvā caraṇābjayorvijayate *luṇṭhañchivāyāḥ śivaḥ 294’
[page 659]

atra karuṇāvasthāyāṃ priyāpādābjayorluṇṭhatā śokena yo vilāpaḥ kṛtaḥ sa iha prakarṣālāpatvena *vipariṇamati ||

atraiva mano 'vasthāpanānvayārtho yathā—

‘akhaṇḍitaṃ prema labhasva patyurityucyate tābhirumā sma namrā | tayā tu tasyārdhaśarīralābhādadhaḥkṛtāḥ snigdhajanāśiṣo 'pi 295’

atraiva—

‘yadaiva pūrvaṃ jvalane śarīraṃ *sā dakṣaroṣātsudatī sasarja | tataḥprabhṛtyeva vimuktasaṅa‍gaḥ patiḥ paśūnāmaparigraho 'bhūt || 296 ||’

iti karuṇāvasthāyāmatisnehenāparigrahatvasāhase yanmano 'vasthāpitaṃ tadihārdhaśarīrapradānamahāsāhasamevāvatiṣṭhate ||

tatraivābhyañjanānvayārtho yathā—

‘bhinna sadyaḥ samādhāvuparamati parajyotiṣi spandasaṃjñe saṃjñāmāpadyamāne mṛdumanasi manāgunmiṣatsvindriyeṣu | vyāpāre pāravaśyaṃ visṛjati maruti brahmasabrahmacārī vāmārdhasparśajanmā jayati purariporantarānandapūraḥ || 297 ||’

atra yatkaruṇāvasthāyāṃ manaḥ śokaprakarṣeṇābhyaktamāsīttadiha priyāśleṣajanmānā paramānandenābhyajyate | so 'yaṃ *karuṇadharmānvayastadanantare 'pi samāsasāmarthyādbhavati | kaḥ punaratra samāsaḥ | ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣa eva | kā vṛttiḥ | jahatsvārthā | na hyatra karuṇārthasya gandho 'pi | kathaṃ tarhyanvayaḥ | yathā mallikāpuṭaḥ campakapuṭa ityatra *niḥkīrṇāsvapi sumanaḥsu mallikādirvāsanāvaśādviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati—ayaṃ mallikāpuṭo 'yaṃ campakapuṭa iti, evaṃ [page 660]nivṛtte 'pi svārthe vāsanāvaśātkaruṇo 'nantarasya viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati | astu vā prathamānurāgādiṣvapi jahatsvārthaiva vṛttiḥ | nanvevaṃ rājapuruṣamānayetyukte puruṣamātrasyānayanaṃ prāpnoti | naiṣa doṣaḥ | vṛttau samarthādhikāraḥ kriyate | sāmarthyaṃ ca bhedaḥ saṃsarga ubhayaṃ vā | tatra rājña ityukte *sarvaṃ svaṃ prasaktam | puruṣa ityukte sarvaḥ svāmī prasaktaḥ | ihedānīṃ rājapuruṣamānayetyukte rājā purūṣaṃ nivartayatyanyebhyaḥ svāmibhyaḥ;puruṣo 'pi rājānamanyebhyaḥ svebhyaḥ* | evamasminnubhayato vyavacchinne yadi rājārtho nivartate, kāmaṃ nivartatām | na *jātucitpuruṣamātrasyānayanaṃ bhaviṣyati | *prāk ca vṛtterakṛtārthasya nivṛttau sāmarthyābhāvādvṛttireva na syāt | vṛttinimittā ca nivṛttistasmādadoṣa iti | tatra rājñaḥ puruṣa ityatra yadā tāvadavadhṛtaparāyatta*vṛttirayaṃ puruṣo na svatantrastadā svāmisaṃsargasyāvagatatvātsvāmiviśeṣajñānāyopādīyamāno rājaśabdaḥ svāmyantarebhyaḥ puruṣaṃ vyāvartayati | so 'yaṃ svāmyantaravyavacchedo bheda *ityucyate | yadā punaranavagataparāyattabhāvasya puruṣasya svāmisaṃbandhadyotanāya rājaśabdaḥ prayujyate tadā viśeṣasaṃsargasya* śabdopādānatvādanavakāśo viśeṣāntarasaṃpāta ityaśabdā* svāmyantaranivṛttiravasīyate | yadā tvarthāntaranivṛttiṃ vārthasaṃsargaṃ *vābhisaṃdhāyopasarjanapadāni prayujyante tadā śabdārthasāmarthyayoḥ pratipattinibandhanayorabhedāpekṣayā* bhedasaṃsargasamudayaḥ sāmarthyaṃ bhavati | yathā nīlaṃ ca tadutpalaṃ ceti nīlotpalam | prathamaścāsāvanurāgaśceti prathamānurāga iti, [page 661]prathamānurāgānantara ityādiṣu ca bhedasāmarthyaṃ yathā rājño bhṛtya iti | yato 'nantara ityukte 'vadhṛtamidaṃ kasyāpyavagheranantaro 'yaṃ na svatantra iti sarvo 'vadhiḥ prasaktaḥ | prathamānurāgasyetyukte sarvaḥ saṃbandhī prasaktaḥ | ihedānīṃ prathamānurāgānantara ityukte prathamānurāgo 'nantaraṃ nivartayatyanyebhyo 'vadhibhyaḥ | anantaraḥ prathamānurāgaṃ nivartayatyanyebhyaḥ saṃbandhibhyaḥ | tatra yo 'sau bhedastatsāmarthyaṃ ca, tannimittā ca vṛttiḥ | bhedanimittāyāṃ ca vṛttau satyāṃ vṛttyabhimukhasya bhedamupajanayyopasarjanasya prathamānurāgasyārtho nivartate | yasyāpi pradhānasyānantarasyāvadhimato nivartate so 'pyavadhimavacchinatti | evamubhayato vyavacchede nirjñāte 'nantaraviśeṣe samudāyārthe cānyasminprādurbhavati | yadi prathamānurāgādyartho nivartate, kāmaṃ nivartatām, na *jātucidavadhimanmātrasya saṃpratyayo bhaviṣyati | nanu cānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ jahatsvārthatvaṃ nopapadyate | tathā hi ‘prathamānurāgānantare’ ityukte kaścicchabdaḥ śrūyate | prathamānurāgetyanantareti ca pratīyamānavibhāgaḥ, artho 'pi kaścidgamyate kanyāvisrambhaṇādiravadhimattvaṃ ca | ‘mānānantare’ ityukte kaścicchabdabhāgo hīyate, kaścidupajāyate, kaścidanvayī | prathamānurāgeti hīyate, *mānetyupajāyate, atantara ityanvayī | artho 'pi kaściddhīyate, kaścidupajāyate, kaścidanvayī | kanyāvisrambhaṇādirhīyate, mānaśaithilyādipajāyate, avadhimattvamanvayi* | tena manyāmahe yaḥ śabdabhāgo hīyate tasyāsāvarthaḥ; yo 'rtho hīyate, ya upajāyate tasyāyamartho; yo 'rtha upajāyate, yo 'nvayī tasyāsāvartho; yo 'rthaḥ so 'nvayīti | maivam | yato 'nanyathāsiddhābhyāmevānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śabdā-[page 662]rthayoḥ saṃbandhāvadhāraṇam | anyathāsiddhau cemau | tathā hi yatra bṛṃhitaṃ hīyate, hneṣitamupajāyate, reṇucakramanvayi; tatra hastino hīyante, aśvā upajāyante, pipīlikā anvayinyaḥ | na caitāvatā reṇucakrādipipīlikāḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavati* | yatra vā kṣīraṃ hīyate, dadhyupajāyate, pātramanvayi, tatra mādhuryaṃ hīyate, amlatopajāyate, tṛptiranvayinī | na caitāvatā pātrasya tṛptiḥ kāryaṃ bhavati | avadhṛtaṃ hi sāmarthyamanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ pravibhajyate | yathā loke badhiro 'pi cakṣuṣmānālokayati, satyapi śrotra upahatacakṣurnālokayati rūpamityanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ cakṣuḥśrotrasaṃnidhāne rūpālokanaṃ cakṣuṣa eva vyavasthāpyate na śrotrasya | yasya kevalasya yo 'rtho 'vadhṛtaḥ padārthāntarasaṃnidhāne 'pi tasya sa eva | nahi rasanamasaṃnidhau darśanasya madhurādivyañjakaṃ darśanasaṃnidhau nīlādivyaktiṃ prati sāmarthyaṃ labhate | prathamānurāgaśabdasya kevalasyotkaṇṭhādiṣu, mānaśabdasyerṣyāyitādiṣu, anantaraśabdasya punaravadhimatsveva sāmarthyamavadhṛtamatasteṣāṃ tāvānevārtho bhavati | yaḥ punaḥ padayoranyonyopaśleṣādvisrambhaṇādirmānaśaithilyādirvāvadhimadviśeṣo 'nyāvadhikaḥ pratīyate vākyārthaḥ sa bhavatīti | yadi vā* yathānapekṣitāvayavārthā vṛkṣaśrotriyaśakragopādayaḥ svasāmarthyaniyatamarthamācakṣate tathā saṃghātā evaite prathamānurāgānantarādayo rājapuruṣādayaścānapekṣitāvayavārthā yathāsāmarthyamartheṣu niviśante | nanu cāvyapadeśyapūrvāparavibhāgā *bhinnārthābhidhāyino vṛkṣādayaḥ pratīyamānabhāgabhedānuyātāḥ saṃbandhipadārthopahitabhedavṛttyabhidhāyinaḥ punarime tatkathaṃ prathamānurāgānantarādayo vṛkṣādivadrụ̄dhiśabdā bhavitumarhanti | tadasat | rụ̄dhiśabdā yaugikā iti vibhāgo 'bhedadarśanādarśanābhyāma*bhiniviṣṭa-[page 663] buddheḥ pratipādanopāya eva | *apathābhiniviṣṭo hyayaṃ krameṇa tasmādapathā*nnivartayitavyaḥ | tato 'syāpratyabhijñāyamānaprakṛtayaḥ śrotriyakṣatriyādayo darśyante | na hyatra prakṛtirūpamavasīyate | yataḥ prakṛtyarthāvacchinnaḥ pratyayārtho 'bhidhīyate | tato 'navasīyamānāvayavavibhāgā rūḍhayaḥ kāścidupanyasyante | yatrātyantamasaṃbhavo 'vayavārthasya yathā—śakragopāḥ, tailapāyikāḥ, *maṇḍapeti | punaḥ kadācitsaṃnihitāvayavārthā jātiviśeṣābhidhāyinaḥ saptaparṇakṛtamālādaya udāhriyante | yataḥ prapalāśo 'pyanudbhinnapalāśo 'pi ca vanaspatiḥ sapta parṇānyasya parvaṇi parvaṇīti saptaparṇa ityākhyāyate | tathā niḥkīrṇakusumastaruranārabdhakalikājālako 'pi kṛtā mālāneneti kṛtamāla ityabhidhīyate | atha ca* pañcāṅa‍gulamivāśvakarṇa iva parṇamasyetyupacaritārthāvayavā jātivācina eva pañcāṅa‍gulāśvakarṇādayo varṇyante | teṣu hi pañcāṅa‍gulādivyapadeśaḥ prodbhidyamānapravālamapi yāvadanuvartate | tataḥ *saṃnidhāne 'pyanāśrīyamāṇavṛttipadārthā* lohitaśālirgaurakhara* ityādayo nigadyante | tatra hi sannapi varṇaviśeṣaḥ samudāyasya jātivacanatvācchabdārthatvena nāvasīyate | tadevamayaṃ śakalīkṛtavṛttipadārthābhiniveśaḥ prathamānurāgānantarādāviva rājapuruṣādāvapyavayavābhiniveśaṃ śakyate tyājayitum | ata eva prathamānurāgādīnāṃ vipralambhasaṃbhogādīnāṃ ca pāribhāṣiko 'pi saṃsargaḥ saṃnidhīyata iti ||

[page 664]

prakīrṇakeṣu spṛhayantīvratamaṣṭamīcandrakaḥ | sa hi caitracaturthīto 'ṣṭamacaturthyāmupādīyamānaḥ kāminībhirarcyate | yathā—

‘avasahiajaṇo païṇā salāhamāṇeṇa ecciraṃ hasio | cando tti tujjha* *muhasaṃmuhadiṇṇakusumaṃjalivilakkho* || 298 ||’
[avaśahṛtajanaḥ patyā ślāghyamāneneyacciraṃ hasitaḥ | candra iti tava mukhasaṃmukhadattakusumāñjalivilakṣaḥ ||]

yasyāṃ yavasrastareṣvabalā lolanti sā kundacaturthī | yathā—

‘luliā gahavaïdhūā diṇṇaṃ va phalaṃ javehiṃ savisesaṃ | *eṇhiṃ aṇivāriameva *gohaṇaṃ *caraü chettammi || 299 ||’
[lulitā gṛhapatisutā dattamiva phalaṃ yavaiḥ saviśeṣam | idānīmanivāritameva godhanaṃ caratu kṣetre ||]

vasantāvatāradivasaḥ suvasantako yathā—

‘chaṇapiṭṭhadhūsaratthaṇi mahumaatambacchi kuvalaāharaṇe | *kaṇṇakaacūamaṃjari putti tue maṃḍio gāmo || 300 ||’
[kṣaṇapiṣṭadhūsarastani madhumadatāmrākṣi kuvalayābharaṇe | karṇakṛtacūtamañjari putri tvayā maṇḍito grāmaḥ ||]

yatra striyo dolāmārohanti sāndolanacaturthī | yathā—

‘aṃdolaṇakkhaṇoṭṭhiāe diṭṭhe tumammi muddhāe | *āsaṃdhijjaï kāuṃ* karapellaṇaṇiccalā* dolā || 301 ||’
[āndolanakṣaṇotthitayā dṛṣṭe tvayi mugdhayā | āśāsyate kartuṃ karapreraṇaniścalā dolā ||]
[page 665]

ekameva *kusumanirbharaṃ śālmalivṛkṣamāśritya sunimīlitakādibhiḥ khelatāṃ krīḍaikaśālmalī | yathā—

‘ko esotti paloṭṭhuṃ* *siṃvalivaliaṃ piaṃ parikkhasaï | haliasuaṃ muddhavahū seajalolleṇa hattheṇa || 302 ||’
[ka eṣa iti pratyāvartituṃ śālmalivalitaṃ priyaṃ paripātayati | hālikasutaṃ mugdhavadhūḥ svedajalārdreṇa hastena ||]

trayodaśyāṃ kāmadevapūjāmadanotsavaḥ | yathā—

‘gāmataruṇīo hiaaṃ haraṃti pọdhāṇa* thaṇaharillīo | *maaṇūsaammi kosuṃbhakaṃcuāharaṇamettāo || 303 ||’
[grāmataruṇyo hṛdayaṃ haranti praụdhānāṃ stanabhāravatyaḥ | madanotsave kausumbhakañcukābharaṇamātrāḥ ||]

gandhodakapūrṇavaṃśanāḍīśṛṅa‍gakādibhiryūnāṃ priyajanābhiṣekakardamena krīḍodakakṣveḍikā | yathā—

‘*aha dhāviūṇa* saṃjhāmaeṇa* savvaṃgiaṃ paḍicchaṃti | *phaggumahe taruṇīo gahavaïsuahatthacikkhillaṃ || 304 ||’
[atha dhāvitvā saṃdhyāmadena sarvāṅgikaṃ pratīkṣante | phalgumahe taruṇyo gṛhapatisutahastakardamam ||]
[page 666]

yatrottamastriyaḥ pādābhighātenāśokaṃ vikāsya* tatkusumamavataṃsayanti sāśokottaṃsikā | yathā—

‘uttaṃsiūṇa dohalaviasiāsoaminduvadaṇāe | *vihiṇo ṇipphalakaṃkellikaraṇasaddo samuppusio || 305 ||’
[uttaṃsayitvā dohadavikasitāśokaminduvadanayā | vidherniṣphalakaṃkolakaraṇaśabdaḥ samutproñchitaḥ ||]

yatrāṅa‍ganābhiścūtamañjaryo 'varujyānaṅa‍gāya *bāṇatvena dāyaṃ dāyamavataṃsyante sā cūtabhañjikā | yathā—

‘raïaṃ pi tā ṇa sohaï raïjoggaṃ kāmiṇīṇa chaṇaṇevacchaṃ | kaṇṇe jā ṇa raïjjaï* kavolagholaṃtasahaāraṃ* || 306 ||’
[racitamapi tāvanna śobhate ratiyogyaṃ kāminīnāṃ kṣaṇanepathyam | karṇe yāvanna racyate kapolaghūrṇamānasahakāram ||]

yatra yuvatayo madirāgaṇḍūṣadohadena bakulaṃ vikāsya* tatpuṣpāṇyavacinvanti sā puṣpāvacāyikā | yathā—

‘pīṇathaṇaesu kesara dohaladāṇummuhīa ṇivalaṃto | tuṃgasiharaggapaḍaṇassa jaṃ phalaṃ taṃ tue* pattaṃ || 307 ||’
[pīnastaneṣu kesara dohadadānonmukhyā nipatan | tuṅa‍gaśikharāgrapatanasya yatphalaṃ tattvayā prāptam ||]
[page 667]

yatra kaste priyatama iti pṛcchadbhiḥ palāśādinavalatābhiḥ priyo jano hanyate sā cūtalatikā | yathā—

‘*ṇavalaïpahāramaṃge jahiṁ jahiṁ mahaï dearo dāuṃ | romaṃcadaṃḍarāī tahiṃ tahiṃ dīsaï bahūe || 308 ||’
[navalatāprahāramaṅa‍ge yatra yatrecchati devaro dātum | romāñcadaṇḍarājistatra tatra dṛśyate vadhvāḥ ||]

*pañcālyanuyātaṃ bhūtamātṛkā | yathā—

‘vihalaï se ṇevacchaṃ pammāaï maṃḍaṇaṃ gaī khalaï | bhūachaṇaṇaccaṇaammi* suhaa mā ṇaṃ *paloesu || 309 ||’
[vihvalayatyasyā nepathyaṃ pramlāyate maṇḍanaṃ gatiḥ skhalati | bhūtakṣaṇanṛtye subhaga maināṃ pralokayeḥ ||]

varṣāsu kadambanīpahāridrakādikusumaiḥ praharaṇabhūtaurdvidhā vanaṃ* vibhajya kāminīnāṃ krīḍāḥ* kadambayuddhāni | yathā—

‘sahiāhiṁ piavisajjiakadaṃbaraabhariaṇibbharucchasio | dīsaï kalaṃvathavaovva thaṇaharo haliasoṇhāe || 310 ||’
[sakhībhiḥ priyavisarjitakadambarajobharitanirbharocchvasitaḥ | dṛśyate kadambastabaka iva stanabharo hālikasnuṣāyāḥ ||]

prathamavarṣaṇaprarūḍhanavatṛṇāṅa‍kurāsu sthalīṣu śādvalamabhyarcya bhuktapītānāṃ [page 668]kṛtrimavivāhādikrīḍā navapattrikā | *tatra ca varaṇavidhānādau teṣāmevaṃvidhāḥ parihāsā bhavanti | yathā—

‘tā kuṇaha kālaharaṇaṃ tuvarantammi vi vare vivāhassa* | *jā[va] *paṃḍuṇahavaāiṃ hoṃti kumārīa aṃgāiṃ || 311 ||’
[tāvatkuruta kālaharaṇaṃ tvaramāṇe 'pi vare vivāhasya | yāvatpāṇḍunakhapadāni bhavanti kumāryā aṅa‍gāni ||]

abhinavabisāṅa‍kurodbhedābhirāmaṃ saraḥ samāśritya kāmimithunānāṃ krīḍā bisakhādikā | yathā—

‘geṇhaṃti piaamā piaamāṇa vaaṇāhi visalaaddhāiṃ | hiaāiṁ vi kusumāuhabāṇakaāṇearaṃdhāiṃ* || 312 ||’
[gṛhṇanti priyatamāḥ priyatamānāṃ vadanādbisalatārdhāni | hṛdayānīva kusumāyudhabāṇakṛtānekarandhrāṇi ||]

śakrotsavadivasaḥ śakrārcā | yathā—

‘saccaṃ caa kaṭṭhamao* suraṇāho jeṇa haliadhūāe* | hatthehiṁ *kamaladalakomalehiṁ chitto ṇa pallavio || 313 ||’
[satyameva kāṣṭhamayaḥ suranātho yena hālikaduhitrā | hastaiḥ kamaladalakomalaiḥ spṛṣṭo na pallavitaḥ ||]

*āśvine paurṇimāsī kaumudī | yathā—

‘aha taï *sahatthadiṇṇo *kaha vi khalaṃtamattajaṇamajjhe | *tissā thaṇesu jāo vilevaṇaṃ komuīvāso* || 314 ||’
[atha tvayā svahastadattaḥ kathamiva skhalanmattajanamadhye | tasyāḥ staneṣu jāto vilepana kaumudīvāsaḥ ||]
[page 669]

dīpotsavo yakṣarātriḥ | yathā—

‘aṇṇe vi hu* hoṃti chaṇā *ṇa uṇo dīāliāsaricchā de* | jattha jahicchaṃ gammaï *piavasahī *dīvaamiseṇa || 315 ||’
[anye 'pi khalu bhavanti kṣaṇā na punardīpālikāsadṛkṣāste | yatra yathecchaṃ gamyate priyavasatirdīpakamiṣeṇa ||]

*śamīdhānyaśūkadhānyānāmārdrāṇāmevāgnipakvānāmabhyavahāro 'bhyū*ṣakhādikā | yathā—

‘*vāaggiṇā karo me *daṭṭhotti puṇo puṇo ccia kahei* | haliasuā* maliacchusadohalī* pāmarajuāṇe* || 316 ||’
[nirvāṇāgninā karo me dagdha iti punaḥ punareva kathayati | hālikasutā mṛditocchvāsadohadinī pāmarayūni ||]

prathamata evekṣubhakṣaṇaṃ navekṣubhakṣikā | yathā—

‘diarassa saraamaüaṃ aṃsūmaïleṇa dei hattheṇa | paḍhamaṃ hiaaṃ bahuā* *pacchā gaṇḍaṃ sadantavaṇaṃ || 317 ||’
[devarasya śaranmṛdukamaśrumalinena dadāti hastena | prathamaṃ hṛdayaṃ vadhūkā paścādikṣuṃ sadantavraṇam ||]
[page 670]

grīṣmādau jalāśayāvagāhanaṃ toyakrīḍā | yathā—

‘pisuṇeṃti kāmiṇīṇaṃ *jalalukkapiāvaūhaṇasuhelliṃ | *kaṇḍaïakavoluphullaṇiccalacchīiṁ vaaṇāiṃ || 318 ||’
[piśunayanti kāminīnāṃ jalalīnapriyāvagūhanasukhakelim | kaṇṭakitakapolotphullaniścalākṣīṇi vadanāni ||]

*nāṭyādidarśanaṃ prekṣā | yathā—

‘ṇaccihii ṇaḍo pecchihii *jaṇavao bhoio* nāyakaḥ | so vi dūsihii *jaï *raṅa‍gavihaḍaṇaarī gahavaïghūā* ṇa baccihii* ||’
[nartiṣyate naṭaḥ prekṣiṣyate janapado bhogiko nāyakaḥ | so 'pi dūṣayiṣyati yadi raṅa‍gavighaṭanakarī gṛhapatiduhitā na vrajiṣyati]

āliṅa‍ganādiglahā durodarādikrīḍā* dyūtāni | yathā—

‘āśleṣe prathamaṃ krameṇa vijite *hṛdye 'dharasyārpaṇe *kelidyūtavidhau paṇaṃ priyatame kāntāṃ punaḥ pṛcchati | sāntarhāsaniruddhasaṃbhṛtarasodbhedasphuradgaṇḍayā* tūṣṇīṃ *sārivisāraṇāya nihitaḥ svedāmbugarbhaḥ karaḥ || 320 ||’

rāgoddīpanāya *mādhvīsevā madhupānaṃ | yathā—

‘thoārūḍhamahumaā khaṇa*pamhaṭṭhāvarāhadiṇṇullāvā | hasiūṇa saṃṭhavijjaï pieṇa saṃmarialajjiā kāvi piā 321’
[page 671]
[stokārūḍhamadhumadā kṣaṇavismṛtiraparādhadattollāpā | hasitvā saṃsthāpyate priyeṇa saṃsmṛtalajjitā kāpi priyā ||]

premaprakāre vipriyādibhirapyavināśanīyo nityo yathā—

‘diṭṭhākuviāṇuṇaā piā sahassajaṇapellaṇaṃ pi visahiaṃ* | jassa *ṇisaṇṇāi ure sirīe* pemmeṇa lahuio* appāṇo 322’
[dṛṣṭā kupitānunayā priyā sahasnajanapreraṇamapi visoḍham | yasya niṣaṇṇayorasi śriyā premṇā laghūkṛta ātmā ||]

tapaścaraṇādijanmā naimittiko yathā—

iyeṣa sā kartumavandhyarūpatāṃ samādhimāsthāya tapobhirātmanaḥ | avāpyate vā kathamanyathā dvayaṃ tathāvidhaṃ prema patiśca tādṛśaḥ 323’

anirdhāritaviśeṣaḥ sāmānyo yathā—

‘kuviāo* vi pasaṇṇāo *oraṇṇamuhīo *vi samāṇīo | jaha gahiā taha hiaaṃ dhāreṃti a ṇivvaïṃ bālā || 324 ||’
[*kupitā api prasannā avaruditamukhyo 'pi samānāḥ | yathā gṛhītāstathā hṛdayaṃ dhārayantīva nirvṛtiṃ bālāḥ ||]

nirdhāritaviśeṣaprakāro viśeṣavān yathā—

‘ṇavi taha aṇālavaṃtī hiaaṃ dūmei *māṇiṇī ahiaṃ | jaha *dūraviaṃbhia*garuarosamajjhatthabhaṇiehiṃ* || 325 ||’
[page 672]
[nāpi tathā nālapantī hṛdayaṃ dunoti māninyadhikam | yathā dūravijṛmbhitagurukaroṣamadhyasthamaṇitaiḥ ||]

iṅgitādibhirapyanavagamyaḥ pracchanno yathā—

‘diahe diahe *sūsaï saṃkeaabhaṃga*vaḍ̣dhiāsaṅa‍kā | *āvaṃḍurovaṇamuhī kalameṇa samaṃ kalamagovī* || 326 ||’
[divase divase śuṣyati saṃketakabhaṅa‍gavardhitāśaṅa‍kā | āpāṇḍurāvanatamukhī kalamena samaṃ kalamagopī ||]

*sakhyādibhiravagataḥ prakāśo yathā—

‘jaï hosi ṇa tassa piā aṇudiahaṃ ṇīsahehiṁ* aṃgehiṃ | ṇavasūapīapeūsamaṃtapāḍi vva* kiṃ suvasi || 327 ||’
[yadi bhavasi na tasya priyānudivasaṃ *niḥsahairaṅa‍gaiḥ | navasūtapīta*pīyūṣamattamahiṣīvatsikeva kiṃ svapiṣi ||]

kāraṇopādhikaḥ kṛtrimo yathā—

‘addaṃsaṇeṇa puttaa suṭa‍ṭhu vi ṇehāṇubaṃdha*gahiāiṃ | hatthaüḍapāṇiāiṁ vi(va)* kāleṇa galaṃti pemmāiṃ* || 328 ||’
[adarśanena putraka suṣṭha‍vapi snehānubandhagṛhītāni | hastapuṭapānīyānīva kālena galanti premāṇi ||]
[page 673]

kāraṇanirapekṣo 'pṛtrimo yathā—

‘jaha jaha jarāpariṇao hoi paī duggao virūo vi | *kulapāliāiṃ taha taha ahiaaraṃ vallaho hoi || 329 ||’
[yathā yathā jarāpariṇato bhavati patirdurgato virūpo 'pi | kulapālikāyāstathā tathādhikataraṃ vallabho bhavati ||]

janmāntarasaṃskārajanitaḥ sahajo yathā—

‘āṇia*pulaübbheo savattipaṇaaparidhūsarammi vi gurue* | piadaṃsaṇe pavaḍḍhaï *maṇṇuṭṭhāṇe vi *ruppiṇīa pahariso || 330 ||’
[ānītapulakodbhedaḥ sapatnīpraṇayaparidhūsare 'pi guruke | priyadarśane pravardhate manyusthāne 'pi rukmiṇyāḥ praharṣaḥ ||]

upacārāpekṣaprakarṣa āhāryo yathā—

‘ghariṇīa akaïavvaṃ* caṭuaṃ* piaame kuṇaṃtammi | akaatthāiṃ vi jāāi *jhaṃti sịdhilāiṃ* aṃgāiṃ || 331 ||’
[gṛhiṇyā akaitavaṃ caṭukaṃ priyatame kurvāṇe sati | akṛtārthānīva jāyāyā jhaṭiti śithilānyaṅa‍gāni ||]

yauvanajo yathā—

‘taṃbamuhakaāhoā jaha* jaha thaṇaā kileṃti kumarīṇam* | taha taha laddhāvāsovva vammaho* hiaamāvisaï || 332 ||’
[page 674]
[tāmramukhakṛtābhogau yathā yathā stanau klāmyataḥ kumārīṇām | tathā tathā labdhāvāsa iva manmatho hṛdayamāviśati ||]

upacārānapekṣo visrambhajo yathā—

‘ṇa vi taha chearaāiṃ haraṃti punaruttarāaramiāiṃ | jaha jatthava tatthava jaha va taha va sabbhāvaramiāiṃ || 333 ||’
[nāpi tathā chekaratāni haranti* punaruktarāgaramitāni | yathā yatraiva tatraiva yathā vā tathā vā sadbhāvaramitāni ||]

premapuṣṭiṣu cakṣuḥprītiryathā—

‘*utpattirdevayajanādbrahmavādī nṛpaḥ pitā | suprasannojjvalā mūrtirasyāḥ snehaṃ karoti me || 334 ||’

manaḥsaṅa‍go yathā—

‘eṣā mano me prasabhaṃ śarīrātpituḥ padaṃ madhyamamutpatantī | *surāṅa‍ganā karṣati khaṇḍitāgrātsūtraṃ mṛṇālādiva rājahaṃsī || 335 ||’

saṃkalpotpattiryathā—

‘taṃ pulaïaṃ* *vi pecchaï taṃ cia* ṇijjhāi* tīa geṇhaï gottaṃ | *ṭhāia tassa samaaṇe aṇṇaṃ vi* viciṃtaammi* saccia hiae ||’
[tāṃ pulakitāṃ prekṣate tāmeva nirdhyāyati tasyā gṛhṇāti gotram | tiṣṭhati tasya samadane anyāmapi vicintayati saiva hṛdaye ||]
[page 675]

pralāpo yathā—

‘amaamaa gaaṇasehara raaṇīmuhatilaa caṃda de chivasu | *chitto jehiṃ piaamo *mamamaṃ *vi tehiṃ cia* karehiṃ || 337 ||’
[amṛtamaya gaganaśekhara rajanīmukhatilaka candra he spṛśa | spṛṣṭo yaiḥ priyatamo māmapi taireva karaiḥ ||]

jāgaro yathā—

‘*tuha *virahujjāgarao siviṇe vi ṇa* dei daṃsaṇasuhāiṃ | vāheṇa jahāloaṇaviṇoaṇaṃ* pi *se vihaam || 338 ||’
[tava virahojjāgarakaḥ svapne 'pi na dadāti darśanasukhāni | bāṣpeṇa yathālokanavinodanamapyasyā vihatam ||]

kārśyaṃ yathā—

‘*aïkovaṇā vi *sāsū *roāviā *gaavaīa soṇhāe | *pāapaḍaṇoṇṇaāe dosu vi* galiesu valaesu || 339 ||’
[atikopanāpi śvaśrū roditā gatapatikayā snaṣayā | pādapatanāvanatayā dvayorapi galitayorvalayayoḥ ||]

aratirviṣayāntare yathā—

‘*asamatto vi samappaï *apariggahialahuo paraguṇālāvo* |[page 676] tassa piāpaḍivaḍ̣dhā* ṇa samappaï raïsuhāsamattā vi kahā || 340 ||’
[asamāpto 'pi samāpyate 'parigṛhītalaghukaḥ paraguṇālāpaḥ | tasya priyāpratibaddhā na samāpyate ratisukhāsamāptāpi kathā ||]

lajjāvisarjanaṃ yathā—

‘agaṇiasesajuāṇā* bālaa volīṇaloamajjāā | aha sā bhamaï disāmuhapasāriacchī tuha kaeṇa || 341 ||’
[agaṇitāśeṣayuvakā bālaka vyatikrāntalokamaryādā | atha sā bhramati diśāmukhaprasāritākṣī tava kṛtena ||]

vyādhiryathā—

‘aṇṇaha* ṇa tīraï ccia parivaḍḍhaṃtaa*garuasaṃtāvaṃ | maraṇaviṇoeṇa viṇā viramāveuṃ virahadukkham || 342 ||’
[anyathā na śakyata eva parivardhamānagurukasaṃtāpam | maraṇavinodena vinā viramayituṃ virahaduḥkham ||]

unmādo yathā—

‘avalaṃbaha *sā saṃkaha ṇa imā gahalaṃghiā paribbhamaï | atthakkagajjiubbhaṃ*tahitthahiaā pahiajāā || 343 ||’
[avalambadhvaṃ mā śaṅa‍kadhvaṃ neyaṃ grahalaṅghitā paribhramati | ākasmikagarjitodbhrāntatrastahṛdayā pathikajāyā ||]

mūrcchā yathā—

‘jaṃ mucchiā ṇa a suo kalaṃbagaṃdheṇa taṃ guṇe paḍiaṃ | iaraha gajjiasaddo jīeṇa viṇā ṇa boliṃto || 344 ||’
[page 677]
[yanmūrcchitā na ca śrutaḥ kadambagandhena tadguṇe patitam | itarathā garjitaśabdo jīvena vinā na vyatikrāmet ||]

maraṇaṃ yathā—

‘*ajja vi tāva ekkaṃ *māmaṃ *vārehi piasahi ruaṃtim | kalliṃ *uṇa tammi gae jaï ṇa marissaṃ ṇa roissam 345’
[adyāpi tāvadekaṃ mā māṃ vāraya priyasakhi rudantīm | kalye punastasmin gate yadi na mariṣyāmi na roṣyāmi ||]

tā imā vipralambhajanmāno dvādaśāpi premapuṣṭibhūmayaḥ saṃbhogeṣu svānurūpāmeva premaprakarṣabhūmikāmāskandayanti ||

nāyakeṣu kathāvyāpī nāyako yathā—

‘guroḥ śāsanamatyetuṃ na śaśāka sa rāghavaḥ | yo rāvaṇaśiraśchedakāryabhāre 'pyaviklavaḥ || 346 ||’

pratināyako yathā—

‘jetāraṃ lokapālānāṃ *svamukhairarciteśvaram | rāmastulitakailāsamarātiṃ bahvamanyata || 347 ||’

upanāyako yathā—

‘sa hatvā vālinaṃ vīraṃ* tatpade cirakāṅkṣite | dhātoḥ sthāna ivādeśaṃ sugrīvaṃ saṃnyaveśayat || 348 ||’
[page 678]

anunāyako yathā—

‘*sa mārutasutānītamahauṣadhihṛtavyathaḥ | laṅa‍kāstrīṇāṃ punaścakre vilāpācāryakaṃ śaraiḥ || 349 ||’

kathāvyāpinī nāyikā yathā—

‘tīe savisesadūniasavattihiaāiṃ *ṇivvalaṃtasiṇehaṃ | piagaruiāi ṇimiaṃ sohaggaguṇāṇa aggabhūmīa paaṃ || 350 ||’
[tayā saviśeṣadūnitasapatnīhṛdayayā nirvartyamānasneham | priyagurūkṛtayā nirmitaṃ saubhāgyaguṇānāmagrabhūmyāṃ padam ||]

pratināyikā yathā—

‘taṃ* tiasakusumadāmaṃ hariṇā ṇimmahiasurahigaṃdhāmoaṃ | appaṇaïaṃ pi dūmia*paṇaï*ṇihiaeṇa ruppiṇīa *viiṇṇam 351’
[tattridaśakusumadāma hariṇā nirgacchatsurabhigandhāmodam | ātmanānītamapi dūnitapraṇayinīhṛdayena rukmiṇyai vitīrṇam ||]

upanāyikā yathā—

‘devīsvīkṛtamānasasya niyataṃ svapnāyamānasya me tadgotragrahaṇādiyaṃ suvadanā yāyātkathaṃ na vyathām | itthaṃ yantraṇayā kathaṃ kathamapi kṣīṇā niśā jāgrato dākṣiṇyopahatena sā priyatamā svapne 'pi nāsāditā 352’

anunāyikā yathā—

‘ślāghyānāṃ guṇināṃ dhuri sthitavati śreṣṭhānvavāye* tvayi pratyastavyasane mahīyasi paraṃ prīto 'smi jāmātari | [page 679] teneyaṃ madayantikādya bhavataḥ prītyai bhavatpreyase* mitrāya prathamānurāgaghaṭitāpyasmābhirutsṛjyate || 353 ||’

ābhāseṣu nāyakābhāso yathā—

‘*kaha mā chijjaü majjho imīa kaṃdoṭṭadalasaricchehiṃ | acchīhiṃ jo ṇa dīsaï ghaṇathaṇahararuddhapasarehiṃ || 354 ||’
[kathaṃ mā kṣīyatāṃ madhya etasyā nīlotpaladalasadṛśābhyām | akṣibhyāṃ yo na dṛśyate ghanastanabhararuddhaprasarābhyām ||]

nāyikābhāso yathā—

‘kṛtasītāparityāgaḥ sa ratnākaramekhalām | bubhuje pṛthivīpālaḥ pṛthivīmeva kevalām || 355 ||’

ubhayābhāso yathā—

‘avaūhiapubbadise samaaṃ* joṇhāe seviapaosamuhe* | māi ṇa jhijjaü *raaṇī varadisāitapacchiammi miaṅa‍ke 356’
[avagūhitapūrvadiśe samakaṃ jyotsnayā sevitapradoṣamukhe | mātarna kṣīyate rajanī aparadiśābhimukhaprasthite mṛgāṅa‍ke ||]

tiryagābhāso yathā—

‘orattapaṅa‍kaamuhiṃ *vammahaṇaḍiaṃ va salilasaaṇaṇisaṇṇaṃ | alliaï tīraṇaliṇiṃ vāāi gamei *sahacariṃ cakkāo* 357’
[uparaktapaṅa‍kajamukhīṃ manmathanaṭitāmiva salilaśayananiṣaṇṇām | āliṅa‍gati tīranalinīṃ vācā gamayati sahacarīṃ cakravākaḥ ||]
[page 680]

nāyakeṣu sarvaguṇasaṃpadyogāduttamaḥ | sa yathā—

‘rāmo 'yaṃ jagatīha vikramaguṇairyātaḥ prasiddhiṃ parāmasmadbhāgyaviparyayādyadi paraṃ devo na jānāti tam | bandīvaiṣa yaśāṃsi gāyati marudyasyaikabāṇāhatiśreṇībhūtaviśālatālavivarodbhūtaiḥ svaraiḥ saptabhiḥ 358’

pādonaguṇasampadyogānmadhyamo yathā—

‘kiṃ no vyāptadiśāṃ prakampitabhuvāmakṣauhiṇīnāṃ phalaṃ kiṃ droṇena kimaṅa‍garājaviśikhairevaṃ yadi klāmyasi | *jīvadbhrātṛśatasya me *bhujabalacchāyāṃ sukhāmāśritā tvaṃ duryodhanakesarīndragṛhiṇī śaṅa‍kāspadaṃ kiṃ tava || 359 ||’

ardhaguṇasampadyogātkaniṣṭho yathā—

‘ekasmiñśayane mayā mayasutāmāliṅa‍gya *nidrālasā- munnidraṃ śayitena maccaraṇayoḥ saṃvāhanavyāpṛtā | pādāgreṇa tilottamā stanataṭe sasnehamāpīḍitā harṣāvegasamarpitāni pulakānyadyāpi no muñcati || 360 ||’

sattvapradhānaḥ sāttviko yathā—

‘śaktyā vakṣasi magnayā saha mayā mụ̄dhe plavaṅa‍gādhipe nidrāṇeṣu ca vidravatsu kapiṣu prāptāvakāśe dviṣi | mā bhaiṣṭeti nirundhataḥ kapibhayaṃ tasyodbhaṭabhrūsthite- rmarmacchedavisaṃṣṭhulākṣarajaḍā vācastvayā na śrutāḥ 361’
[page 681]

rajaḥpradhāno rājaso yathā—

‘sāmantamaulimaṇirañjitaśāsanāṅa‍ka- mekātapattramavanerna tathā prabhutvam | asyāḥ sakhe caraṇayoradhigamya samya- gājñākaratvamahamadya yathā kṛtārthaḥ || 362 ||’

tamaḥpradhānastāmaso yathā—

‘tapo vā śastraṃ vā *vyapadiśati yaḥ kaścidiha vaḥ sa darpādu*ddāmadviṣamasahamānaḥ kalayatu | arāmāṃ niḥsīradhvajadaśarathīkṛtya vasudhā*- matṛptastatkulyānapi* paraśurāmaḥ śamayati || 363 ||’

anekajātiḥ sādhāraṇo yathā—

‘snātā tiṣṭhati kuntaleśvarasutā vāro 'ṅa‍garājasvasu- rdyūtai rātririyaṃ jitā kamalayā devī prasādyādya ca | ityantaḥpurasundarī prati mayā vijñāya vijñāpite devenāpratipattimūḍhamanasā dvitrāḥ sthitaṃ nāḍikāḥ || 364 ||’

ananyajānirasādhāraṇo yathā—

‘āvivāhasamayādgṛhe vane śaiśave tadanu yauvane punaḥ | svāpahetura*nupāsito 'nyayā rāmabāhurupadhānameṣa te || 365 ||’

ahaṃkārapradhāno dhīroddhato yathā—

‘cakraṃ vā madhuhā *﻿kṛtāntagṛhiṇīdattāgrapañcāṅa‍gulaṃ vajraṃ bhūdharapakṣaśoṇitasurāpānonmadaṃ vā vṛṣā | [page 682] śūlaṃ *vāsuraraktabindunicitaṃ gṛhṇātu śūlāyudho dhṛṣṭadyumnamahaṃ nihanmi samare kaścitparitrāyatām || 366 ||’

ratyupacārapradhāno dhīralalito yathā—

‘ādhātuṃ vinayaṃ nirāgasi nare kupyantu nāmeśvarā- stena svāśayaśuddhireva sukarā prāyaḥ prabhūṇāṃ puraḥ | mithyāmānini manyase yadi tadā nityaṃ manovartinī dhyātā tāmarasākṣi citrapaṭake* kā vā tvadanyā mayā || 367 ||’

upaśamapradhāno *dhīrapraśānto yathā—

‘kulamamalinaṃ bhadrā mūrtirmatiḥ śrutiśālinī bhujabalamalaṃ sphītā lakṣmīḥ prabhutvamakhaṇḍitam | prakṛtisubhagā hyete* bhāvā madasya ca hetavo vrajati puruṣo yairunmādaṃ ta eva tavāṅa‍kuśāḥ* || 368 ||’

*visrabdhodārakarmā dhīrodāttaḥ | sa yathā—

‘kapole jānakyāḥ karikalabhadantadyutimuṣi smarasmeraṃ gaṇḍoḍḍamarapulakaṃ vaktrakamalam | muhuḥ paśyañśrṛṇvanrajanicarasenākalakalaṃ jaṭājūṭagranthiṃ draḍhayati raghūṇāṃ parivṛḍhaḥ || 369 ||’

kaitavapradhānaḥ śaṭho yathā—

‘dṛṣṭa‍vaikāsanasaṃsthite priyatame paścādupetyādarādekasyā nayane nimīlya vihitakrīḍānubandhacchalaḥ |[page 683] īṣadvakritakandharaḥ sapulakaḥ premollasanmānasāmantarhāsalasatkapolaphalakāṃ dhūrto 'parāṃ cumbati || 370 ||’

kṛtāparādho 'pyavilakṣo dhṛṣṭo yathā—

‘śataṃ vārānuktaḥ priyasakhi vacobhiḥ sa paruṣaiḥ sahasraṃ nirdhūtaḥ padanipatitaḥ pārṣṇihatibhiḥ | *kiyatkṛtvo baddhāḥ punariha na vedmi bhrukuṭaya- stathāpi kliśyanmāṃ kṣaṇamapi na dhṛṣṭo viramati || 371 ||’

hṛdayaṃgamapravṛttiranukūlo yathā—

‘muñca kopama*nimittakopane sandhyayā praṇamito 'smi nānyayā | kiṃ na vetsi sahadharmacāriṇaṃ cakravākasamavṛttimātmanaḥ || 372 ||’

auparodhikapravṛttirdakṣiṇo yathā—

anena kalyāṇi mṛṇālakomalaṃ vratena gātraṃ glapayasyakāraṇam | prasādamākāṅa‍kṣati yastavotsukaḥ sa kiṃ tvayā dāsajanaḥ prasādyate ||’

nāyikāguṇeṣu sarvaguṇasaṃpadyogāduttamā yathā—

hasiāiṃ samaṃsalakomalāiṃ vīsaṃbhakomalaṃ vaaṇaṃ | *sabbhāvakomalaṃ pulaïaṃ ca ṇamimo sumahilāṇaṃ || 374 ||’
[hasitāni samāṃsalakomalāni visrambhakomalaṃ vacanam | sadbhāvakomalaṃ pralokitaṃ ca namāmaḥ sumahilānām ||]

pādonaguṇasaṃpadyogānmadhyamā yathā—

‘ṇiadaïadaṃsaṇukkhitta pahia aṇena vaccasu paheṇa | *gahavaïbahuā *dullaṃghiavāurā iha ggāme* || 375 ||’
[page 684]

ardhaguṇasaṃpadyogādadhamā yathā—

‘*taṃ kira khaṇā virajjasi taṃ kira *uvahasasi *saalamahilāo | ehehi vāravālii *aṃsū maïlaṃ samuppisimo* || 376 ||’
[tvaṃ kila kṣaṇādvirajyase tvaṃ kilopahasasi sakalamahilāḥ | ehyehi vārapālike aśru malinaṃ samutproñchāmaḥ ||]

vayaḥkauśalābhyāmasaṃpūrṇā mugdhā yathā—

‘sahiāhiṁ bhaṇṇamāṇā thaṇae laggaṃ kusuṃbhapupphaṃ* tti | *muddhabahuā hasijjaï papphoḍaṃtī ṇahavaāiṃ || 377 ||’
[sakhībhirbhaṇyamānā stane lagnaṃ kusumbhapuṣpamiti | mugdhavadhūkā hasyate prasphoṭayantī nakhapadāni ||]

vayasā paripūrṇā madhyamā yathā—

‘paḍivakkhamaṇṇuuṃje* lāvaṇṇaüḍe* aṇaṃgagaakumbhe* | purisasaahiaadharie kīsa thaṇaṃtī thaṇe vahasi || 378 ||’
[pratipakṣamanyupuñjau lāvaṇyapuṭāvanaṅa‍gagajakumbhau | puruṣaśatahṛdayadhṛtau kimiti stanantī stanau vahasi ||]

vayaḥkauśalābhyāṃ saṃpūrṇā pragalbhā yathā—

‘*khiṇṇassa *ṭhavei ure païṇo gimhāvaraṇharamiassa* | ollaṃ galantaüpphaṃ* ṇhaṇasuandhaṃ ciurabhāram || 379 ||’
[khinnasya sthāpayatyurasi patyurgrīṣmāparāhṇaramitasya | ārdre galatkusumaṃ snānasugandhaṃ cikurabhāram ||]
[page 685]

yatnāpaneyamānā dhīrā yathā—

‘ṇa vi taha aṇālavaṃtī hiaaṃ dūnei māṇiṇī ahiam* | *jaha *dūraviambhia*garuarosamajjhatthabhaṇiehiṃ || 380 ||’
[nāpi tathānālapantī hṛdayaṃ dunoti māninyadhikam | yathā dūravijṛmbhitakaroṣamadhyasthabhaṇitaiḥ ||]

*ayatnāpaneyamānā 'dhīrā yathā—

‘avalaṃbiamāṇaparaṃmuhīa* *eṃtassa māṇiṇi piassa | *puṭṭhipulaüggamo tuha kahei *saṃmuhaṭṭhiaṃ hiaaṃ || 381 ||’
[avalambitamānaparāṅa‍bhukhyā āgacchato mānini priyasya | pṛṣṭhapulakodgamaste kathayati saṃmukhasthitaṃ hṛdayam ||]

ātmīyā svā yathā—

‘dhariṇīa* mahāṇasakammalaggamasimaliieṇa* hattheṇa | chittaṃ muhaṃ hasijjaï caṃdāvatthaṃ gaaṃ païṇā* || 382 ||’
[gṛhiṇyā mahānasakarmalagnamalinitena hastena | spṛṣṭaṃ mukhaṃ hasyate candrāvasthāṃ gataṃ patyā ||]

parakīyānyadīyā yathā—

‘vaïvivaraṇiggaadalo eraṇḍo* sāhaïvva* taruṇāṇaṃ | ettha ghare haliavahū eddahamettatthaṇī vasaï || 383 ||’
[page 686]
[vṛtivivaranirgatadala eraṇḍaḥ sādhayatīva taruṇebhyaḥ | atra gṛhe hālikavadhūretāvanmātrastanī vasati ||]

pāṇigṛhītā ụ̄dhā yathā—

‘*bālattaṇadullaliāe ajja aṇajjaṃ kaaṃ ṇavavahūe | *bhāāmi ghare eāiṇitti* ṇiṃto* paī ruddho || 384 ||’
[bālatvadurlalitayādya anārye kṛtaṃ navavadhvā | bibhemi gṛhe ekākinīti niryan patī ruddhaḥ ||]

anụ̄dhā kumārī yathā—

‘kassa karo bahupuṇṇaphalekkataruṇo tuhaṃ *visimmihii | thaṇapariṇāhe mammahaṇihāṇakalaso vva* *pāroho || 385 ||’
[kasya karo bahupuṇyaphalaikatarostava viśramiṣyati | stanapariṇāhe manmathanidhānakalśa iva prarohaḥ ||]

prathamọdhā jyeṣṭhā yathā—

‘paṇaaṃ *paḍhamapiāe *rakkhiukāmo vi *mahuramahurehiṃ | *cheavaro *viṇaḍijjaï ahiṇavabahu*āvilāsehiṃ || 386 ||’
[praṇayaṃ prathamapriyāyā rakṣitukāmo 'pi madhuramadhuraiḥ | chekavaraḥ sukhāyate 'bhinavavadhūkāvilāsaiḥ ||]
[page 687]

paścādụ̄dhā kanīyasī yathā—

*‘uṭṭhantamahārambhe thaṇae *daṭṭhūṇa muddhavahuāe* | *osaṇṇakavolāe ṇīsasiaṃ paḍhamaghariṇīe || 387 ||’
[uttiṣṭhanmahārambhau stanakau dṛṣṭa‍vā mugdhavadhvāḥ | avasannakapolayā niḥśvasitaṃ prathamagṛhiṇyā ||]

ahaṃkārarddhiruddhatā yathā—

‘aṇṇamahilāpasaṃgaṃ de deva* karesu amha daïassa* | purisā ekkaṃtarasā* ṇa hu dosaguṇe viāṇaṃti || 388 ||’
[anyamahilāprasaṅa‍gaṃ he deva kurvasmākaṃ dayitasya | puruṣā ekāntarasā na khalu doṣaguṇau vijānanti ||]

gūḍhamānarddhirudāttā yathā—

‘*jāṇaï jāṇāveuṃ *aṇuṇaavihurīamāṇaparisesaṃ | *raïvikkamammi viṇaāvalaṃbaṇaṃ sa ccia kuṇantī* || 389 ||’
[jānāti jñāpayitumanunayavidhuritamānapariśeṣam | rativikrame vinayāvalambanaṃ saiva kurvantī ||]

nirvāṇamānā* śāntā yathā—

‘jaïā pio ṇa dīsaï bhaṇaha halā kassa kīrae māṇo | aha diṭṭhammi* vi māṇo tā tassa piattaṇaṃ katto* || 390 ||’
[page 688]
[yadā priyo na dṛśyate bhaṇata halā kasya kriyate mānaḥ | atha dṛṣṭe 'pi mānastattasya priyatvaṃ kutaḥ ||]

ślāghanīyamānā lalitā yathā—

‘hasiehiṁ uvālaṃbhā *accuvaārehiṁ rūsiavvāiṃ | *aṃsūhi *bhaṃḍaṇāhiṃ eso maggo *sumahilāṇaṃ || 391 ||’
[hasitairupālambhā atyupacārai rūṣitavyāni | aśrubhiḥ kalahā eṣa mārgaḥ sumahilānām ||]

aniyatānekopabhogyā sāmānyā yathā—

‘*kaḍue *dhūmaṃdhāre *abbhuttaṇamaggiṇo *samappihii | muhakamalacuṃbaṇalehalammi *pāsaṭṭhie diare || 392 ||’
[kaṭuke dhūmāndhakāre 'bhyuttejanamagneḥ samāpsyate | mukhakamalacumbanābhilāṣiṇi pārśvasthite devare ||]

patyantaraṃ prāptā punarpbhūryathā—

‘mayena nirmitāṃ *labdhvā laṅa‍kāṃ mandodarīmapi | reme mūrtāṃ daśagrīvalakṣmīmiva vibhīṣaṇaḥ || 393 ||’

ātmacchandā svairiṇī yathā—

‘taha sā jāṇaṃi *pāvā loe *pacchaṇṇamaviṇaaṃ kāum* | jaha paḍhamaṃ cia saccia* *likkhaï majjhe carittavaṃtīṇa || 394 ||’
[page 689]
[tathā sā jānāti pāpā loke pracchannamavinayaṃ kartum | yathā prathamameva saiva lekhyate madhye caritravatīnām* ||]

kalācatuḥṣaṣṭivid gaṇikā yathā—

‘sachandaramaṇadaṃsaṇarasavaḍ̣dhiagaruavammahavilāsaṃ | *suviaḍḍhavesavaṇiāramiaṃ ko vaṇṇiuṃ taraï || 395 ||’
[svacchandaramaṇadarśanarasavardhitagurukamanmathavilāsam | suvidagdhaveṣavanitāramitaṃ ko varṇituṃ śaknoti ||]

rūpayauvanamātropajīvinī rūpājīvā yathā—

‘ayameva dahyamānasmaranirgatadhūmavartikākāraḥ | cikurabharastava sundari kāmijanaṃ rkikarīkurute || 396 ||’

kuṭṭamitādīnāṃ kartrī vilāsinī yathā—

‘sāmaṇṇasundarīṇaṃ vibbhamamāvahaï aviṇao ccea | dhūma ccia pajjaliāṇaṃ bahu mao surahidārūṇa || 397 ||’
[sāmānyasundarīṇāṃ vibhramamāvahatyavinaya eva | dhūṃma eva prajvālitānāṃ bahu mataḥ surabhidārūṇām ||]

yathoktalakṣaṇāsu khaṇḍitā yathā—

‘*paccūsāgaaṇurattadeha taïloaloṇāṇanda | aṇṇatthakhaviasavvaria ṇahabhūsaṇa diṇavaï* ṇamo de || 398 ||’
﻿[page 690]
[pratyūṣāgatānuraktadeha trailokyalocanānanda | anyatrakṣapitaśarvarīka nabhobhūṣaṇa dinapate namaste ||]

kalahāntaritā yathā—

‘aha so vilakkhahiao mae *ahavvāi agaṇiappaṇao | paravajjaṇaccirīhiṁ tumhehiṁ uvekkhio jaṃ(jeṃ)to* || 399 ||’
[atha sa vilakṣahṛdayo mayā bhavyayāgaṇitapraṇayaḥ | paravādyanartanaśīlābhiryuṣmābhirupekṣito gacchan ||]

vipralabdhā yathā—

‘aha sā tahiṃ tahiṃ vvia* vāṇīravaṇammi *cukkasaṃkeā | tuha daṃsaṇaṃ vimaggaï* pabbhaṭṭhaṇihāṇaṭhāṇaṃ va* || 400 ||’
[atha sā tatra tatraiva vānīravane vismṛtasaṃketā | tava darśanaṃ vimārgati prabhraṣṭanidhānasthānamiva ||]

vāsakasajjā yathā—

‘ehii pio tti ṇimisaṃ va jaggiaṃ jāmiṇīa paḍhamaddhaṃ | sesaṃ saṃtāvaparavvasāe barisaṃ ba bolīṇam || 401 ||’
[eṣyati priya iti nimiṣamiva jāgṛtaṃ yāminyāḥ prathamārdham | śeṣaṃ saṃtāpaparavaśayā varṣamiva vyatikrāntam ||]

svādhīnapatikā yatha—

‘sāloe ccia* sūre ghariṇī gharasāmiassa ghettūṇa | ṇecchaṃtassa vi pāe dhuaï* hasaṃtī hasaṃtassa || 402 ||’
[page 691]
[sāloka eva sūrye gṛhiṇī gṛhasvāmino gṛhītvā | necchato 'pi pādau dhāvati hasantī hasataḥ ||]

abhisārikā yathā—

‘gammihisi *tassa pāsaṃ mā *jūrasu taruṇi vaḍḍhaü* miaṃko | *duddhe duddhambhiva* caṃdiāe* ko pecchaï* muhaṃ de || 403 ||’
[gamiṣyasi tasya pārśvaṃ mā khidyasva taruṇi vardhatāṃ mṛgāṅa‍ka | dugdhe dugdhamiva candrikāyāṃ kaḥ prekṣate mukhaṃ te ||]

proṣitabhartṛkā yathā—

‘gimhe *davaggimasimaïliāiṁ dīsaṃti *viṃjhasiharāiṃ | *āsasu paütthavaïe ṇa hoṃti ṇavapāusabbhāiṃ || 404 ||’
[griṣme dāvāgnimaṣīmalinitāni dṛśyante vindhyaśikharāṇi | āśvasihi proṣitapatike na bhavanti navaprāvṛḍabhrāṇi ||]

virahotkaṇṭhitā yathā—

‘asmin varṣamahe na vartata idaṃ yatkāmadevotsave stheyaṃ putri nirannayā tadadhunā kiṃcinmukhe dīyatām | ityuke jaratījanena kathamapyadhvanyavadhvā tataḥ paryaste 'hani kalpitaśca kavalo dhautaśva *dhārāśrubhiḥ || 405 ||’
[page 692]

hīnapātreṣu śakāro yathā—

‘*palicca le *laṃbadaśākalāaṃ pāvālaaṃ *śuttaśadeṇa *chattaṃ | maṃśaṃ ca khāduṃ* *tuha oṭṭhakāṃhiṁ cuṃkuścakuścucukuścukuṃti* || 406 ||’
[pratīccha re lambadaśākalāpaṃ pravārakaṃ sūtraśatena channam | māṃsaṃ ca khādituṃ tava oṣṭhakābhyāṃ cukuścukuścukkucukuścukuṃti ||]

lalako yathā—

‘*kaṃbalivālie kaṃtti* *kuḍammaladanti dhiddhiluddhie* maïveālasi | lattiṃsovari *jaggiri tuma sahiṃ kharāvidupopphali* ṇa lekīsi* ṇa āgasi || 407 ||’
[. . . . . . . . . . . . . | . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . ||]

amātyādirādirāsanārhaḥ pāṣaṇḍādirvā pīṭhamardaḥ | tayoramātyeṣu mālyavān yathā—

‘hā vatsāḥ kharadūṣaṇatriśiraso vadhyāḥ stha pāpasya me hā hā vatsa vibhīṣaṇa tvamapi me kāryeṇa heyaḥ *sthitaḥ | [page 693] hā madvatsala vatsa rāvaṇa mahatpaśyāmi te saṃkaṭaṃ vatse kaikasi* hā hatāsi *na ciraṃ trīnputrakāndrakṣyasi 408’

pāṣaṇḍeṣu bhairavānando yathā—

‘daṃsemi taṃ pi *sasiṇaṃ vasuhāvaïṇṇaṃ* thambhemi tassa vi raïssa* rahaṃ ṇahaddhe | āṇemi jakkhasurasiddhagaṇaṃgaṇāo taṃ ṇatthi bhūmivalae* maha jaṃ ṇa *sajjham || 409 ||’
[darśayāmi tamapi śaśinaṃ vasudhāvatīrṇaṃ stabhnāmi tasyāpi rave rathaṃ nabho 'rdhe | ānayāmi yakṣasurasiddhagaṇāṅa‍ganāstannāsti bhūmivalaye mama yanna sādhyam ||]
vaihāsikaḥ krīḍanako viśvāsyaśca vidūṣakaḥ |

yathā—

‘phullukkaraṃ kalamakūrasamaṃ vahaṃti je siṃduvāraviḍavā maha vallahā de | je gālidassa mahisīdahiṇo saricchā *ruccaṃti muddhaviaïllapasūṇapuṃjā || 410 ||’
[puṣpotkaraṃ kalamabhaktasamaṃ vahanti ye sinduvāraviṭapā mama vallabhāste | ye gālitasya mahiṣīdadhnaḥ sadṛkṣā rocante mugdhavicakilaprasūnapuñjāḥ ||]
mānyaḥ kalatravānbhuktavibhavo guṇavānviṭaḥ || 170 ||
[page 694]

sa yathā—

‘śakāra kiṃ prārthanayā prāvāreṇāmiṣeṇa vā* | *akāryavarjaṃ me brūhi kimabhīṣṭaṃ *karomi te || 411 ||’

dhātreyakādiśceṭo yathā—

‘candrāpīḍo 'tha saṃjātapīḍaḥ kādambarīṃ prati | prāhiṇotsrastakeyūraḥ keyūrakamupasthitam || 412 ||’

patākāsu—

svātmopayoginyanyopayoginyanupayoginī | patāketyāpatāketi prakarīti prakīrtyate || 171 ||

tāsu patākā hanūmān yathā—

‘diṣṭyā so 'yaṃ mahābāhurañjanānandavardhanaḥ | yasya vīryeṇa kṛtino vayaṃ ca bhuvanāni ca || 413 ||’

āpatākāprakaryau mārīcajaṭāyuṣau yathā—

‘rakṣasā mṛgarūpeṇa vañcayitvā sa rāghavau | jahāra sītāṃ pakṣīndraprayāsakṣaṇavighnitaḥ || 414 ||’
sahajā pūrvajāgantuḥ sakhīha trividhocyate |

tāsu lavāṅgikādiḥ sahajā yathā—

‘ujjvalālokayā snigdhā tvayā tyaktā na rājate | malīmasamukhī vartiḥ pradīpaśikhayā yathā || 415 ||’

kāmandakyādiḥ pūrvajā yathā—

‘tathā vinayanamrāpi *mayā mālatyupāyataḥ | nītā *katipayāhobhiḥ sakhī visrambhasevyatām || 416 ||’
[page 695]

trijaṭādirāganturyathā—

‘jāṇaï siṇehabhaṇiaṃ mā raaṇiaritti me *juucchasu vaaṇam | ujjāṇammi *vaṇammi a jaṃ surahiṃ taṃ laāṇa *gheppaï kusumaṃ 417’
[jānaki snehabhaṇitaṃ mā rajanīcarīti me jugupsasva vacanam | udyāne vane ca yatsurabhi tallatānāṃ gṛhyate kusumam ||]

nāyakaguṇeṣu mahākulīnatvaṃ puṃso yathā—

‘vāsiṣṭhaiḥ sukṛtonadbhavo 'dhvaraśatairastyagnikuṇḍodbhavo bhūpālaḥ paramāra ityadhipatiḥ saptābdhikāñcerbhuvaḥ | adyāpyadbhutaharṣagadgadagiro gāyanti yasyedbhaṭaṃ viśvāmitrajayorjitasya bhujayorvisphūrjitaṃ gurjarāḥ* || 418 ||’

audāryaṃ yathā—

‘diṅmātaṅa‍gaghaṭāvibhaktacaturāghāṭā mahī sādhyate siddhā *sāpi vadanta eva hi vayaṃ romāñcitāḥ paśyata | viprāya pratipādyate kimaparaṃ rāmāya tasmai namo yasmādāvirabhūtkathādbhutamidaṃ yatraiva* cāstaṃ gatam || 419 ||’

mahābhāgyaṃ yathā—

‘*dorniṣpeṣaviśīrṇavajraśakalapratyuptarūḍhavraṇa- granthyudbhāsini bhagnamoghamaghavanmātaṅa‍gadantodyame | bharturnandanadevatāviracitasragdāmni bhūmeḥ sutā vīraśrīriva tasya vakṣasi jagadvīrasya viśrāmyatu || 420 ||’
[page 696]

kṛtajñatā yathā—

‘kṛtakakupitairbāṣpāmbhobhiḥ sadainyavilokitai- rvanamasi gatā yasya prītyā dhṛtāpi tathāmbayā | navajalasadharaśyāmāḥ paśyandiśo bhavatīṃ vinā kaṭhinahṛdayo jīvatyeva priye sa kava priyaḥ || 421 ||’

rūpasaṃpad yathā—

‘vyụ̄dhorasko vṛṣaskandhaḥ śālaprāṃśurmahābhujaḥ | ātmakarmakṣamaṃ dehaṃ kṣāttro dharma ivāśritaḥ* || 422 ||’

yauvanasaṃpad yathā—

‘mahokṣatāṃ vatsataraḥ spṛśānniva dvipendrabhāvaṃ kalabhaḥ śrayanniva | raghuḥ kramādyauvanabhinnaśaiśavaḥ pupoṣa gambhīramanoharaṃ vapuḥ || 423 ||’

vaidagdhyasaṃpad yathā—

‘ko 'yaṃ bhāmini bhūṣaṇaṃ kitava te śoṇaḥ kathaṃ kuṅkumā- tkūrpāsāntaritaḥ priye vinimayaḥ paśyāparaṃ *kvāsti me | paśyāmītyabhidhāya sāndrapulakau mṛdnanmṛḍānyāḥ stanau hastena pratinirjitenduravatādda‍yūte hasanvo haraḥ || 424 ||’

śīlasaṃpad yathā—

‘kā tvaṃ śubhe kasya parigraho vā kiṃ vā madabhyāgamakāraṇaṃ te | ācakṣva matvā vaśināṃ raghūṇāṃ manaḥ parastrīvimukhapravṛtti || 425 ||’

saubhāgyasaṃpad yathā—

‘asau vidyādhāraḥ śiśurapi vinirgatya bhavanādihāyātaḥ saṃpratyavikalaśaraccandramadhuraḥ |[page 697] yadālokasthāne bhavati puramunmādataralaiḥ kaṭākṣairnārīṇāṃ kuvalayitavātāyanamiva || 426 ||’

mānitā yathā—

‘yadāttha kāmaṃ bhavatā sa yācyatā- miti kṣamaṃ naitadanalpacetasām | kathaṃ prasahyāharaṇaiṣiṇāṃ priyāḥ *parānuvṛttyā malinīkṛtāḥ śriyaḥ || 427 ||’

udāravākyatvaṃ yathā—

‘*khyātā eva vayaṃ jagatsu caritairvāgbhiḥ kimākhyāyate saṃyatto bhava *śaktirasti bhavataḥ satyaṃ manuṣyo bhavān | śastrairavyavadhīyamānayaśasaḥ* prāyo vayaṃ teṣu ce- tprāhuste nanu santi* te 'pi girayo yairvānarāḥ śastriṇaḥ || 428’

sthirānurāgitā yathā—

‘tataḥ kairapyukte pariṇayavidhau kāṣṭhamunibhiḥ purāṇairataṅa‍kaglapitahṛdayena kṣitibhṛtā | vinā vācaṃ naitatkṣamamiti* nidhāyānanamadhaḥ patadbāṣpāmbhobhirnikhilamiva dattaṃ prativacaḥ || 429 ||’

nāyikāguṇeṣu striyā mahākulinatā yathā—

‘*mānuṣīṣu kathaṃ vā syādasya rūpasya saṃbhavaḥ | na prabhātaralaṃ jyotirudeti vasudhātalāt || 430 ||’
[page 698]

audāryaṃ yathā—

‘*bhrūbhede sahasodgate 'pi* vadanaṃ nītaṃ parāṃ namratā- mīṣanmāṃ prati bhedakāri hasitaṃ noktaṃ vaco niṣṭhuram | antarbāṣpajalīkṛtaṃ* prabhutayā cakṣurna visphāritaṃ kopaśca prakaṭīkṛto dayitayā muktaśca na *pratyayaḥ || 431 ||’

mahābhāgyaṃ yathā—

‘tāṃ nāradaḥ kāmacaraḥ kadācitkanyāṃ kila prekṣya pituḥ samīpe | samādideśaikavadhūṃ bhavitrīṃ premṇā śarīrārdhaharāṃ harasya || 432 ||’

kṛtajñatā yathā—

‘purisasarisaṃ tuha imaṃ rakkhasasarisaṃ *kaaṃ ṇisāaravaïṇā | kaha tā *ciṃtijjaṃtaṃ* mahilāsarisaṃ ṇa saṃpaḍaï me maraṇaṃ || 433 ||’
[puruṣasadṛśaṃ tavedaṃ rākṣasasadṛśaṃ kṛtaṃ niśācarapatinā | kathaṃ tāvaccintitasulabhaṃ mahilāsadṛśaṃ na saṃpadyate me maraṇam ||]

rūpasaṃpad yathā—

‘ābharaṇasyābharaṇaṃ prasādhanavidheḥ prasādhanaviśeṣaḥ | upamānasyāpi sakhe pratyupamānaṃ vapustasyāḥ || 434 ||’

yauvanasaṃpad yathā—

‘unmīlitaṃ tūlikayeva citraṃ sūryāṃśubhirbhinnamivāravindam | babhūva tasyāścaturasraśobhi vapurvibhaktaṃ navayauvanena || 435 ||’

vaidagdhyasaṃpad yathā—

‘ekatrāsanasaṃsthitiḥ parihṛtā pratyudgamāddūrata- *stāmbūlānayanacchalena rabhasāśleṣo 'pi saṃvighnitaḥ | [page 699] ālāpo 'pi na miśritaḥ parijanaṃ vyāpārayantyāntike kāntaṃ *pratyupacārataścaturayā kopaḥ kṛtārthīkṛtaḥ || 436 ||’

śīlasampad yathā—

‘*cattaraghariṇī piadaṃsaṇā a *bālā paütthavaïā* a | *asaī saajjhiā duggaā a ṇa hu khaṃḍiaṃ sīlam || 437 ||’
[catvaragṛhiṇī priyadarśanā ca bālā proṣitapatikā ca | asatī prativeśinī durgatā ca na khalu khaṇḍitaṃ śīlam ||]

saubhāgyasampad yathā—

‘saṃcāriṇī dīpaśikheva rātrau yaṃ yaṃ vyatīyāya patiṃvarā sā | narendramārgāṭṭa iva prapede vivarṇabhāvaṃ sa sa bhūmipālaḥ || 438 ||’

mānitā yathā—

‘śailātmajāpi piturucchiraso 'bhilāṣaṃ vyarthaṃ samarthya lalitaṃ vapurātmanaśca | sakhyoḥ samakṣamiti cādhikajātalajjā śūnyā jagāma bhavanābhimukhaṃ kathaṃcit || 439 ||’

udāravākyatvaṃ yathā—

‘yathā śrutaṃ vedavidāṃ vara tvayā jano 'yamuccaiḥ padalaṅa‍ghanotsukaḥ | [page 700] tapaḥ kiledaṃ tadavāptisādhanaṃ manorathānāmagatirna vidyate || 440 ||’

sthirānurāgitā yathā—

‘alaṃ vivādena yathā śrutaṃ tvayā* tathāvidhastāvadaśeṣamastu saḥ | mamātra bhāvaikarasaṃ manaḥ sthitaṃ na kāmavṛttirvacanīyamīkṣate || 441 ||’

pākabhaktiṣu ādāvasvādu, ante svādu mṛdvīkāpākaṃ yathā—

‘prākkāmaṃ dahatā kṛtaḥ paribhavo yenātha *saṃdhyāvatau serṣyā vo 'vatu caṇḍikā caraṇayostaṃ pātayantī patim | *kurvantyābhyadhikaṃ kṛte pratikṛtaṃ muktena maulau muhu- *rbāṣpeṇāhṛtakajjalena likhitaṃ lakṣmeva candre yathā || 442’ ||

ādyantayoḥ svādu nārikelīpākaṃ* yathā—

‘jaha icchā taha ramiaṃ jāā pattā *païṃ gaā dhūā | gharasāmiassa* ajja vi *sakouhallāiṁ acchīiṃ || 443 ||’
[yathecchā tathā ramitaṃ jāyā prāptā patiṃ gatā duhitā | gṛhasvāmino 'dyāpi sakautūhalānyakṣīṇi ||]

ādimadhyānteṣu svādu svādutaraṃ svādutamamityāmrapākaṃ yathā—

‘śāpādasi pratihatā smṛtiloparūkṣe* bhartaryapetatamasi* prabhutā tavaiva | [page 701] chāyā na mūrcchati malopahataprasāde śuddhe tu darpaṇatale sulabhāvakāśā || 444 ||’

yannāpaiti na cātiśobhate tannīlīrāgaṃ yathā—

‘*hītvā sītāṃ daśamukharipurnopayeme yadanyāṃ tasyā evaṃ pratikṛtisakho yatkratūnājahāra | vṛttāntena śravaṇaviṣayaprāpiṇā tena bhartuḥ sā *durvāravyathamapi parityāgaduḥkhaṃ viṣehe || 445 ||’

*yadapaiti ca śobhate ca tatkusumbharāgaṃ yathā—

‘vahuvallahassa jā hoi vallahā kaha vi paṃcadiahāiṃ | sā kiṃ chaṭṭhaṃ *maggaï katto *miṭṭhaṃ ca bahuaṃ ca* || 446 ||’
[bahuvallabhasya yā bhavati vallabhā kathaṃ kathamapi paścadivasāni | sā kiṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ mārgate kuto mṛṣṭaṃ ca bahukaṃ ca ||]

*yannāpaityati ca śobhate tanmañjiṣṭhārāgaṃ yathā—

‘vevaï jassa saviḍiaṃ valiuṃ mahaï pulaāiatthaṇaalasaṃ | pemmasahāvavimuhiaṃ *vīovāsagamaṇūsuaṃ vāmaddham || 447 ||’
[vepate yasya savrīḍaṃ valituṃ vāñchati pulakāñcitastanakalaśam | premasvabhāvavimuktaṃ dvitīyapārśvagamanotsukaṃ vāmārdham ||]
[page 702]

gūḍhavyalīkamantarvyājaṃ yathā—

‘pratyagrojjhitagokulasya śayanādutsvapnamūḍhasya me sā gotraskhalanādapaitu ca divā rādheti bhīroriti | rātrāvasvapato divā ca vijane *lakṣmīti cābhyasyato rādhāṃ prasmarataḥ śriyaṃ ramayataḥ khedo hareḥ pātu vaḥ 448’

agūḍhavyalīkaṃ bahirvyājaṃ yathā—

‘cakṣuryasya tavānanādapagataṃ nābhūtkvacinnirvṛtaṃ yenaiṣā satataṃ tvadekaśayanaṃ vakṣaḥsthalī kalpitā | yenoktāsi vinā tvayā mama jagacchūnyaṃ kṣaṇājjāyate so 'yaṃ dambhadhṛtavrataḥ priyatamaḥ kartuṃ kimapyudyataḥ* || 449 ||’

*avyalīkaṃ nirvyājaṃ yathā—

‘kiṃ kaṇṭhe śithilīkṛto bhujalatāpāśaḥ pramādānmayā *nidrācchedavivartaneṣvabhimukhī nādyāpi saṃbhāvitā* | anyastrījanasaṃkathālaghurahaṃ svapne tvayā lakṣito* doṣaṃ paśyasi kaṃ* priye parijanopālambhayogye mayi || 450 ||’

dharmānubandhi *dharmodarkaṃ yathā—

‘atha sa viṣayavyāvṛttātmā yathāvidhi sūnave nṛpatikakudaṃ datvā yūne sitātapavāraṇam | munivanatarucchāyāṃ devyā tayā saha śiśriye galitavayasāmikṣvākūṇāmidaṃ hi kulavratam || 451 ||’
[page 703]

arthānubandhi arthodarkaṃ yathā—

‘bhūtvā cirāya caturantamahīsapatnī* *dauṣyantimapratirathaṃ tanayaṃ prasūya* | *martrā tadarpitakuṭumbabhareṇa sārdhaṃ śānte kariṣyasi padaṃ punarāśrame 'smin || 452 ||’

yatpunaḥ kāmamevānubadhnāti tatkāmodarkaṃ yathā—

‘advaitaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoranuguṇaṃ* sarvāsvavasthāsu ya- dvisrambho* hṛdayasya yatra jarasā yasminnahāryo rasaḥ | kālenāvaraṇātyayā*tpariṇate yatsnehasāre* sthitaṃ *bhadraṃ tasya sumānuṣasya kathamapyekaṃ hi yatprāpyate* || 453 ||’

‘nānālaṃkārasaṃsṛṣṭeḥ *prakārāśca rasoktayaḥ |

ityuktaṃ tatra ‘alaṃkārasaṃsṛṣṭeḥ’ itīyatyeva* vaktavye nānālaṃkāragrahaṇaṃ* guṇarasānāmupasaṃgrahārtham | teṣāmapi hi kāvyaśobhākaratvenālaṃkāratvāt || yadāha—

kāvyaśobhākarāndharmānalaṃkārānpracakṣate | te cādyāpi vikalpyante kastānkārtsnyena vakṣyati ||
kāścinmārgavibhāgārthamuktāḥ prāgapyalaṃkriyāḥ | sādhāraṇamalaṃkārajā*tamanyat pradarśyate ||
[page 704]

tatra ‘kāvyaśobhākarān’ ityanena śleṣopamādivadguṇarasabhāvatadābhāsapraśamā*dīnapyupagṛhṇāti* | mārgavibhāgaṃkṛdguṇānāmalaṃkriyopadeśena śleṣādīnāṃ guṇatvamivālaṃkāratvamapi jñāpayati—

śleṣaḥ prasādaḥ samatā mādhuryaṃ sukumāratā | arthavyaktirudāratvamojaḥkāntisamādhayaḥ ||
iti vaidarbhamārgasya prāṇā daśa guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ | teṣāṃ viparyayaḥ prāyo *lakṣyate gauḍavartmani ||

iti śleṣādīnāṃ daśānāmeva *mārgapravibhāgakāritāṃ bruvankāvyaśobhākaratvena guṇāntarāṇāmapyalaṃkāratvamupakalpayati || tadāha, ‘kastānkārtsnyena *vakṣyati’ | yuktamidamuktam | ayuktaṃ tvidamuktaṃ rasānāmalaṃkārateti ||

teṣāṃ guṇānāmivālaṃkāravyapadeśābhāvāt | nāyuktam | *yuktotkarṣāṇāmūrjasvirasava*tpreyasāmalaṃkāreṣūpadeśāt | tad yathā—

preyaḥ priyatarākhyānaṃ rasavad rasapeśalam | ūrjasvi rụ̄dhāhaṃkāraṃ yuktotkarṣaṃ ca tattrayam || 172 ||

tatrorjasvi rụ̄dhāhaṃkāramityanena ātmaviśeṣaniṣṭhasyotkṛṣṭā*dṛṣṭajanmano 'nekajanmānubhava*saṃskārāhitadrạdhimnaḥ *saṃgrāme guṇasaṃpadutpādātiśayahetoralaṃkāra*viśeṣasyopasaṃgrahādahaṃkārābhimānaśrṛṅa‍gārāparanāmno rasasya mānamayavikārarūpeṇābhimānināṃ manasi jāgrataḥ parāṃ koṭimupavarṇayati | rasa-[page 705] vadrasapeśalamityanena vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisāttvikasaṃyogādrasaniṣpattiriti ratyādirūpeṇānekadhāvirbhavato 'bhivardhamānasya* paraprakarṣagāminaḥ śrṛṅa‍gārasya *madhyāvasthāṃ sūcayati | preyaḥ *priyatarākhyānamityanena samastabhāvamūrdhābhiṣiktāyā rateḥ *paraprakarṣādhigamād *bhāvanādhigame bhāvarūpatāmullaṅa‍ghya premarūpeṇa *pariṇatāyā upādānād bhāvāntarāṇāmapi paraprakarṣādhigame rasarūpeṇa pariṇatiriti *jñāpayannahaṃkārasyottarāṃ koṭimupalakṣayati | sarveṣāmapi hi ratyādiprakarṣāṇāṃ ratipriyo raṇapriyaḥ parihāsapriyo 'marṣapriya iti *premṇayeva paryavasānaṃ bhavati | yuktotkarṣaṃ ca tat trayamityanenāyuktotkarṣāṇāṃ trayāṇāmapyūrjasviprabhṛtīnāṃ guṇatvameva nālaṃkāratvamityavasthāpayati | tathā hi—aurjityaṃ bhāvikatvaṃ* preya iti guṇeṣūpadiśyate,* kutaḥ punaridamekadorjasvi—rasavat—preyasāmalaṃkāratvamanyadā guṇatvam* |

ucyate—

bhūmanindāpraśaṃsāsu nityayoge 'tiśāyane | saṃsarge 'stivivakṣāyāṃ bhavanti matubādayaḥ ||

yathā gomān deśaḥ, vācālo baṭuḥ, vāgmī vipaścit, *kṣīriṇo vṛkṣāḥ, balavān mallaḥ* daṇḍī, gomatī *śāleti | tatrorjasvirasavatoralaṃkāratvavivakṣāyāmatiśāyane* bhūmni vā *matvarthīyaḥ | guṇatvavivakṣāyāṃ tu [page 706] praśaṃsānityayoriti yogayoriti draṣṭavyam | nityo hi kāvye guṇayoga iva rasādiyogaḥ | guṇavato rasavataśca niścitaivāsya praśaṃsā | saṃsargastu guṇānāmavaśyamupādāneṣu | nindā punardoṣahānernāvatarati* | guṇeṣu *preya iti rūpābhedāt kathamalaṃkāratve tadutkarṣapratītiḥ | yathā ‘yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śreṣṭhatamaḥ kurūṇām’ iti tatrātiśāyikāntareṇa* tadavagatiriti cet ihāpi ‘yuktotkarṣaṃ ca tattrayam’ iti vākyāntareṇa bhaviṣyati | na cātiśāyikā svārthātiriktaṃ kimapi bruvate, api tu prakṛtyupāttameva prakarṣādikaṃ gamayanti | svārthikeṣu hyete vidhīyante | evamavasthāpite guṇarasānāmalaṃkāratve *ṣaṭprakāro rasālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ saṃbhavati—guṇasaṃkaraḥ, alaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ, guṇālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ, rasasaṃkaraḥ, rasaguṇasaṃkaraḥ, *rasālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ iti | *nanu ca guṇānāṃ saṃkaravyavahāro nopapadyate bahuṣvapi guṇeṣu guṇavadityeva vyapadeśāt | maivam | trividhā guṇāḥ—śabdaguṇāḥ, arthaguṇāḥ, doṣaguṇāśca | te tu pratyekaṃ dvidhā—ullekhavantaḥ, nirullekhāśca | tatra śabdaguṇeṣu samādhimādhuryaudāryagāmbhīryādayaḥ sollekhāḥ, śleṣaprasādasamatā*mādhuryādayo nirullekhāḥ | arthaguṇeṣu prasādarītikāntyādayaḥ sollekhāḥ, arthavyaktisaukṣmya*gāmbhīryasaṃmitatvādayo nirullekhāḥ | doṣaguṇeṣu grāmyapunaruktāpārthānyārthādayaḥ sollekhāḥ, śabdahīnasaṃbhramāpakramaviṃsandhyādayo nirullekhāḥ | tatra sajātīyānāṃ sollekhānāmevaṃ, *vijātīyānāṃ tu nirullekhānāmapi saṃkaravyavahāraḥ pravartate ||

[page 707]

sajātīyānāṃ śabdaguṇeṣu samādhyādīnāṃ yathā—

‘ṇavapallavesu lolaï gholaï *viḍavesu valaï siharesu | thavaï thavaesu a *tahā vasaṃtalacchī asoassa || 455 ||’
[navapallaveṣu lolati ghūrṇate viṭapeṣu valate śikhareṣu | sthagati stabakeṣu ca tathā vasantalakṣmīraśokasya ||]

atrānyadharmāṇāmanyatrāropaṇaṃ samādhiḥ pṛthakpadatā mādhuryaṃ, *bandhavikaṭatvamudāratā, *dhvanimattā, gāmbhīryamiti sajātīyāḥ saṃkīryante | yato vasantalakṣmīraśokasyeti padayoḥ śabdadhvanirapi parisphurati | yathā kasyacidaśokasya mānino 'ṅa‍geṣu priyāṅa‍ganā savilāsaṃ ceṣṭate tathāsyeyamiti ||

*arthaguṇeṣu śleṣādīnāṃ yathā—

‘janaḥ puṇyairyāyājjaladhijalabhāvaṃ jalamuca- stathāvasthaṃ cainaṃ nidadhatu *śubhaiḥ śuktivadane | tatastāṃ śreyobhiḥ pariṇatimasau vindatu *yayā ruciṃ tanvanpīnastani hṛdi tavāyaṃ viluṭhati || 456 ||’

atra *saṃvidhāne susūtratā śleṣaḥ, arthasya prākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ, utpattyādikriyākramo rītiḥ dīptarasatvaṃ kāntirityarthaguṇāḥ sajātīyāḥ saṃkīryante ||

doṣaguṇeṣu *grāmyādīnāṃ yathā—

‘hanyate sā varārohā smareṇākāṇḍavairiṇā | hanyate cārusarvāṅa‍gī hanyate mañjubhāṣiṇī || 457 ||’

atra hanyata *ityamaṅa‍galārtham, varārohetyaślīlārtham, *hanyate hanyata [page 708]iti punaruktam, cārusarvāṅa‍gītyuktvā *varāroheti vyartham, ta ete sajātīyāścatvāro 'pi doṣaguṇāḥ saṃkīryamāṇāḥ kasyacidunmattabhāṣiṇo 'nukampādyatiśayavivakṣāyāmabhyanujñāyante || yadāha—

*anukampādyatiśayo yadi kaścidvivakṣyate* | na doṣaḥ punaruktādau pratyuteyamalaṃkriyā ||

*arthāsajātīyānāṃ śabdaguṇānāmarthaguṇānāṃ ca saṃkaro yathā—

‘ko nāma nodayati nāstamupaiti ko vā lokottaraḥ punarayaṃ savitā jagatsu | yatrodayāstamayabhāji rucāṃ nidhāne dvedhā bhavatyahariti kṣaṇadeti kālaḥ || 458 ||’

atra yāvadarthapadatā *saṃmitatvam, samyagbandhavikaṭatvamudāratā, *ślādhyaviśeṣaguṇayoga udāttatvamiti śabdaguṇāḥ, uktārthanirvahaṇaṃ praụdhiḥ, arthaprākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ, rụ̄dhāhaṃkārataurjityamityarthaguṇāḥ saṃkīryante ||

śabdaguṇānāṃ doṣaguṇānāṃ ca yathā—

‘ehyehi vatsa raghunandana pūrṇacandra cumbāmi mūrdhani *ciraṃ ca pariṣvaje tvām | āropya vā hṛdi divāniśamudvahāmi vande 'thavā caraṇapuṣkarakadvayaṃ te || 459 ||

atra bhāvato *vākpravṛttirbhāvikatvam, prasiddhārthapadatā prasādaḥ, *priyārthapadopādānaṃ preya iti śabdaguṇāḥ, ehyehīti punaruktam, vatse-[page 709]tyuktvā tvatpādābjadvayaṃ vanda iti viruddham, mūrdhni cumbāmi hṛdi vahāmītyādau vanda iti kriyāsvanupayogāt *pūrṇacandretidarśanādikriyopayogi vyarthaṃ ceti *doṣaguṇāḥ saṃkīryante | rasākṣiptacittādau hi punaruktādayo *na duṣyanti ||

arthaguṇānāṃ doṣaguṇānāṃ yathā—

‘kiṃ dvāri daivahatike sahakārakeṇa saṃvardhitena viṣapādapa eṣa pāpaḥ | asminmanāgapi vikāsavikārabhāji bhīmā bhavanti madanajvarasaṃnipātāḥ || 460 ||’

atra dīptarasatvaṃ kāntiḥ, arthaprākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ, uktārthanirvahaṇaṃ praụdhirityarthaguṇāḥ, daivahatike viṣapādapo 'yaṃ pāpa ityamaṅa‍galārthaṃ grāmyaṃ, kimanena saṃvardhitenetyatra madanajvarasaṃnipātā ityatra ca kṛtyaprayojanādervirahiṇo draṣṭurityādeścādhyāhārādasaṃpūrṇavākyatāyāmarthavyaktiviparyayaḥ | asminvikāsavikārabhājīti vikāsaśabdasya puṣpaviṣayatvādvṛkṣe 'pi prayogo 'vācakatvādasamartha iti doṣaguṇā mithaḥ saṃkīryante | yato rasākṣepātparihāsaleśoktyāmaṅa‍galam, praviśa piṇḍīṃ dvāraṃ bhakṣaya iti nyāyātprasiddhādhyāhāraḥ, ‘darī vadati, mañcāḥ krośantī’ ti prayogadarśanādādhārādheyayorabhedopacāraśca viruddhalakṣaṇādibhiḥ prayujyamāno na doṣāyeti ||

athālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ |
