sa yadyapi vyaktāvyaktobhayātmatayā tilataṇḍulakādibhedaiḥ pradhānāṅa‍gabhāvasamakakṣatābhyāṃ purastāduktaḥ tathāpi teṣāṃ guṇādisaṃkarāsādhāraṇa-[page 710]tvātsaṃprati sādhāraṇaḥ prakāra ucyate | sa ṣọdhā śabdālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ, arthālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ, ubhayālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ śabdārthālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ, *śabdārthobhayālaṃkārasaṃkaraḥ, arthobhayālaṃkārasaṃkaraśca* | teṣu śabdālaṃkārasaṃkaro yathā—

*haṃsālī bhayataralā sārā sarasā sarāsasārasarāsā* | *ambaramaramārụ̄dhā sārāsarasā sarāsasārasarāsā ||

atra saṃskṛtaprākṛtabhāṣāsaṃśleṣaḥ, gatapratyāgataṃ citraṃ, *padāvṛttiyamakaṃ, varṇānuprāsaśceti catvāraḥ *śabdālaṃkārāḥ saṃkīryante ||

arthālaṃkārasaṃkaro yathā—

‘vāsāvasthitatāmracūḍavayasāmāyāmibhiḥ kūjitairdūrādapyanumīyamānavasatirgrāmo 'yamantarvaṇam | yatroddīptakukūla*kūṭavisarajjhampāghanaṃ ghūrṇate sandhyāntollasadacchabhallapaṭalacchāyājaṭālaṃ tamaḥ || 461 ||’

atra tāmracūḍavayasāṃ kūjitairityanumānam, yatra tamo ghūrṇata iti jñāpakahetuḥ, kukūlakūṭavisarajjhampāghanamiti sandhyāntollasadacchabhallapaṭa-[page 711] lacchāyājaṭālamiti ca kārakahetuḥ, jāyamānapadārthasvarūpābhidhānaṃ jātirityarthālaṃkārāścatvāro mithaḥ saṃkīryante ||

ubhayālaṃkārasaṃkaro yathā—

‘ṇa hu ṇavaraṃ dīvasihāsāricchaṃ* caṃpaehiṃ* paḍivaṇṇam | kajjalakajjaṃ ri *kaaṃ *uari bhamantehiṁ bhamarehiṁ || 462 ||’
[na khalu kevalaṃ dīpaśikhāsādṛśyaṃ campakaiḥ pratipannam | kajjalakāryamapi kṛtamupari bhramadbhirbhramaraiḥ ||]

atra campakādīnāṃ pradīpaśikhābhirākārakāntibhyāmupamā,* virahiṇīhṛdayadāhodyā*nadyotanārthakriyābhyāṃ sāmyaṃ, *kajjalapaṭalānāmiva bhramarapaṭalānāmupari melanānmelitaṃ, campakadīpakalikayoriva bhramarakajjalapaṭalayoraupamyādisaṃbandhātsamuccaya ityubhayālaṃkārāścatvāro* mithaḥ saṃkīryamāṇā upalabhyante ||

śabdārthālaṃkārasaṃkaro yathā—

‘sarvāśārudhi *dagdhavīrudhi *sadā sāraṅa‍gabaddhakrudhi kṣāmakṣmāruhi mandamunmadhulihi svacchandakandadruhi* | śuṣyatsrotasi *taptabhūmirajasi jvālāyamānāmbhasi *grīṣme māsi kharārkatejasi kathaṃ pāntha vrajañjīvasi || 463 ||’

atrāvantikā rītiḥ, padamudrā, vibhaktimudrā, anuprāsaśceti śabdā-﻿[page 712]laṃkārāḥ, jātiḥ, *kārakajñāpakau hetū, citrahetuścetyarthālaṃkārā *mithaḥ saṃkīryante |

*śabdobhayālaṃkārasaṃkaro yathā—

‘stokastokamamūbhirambaratale tārābhirastaṃ gataṃ gacchatyastagireḥ śirastadanu ca cchāyādaridraḥ śaśī | pratyāsannatarodayasya taraṇerbimbāruṇimnā tato mañjiṣṭhārasalohinī digapi ca prācī samunmīlati || 464 ||’

atra samunmīlatīti vibhaktimudrā, stokastokamastaṃ gataṃ* gacchatītyādiranuprāsaśca śabdālaṃkārāḥ, hetūpamā, samādhiḥ, anukramaḥ, samuccayoktiścetyubhayālaṃkārā mithaḥ saṃkīryante ||

arthobhayālaṃkārasaṃkaro yathā—

‘khaṃ vaste kalaviṅa‍kakaṇṭhamalinaṃ kādambinīkambalaṃ *carcāṃ pārayatīva dardurakulaṃ kolāhalairunmadam | gandhaṃ muñcati siktalā*jasurabhiṃ varṣeṇa dagdhā sthalī durlakṣyo 'pi vibhāvyate kamalinīhāsena bhāsāṃ patiḥ || 465 ||’

atra jātiḥ, anumānam, kārakajñāpakahetū cetyarthālaṃkārāḥ, rūpakopamā, hetūpamā, utprekṣopameti *cobhayālaṃkārā mithaḥ saṃkīryante ||

etena guṇālaṃkārasaṃkaro 'pi vyākhyātaḥ | *yato yadyapi guṇavatyeva vākye 'laṃkā*rayogastathāpi kvacid guṇasya prādhānyaṃ kvacidalaṃkārasyeti pradhānāṅa‍gabhāvena guṇālaṃkārayoḥ saṃkaravyavahāraḥ pravartate | sa ṣọdhā—śabda-[page 713]guṇapradhānaḥ, arthaguṇapradhānaḥ, *doṣaguṇapradhānaḥ, śabdālaṃkārapradhānaḥ, arthālaṃkārapradhānaḥ, ubhayālaṃkārapradhānaśca* ||

teṣu śabdaguṇapradhāno yathā—

‘prāptaśrīreṣa kasmātpunarapi *mayi taṃ manthakhedaṃ vidadhyānnidrāmapyasya pūrvāmanalasamanaso naiva* saṃbhāvayāmi | setuṃ badhnāti bhūyaḥ kimiti ca sakaladvīpanāthānuyātastvayyāyāte vitarkāniti dadhata* ivābhāti kampaḥ payodheḥ 466’

atra hetūtprekṣābhidhāne tvayītyādau pade viṣṇoḥ svarūpādhyāsena tadbhāvāpattau samādheriha prādhānyaṃ* pratīyate | nanu cāyamarthasya prākaṭyātprasādo 'rthaguṇaḥ kasmānna bhavati | asminnapi tavdyapadeśena śabdaśakterādhikyāt | nanu ca tvayi iti, eṣa iti, asya iti, *yuṣmadetadidamāṃ na kaścana* viṣṇuvācī *sa kathaṃ varṇanīye nyastastaṃ tamarthamabhidadhīta | ucyate, sarvanāmatvenaiṣāṃ sarvavācitvāt | sarvanāmāni hi *sarvābhidhāyīnyapi *prakaraṇādigamyaṃ viśeṣameva bruvate sa ca iha prāptaśrīrityevamādimirabhivyakta*mevāvagamyata iti ||

arthaguṇapradhāno yathā—

‘lakṣmīvaśīkaraṇacūrṇasahodarāṇi tvatpādapaṅa‍kajarajāṃsi ciraṃ jayanti | [page 714] yāni praṇāmamilitāni nṛṇāṃ lalāṭe * lumpanti daivalikhitāni durakṣarāṇi || 467 ||

*atra hetusāmyobhayālaṃkārābhidhāne 'pi prādhānyenārthaprākaṭyamarthaguṇaḥ pratīyate ||

doṣaguṇapradhāno yathā—

‘yenāpaviddhasalilasphuṭanāgasadmā devāsurairamṛtamambunidhirmamanthe | vyāvartanairahipaterayamāhitāṅa‍kaḥ khaṃ vyālikhanniva vibhāti sa mandarādriḥ || 468 ||’

atra ‘vyāvartanairahipaterayamāhitāṅa‍kaḥ’ iti jñāpakahetoḥ ‘khaṃ vyālikhanniva’ iti utprekṣāvayavācca, devāsurairiti *nityavairāvivakṣāyāṃ bahuvacanam, ‘amṛtamambunidhirmamanthe’ iti dvikarmakeṣvapi mathiprabhṛtīnāmupasaṃkhyānamiti amṛtaśabdāddvitīyā iti doṣaguṇayoḥ prādhānyaṃ pratīyate | nanu cātrārthasya *prādhānyaṃ kathaṃ bhavati tadviṣayasya jñāpakahetunāpahṛtatvātso 'pyarthālaṃkāra eva | guṇālaṃkārayośca tulyakakṣatāyāmalaṃkāraḥ pradhānaṃ bhavati na guṇaḥ | guṇairhi guṇabhūtairevālaṃkārāḥ prāya ārabhyante | tadyathā—

‘aspṛṣṭā doṣamātrābhiḥ samagraguṇagumphitā | vipañcīsvarasaubhāgyā vaidarbhī rītiripyate |
*samastātyudbhaṭapadāmojaḥkāntisamanvitām | *gauḍīyeti vijānanti rītiṃ rītivicakṣaṇāḥ ||
[page 715]
āśliṣṭaṃ ślathabhāvāṃ tu purāṇacchāyamāśritām | madhurāṃ *sukumārāṃ ca pāñcālīṃ kavayo viduḥ ||
mādhuryamapi vāñchanta; prasādaṃ ca subhedhasaḥ | samāsavanti bhūyāṃsi na padāni prayuñjate ||
lāṭīyāvantyayo rītyormāgadhyāṃ ca kvacitkvacit | kecidojo 'bhidhitsantaḥ samasyanti bahūnyapi ||
pratītaśabdamojasvi *suśliṣṭapadasaṃdhi ca | prasādi svabhidhānaṃ ca yamakaṃ kṛtinā matam* ||’ iti |

mā bhūdalaṃkāratulyakakṣatayā arthasya prādhānyaṃ* śabdaguṇasya tu ślāghyaviśeṣaguṇayoga udāttamityādeḥ kimiti prādhānyaṃ na bhavati doṣaguṇānāmatīvollekhavattvena* prādhānyāt* ||

*sā vāmanaprasiddhirlaṅghitanabhaso balidviṣo 'dyāpi | matsariṇaḥ khalu lokā marmāṇyevānubadhnanti ||

doṣasya yo guṇībhāvaḥ sa tato 'pyadhikaṃ prakāśata iti ||

śabdālaṃkāraprādhāno yathā—

‘yaccandrakoṭikarakorakabhārabhāji* babhrāma babhruṇi jaṭāpaṭale harasya | tadvaḥ punātu himaśailaśilānikuñjajhā- *tkāraḍambaravirāvi surāpagāmbhaḥ || 469 ||’
[page 716]

atrārthaprākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ vibhavotkarṣa udāttatā mṛduprasphuṭonmiśravarṇānāmavaiṣamyaṃ samatā, bandhagāḍhatā, aurjityamityādibhyo guṇebhyaḥ prādhānyena śabdālaṃkārānuprāsaḥ pratīyate ||

arthālaṃkārapradhāno yathā—

‘āśleṣiṇaḥ *pṛthutaraklamapītaśītamāyāvinīrghanamudo rajanīryuvānaḥ | *ūrdhvormuhurvalanabandhanasandhilolapādāntasaṃvalitatūlapaṭāḥ* svapanti || 470 ||’

atra bandhavikaṭatvamudāratā, ślādhyaviśeṣaṇayoga udāttatvam*, vibhavotkarṣa audāryam, dīptarasatvam, kāntirityādibhyo guṇebhyaḥ prādhānyena jātirarthālaṃkāraḥ pratīyate |

ubhayālaṃkārapradhāno yathā—

‘*abhyuddhṛtā vasumatī dalitaṃ ripūraḥ kroḍīkṛtā balavatā balirājalakṣmīḥ | atraikajanmani kṛtaṃ yadanena yūnā janmatraye tadakarotpuruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ || 471 ||’

atroktiparipāṭīḥ* praụdhiḥ, bandhavikaṭatvamudāratā, āśayotkarṣa udāttatvam, arthaprākaṭyaṃ, prasādaḥ—ityādibhyo guṇebhyaḥ śleṣopasarjanā viśeṣoktirubhayālaṃkāraḥ prādhānyena pratīyate || rasasaṃkaro 'pi cālaṃkārasaṃkaravadeva | bhāvarasābhāsapraśamānāṃ tilataṇḍulādiprakāreṇa saṃkaraḥ *ṣaṭprakārako bhavati | tatra bhāvānāṃ tilataṇḍulaprakāro yathā—

[page 717]
‘nyakkāro hṛdi vajrakīla iva me tīvraḥ parispandate ghīrāndhe tamasīva majjati manaḥ saṃmīlitaṃ lajjayā | *śokastārkṣyavipattito *dahati māṃ nāstyeva yasminkriyā *marmāṇyeva punaśchinatti karuṇā sītāṃ varākīṃ prati || 472 ||’

atrāmarṣalajjāśokānukampāḥ samakakṣatayā mithastilataṇḍulavatsaṃkīryamāṇā rāmasya virahiṇo vāgārambhānubhā*voktiparatayā pratīyante ||

kṣīranīraprakāro yathā—

‘mānonnatetyasahanetyatipaṇḍiteti mayyeva dhikkṛtiranekamukhī sakhīnām | dākṣiṇyamātramasṛṇena viceṣṭitena dhūrtasya tasya hi guṇā nu paraṃ jayanti || 473 ||’

atra sakhīṣu roṣaḥ priyaguṇeṣu cāsūyā, kṣīranīravanmithaḥ *saṃkīryamāṇau māninīvāgārambhaparatayā *pratīyete ||

chāyādarśaprakāro yathā

‘āḥ sīte patigarvavibhramabharabhrā*ntabhramadbāndhavapradhvaṃsasmitakāntimattava tadā jātaṃ yadetanmukham | saṃpratyeva haṭhāttadeṣa* kurute *keśoccayākarṣaṇatrāsottānitalolalocanapatadbāṣpaplutaṃ rāvaṇaḥ || 474 ||’

atra krodhābhāse chāyādarśanyāyena ratyābhāsaḥ *saṃkīryamāṇa upalabhyate ||

[page 718]

*narasiṃhaprakāro yathā—

‘kiṃ dvāri daivahatike sahakārakeṇa saṃvardhitena viṣapādapa eṣa pāpaḥ | asminmanāgapi *vikāśavikārabhāji bhīmā bhavanti madanajvarasaṃnipātāḥ || 475 ||’

atra narasiṃhajātāviva siṃhanaraśarīrabhāgau* sahakāravarṇanāvāgārambhānusāreṇa sakhīviṣayānukampā sahakāraviṣayā ca kutsā mithaḥ saṃkīryete | tathā hi *daivahatike itiśabdena labdhāyāṃ niyatyupādhau sarvathaivānukampyamānatāyāṃ sahakārasaṃvardhananibandhanatvamevāsyāḥ kalā dyotyate | evaṃ nāma tvaṃ daivopahatāsi yatsahakārachadmānaṃ viṣapādapaṃ* dvāri saṃvardhayasīti* | viṣapādapaśabdena ca* labdhāyāṃ sahakārasya sarvathaiva kutsāyāṃ *vikāsakāle kāminīnāmasahyasmarajvarasaṃnipātahetukatvamevāsyāḥ kapratyayena* pratyāyyate || taduktam—

kutsitatvena kutsāvānsamyagvāpi hi kutsitaḥ | svaśabdābhihite kena viśiṣṭo 'rthaḥ pratīyate ||
na ca sāṃpratikī kutsā śabdabhede pratīyate | *pūjyate kutsitatve 'pi praśastatve 'pi kutsyate* ||
[page 719]

tad yathā—

‘eka iha jīvaloke jīvatirūpaṃ nṛrūpapaśurūpaḥ* | yaḥ *premapāśapāśe *mṛga iva na mṛgīdṛśāṃ patita || 476 ||’

pāṃsūdakaprakāro* yathā—

‘mā garvamudvaha kapolatale cakāsti kāntasvahastalikhitā mama mañjarīti | anyāpi kiṃ na sakhi bhājanamīdṛśānāṃ vairī na cedbhavati vepathurantarāyaḥ || 477 ||’

atra svasaubhāgyavarṇanā mṛtpiṇḍe *pāṃsūdakayorivāvibhāgamāpādyamānayorasūyāgarvayoḥ saṃkara upalabhyate* ||

citravarṇaprakāro yathā—

‘virodho viśrāntaḥ prasarati raso nirvṛtighana- stadauddhatya kvāpi vrajati vinayaḥ prahvayati mām | jhaṭityasmindṛṣṭe kimapi paravānasmi yadi vā mahārghastīrthānāmiva* hi mahatāṃ ko 'pyatiśayaḥ || 478 ||’

atra vīrauddhatyasvātantryavyarasānāmānandapraśamapāravaśyarasaistiraskriyamāṇānāṃ *paṭa iva nīlādibhiḥ *sītādīnāṃ praśamā rāmadarśanaprabhāvodbhave-[page 720]lavasya vismayātiśayapraśamajanmani *vāgārambhānubhāvopamāpade citravarṇavatsaṃkīryamāṇāḥ samupalabhyante ||

atha *rasaguṇasaṃkaraḥ |

nanu ca *doṣahānamiva guṇopādānamapi niyamanirvartyam* | alaṃkārayoga iva rasāviyogo 'pyavaśyaṃ vidheyaḥ | kadācidalaṃkārayogo 'pi tyajyate *na tu rasāviyogo guṇayogaśca vyabhicaritasaṃbandhāviti | atrocyate | yatra citra*varṇavannarasiṃhavatpāṃsūdakava*ccāvayavāvayavinyāyena jātivyaktinyāyena *cāpṛthakprayatnanirvartyānāṃ* guṇarasānāṃ vākye saṃniveśastatra saṃkaravyavahāro na pravartate ||

tad yathā—

madhuraṃ rasavadvāci vastunyapi rasasthitiḥ | yena mādyanti dhīmanto madhuneva madhuvratāḥ ||
kāmaṃ sarvo 'pyalaṃkāro rasamarthe niṣiñcati | tathāpyagrāmyataivainaṃ bhāraṃ vahati bhūyasā ||
śṛṅa‍gāra eva *madhuraḥ paraprahlādano rasaḥ* | tanmayaṃ kāvyamāśritya mādhuryaṃ pratitiṣṭhati ||
śṛṅa‍gāre vipralambhākhye karuṇe ca prakarṣavat | mādhuryamārdratāṃ yāti yatastatrādhikaṃ manaḥ ||
[page 721]
raudrādayo rasā dīptyā lakṣyante *kāvyavartinaḥ | *tavdyaktihetū śabdārthāvojodhiṣṭhāya tiṣṭhati ||
*samarthakatvaṃ vākyasya yattu sarvarasānprati | sa prasādo guṇo jñeyaḥ sarvasādhāraṇakriyaḥ ||’

seyaṃ guṇānāṃ rasārambhakatve saṃkarāprasiddhiḥ | evaṃ rasānāṃ guṇārambhakatve 'pi | tadyathā—rụ̄dhāhaṃkārataurjityam, *bhāvato vāk‌pravṛttirbhāvikatvam, *krodhādāvapyatīvratā, mādhuryam, āśayotkarṣaḥ, udāttatvam, arthasyābhīṣṭatamatā, *preyaḥ, dīptarasatvaṃ, kāntiriti | yatra tu tilatandulavat* kṣīranīravacchāyādarśavat tulyakakṣatayaiva guṇarasānāṃ *vākye 'pṛthakprayatnanirvartyānāṃ viniveśastatra saṃkaravyavahāraḥ pravartata eva | sa ṣọdhā—guṇapradhānaḥ—rasapradhānaḥ, ubhayapradhānaḥ, ubhayāpradhānaḥ, guṇādhikaḥ, rasādhika iti ||

teṣu guṇapradhāno yathā—

‘atrāntare lalitahāralatānitambasaṃvāhanaskhalitavegataraṅgitāṅa‍gī | devī vyapāsya śayanaṃ dhṛtamānatanturantaḥpuraṃ gatavatī saha sauvidallaiḥ || 479 ||’
[page 722]

atrārthaprākaṭyaudāryayorarthaśabdaguṇayoḥ *prādhānyaṃ *na ratikrodhayoriti guṇapradhānaḥ ||

rasapradhāno yathā—

‘asminnagṛhyata pinākabhṛtā salīla- mārabdhavepathuradhīravilocanāyāḥ | vinyastamaṅa‍galamahauṣadhirīśvarāyāḥ srastoragapratisareṇa kareṇa pāṇiḥ || 480 ||’

atra ślādhvaviśeṣaṇayoga udāttatvam, bandhavikaṭatvamudāratā, arthaprākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ, dīptarasatvaṃ kāntiriti guṇāḥ sādhvasavilāsānurāgasaṃgamarasairatiśayyanta iti rasapradhānaḥ ||

ubhayapradhāno yathā—

‘āpātamātrarasike sarasīruhasya kiṃ bījamarpayitumicchasi vāpikāyām | kālaḥ kalirjagadidaṃ na kṛtajñamajñe sthitvā hariṣyati tavaiva mukhasya śobhām || 481 ||’

atra bhaṇitiviśeṣa uktiḥ saṃvidhāne *susūtratā śleṣa iti śabdaguṇayorlāvaṇyavilāsavarṇanīyarasayośca tulyakakṣatayā nirdeśa* ityubhayapradhānaḥ ||

ubhayāpradhāno yathā—

‘abhinavavadhūroṣasvāduḥ karīṣatanūnapā- dasaralajanāśleṣakrūrastuṣārasamīraṇaḥ | galitavibhavasyājñevādya* dyutirmasṛṇā rave- rvirahivanitāvaktraklaibyaṃ bibharti niśākaraḥ || 482 ||’
[page 723]

atra svādukrūramasṛṇaklaibya*mityanyadharmāṇāmanyatrāropaṇaṃ samādhiḥ, abhinavavadhūroṣādīnāṃ caturṇāmapyarthānāṃ svādvādīnāṃ ca lakṣaṇādilakṣitānāṃ prākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ, abhinavavadhūroṣasvāduḥ karīṣatanūnapāt iti viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyāṇāmupakrameṇa nirvahaṇaṃ* rītiḥ, pādacatuṣṭaye caturṇāmarthānāṃ vibhaktyasamatvena niveśaḥ saṃbhitatvamiti catvāro guṇāḥ, catvāraśca ratyamarṣaviṣādajugupsātmāno rasāḥ kālāvasthānivedanaparatvena pratīyanta ityubhayāpradhānaḥ ||

guṇādhiko yathā—

‘ajananirastu bibhūterapūraṇirbhavatu sarvakāmānām | mā yāciṣi mā seviṣi mā sahiṣi parābhavaṃ dhaninaḥ || 483 ||’

atra suptiṅvyutpattiḥ* sauśabdyam, vākyānāṃ paripūrṇatvamarthavyaktiḥ, arthasya prākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ, vibhūteranutpattau kāmā na pūryante, aparipūrṇakāmo yācate, yācamānastadanāpnuvan dhaninaḥ sevate, sevamānastu taiḥ paribhūyata ityutpattyādikriyākramo rītiriti guṇāścatvāraḥ, rasastu nirveda evaika iti guṇādhikaḥ ||

ssādhiko yathā—

‘kamalamanambhasi kamale kuvalayametāni kanakalatikāyām | sā ca sukumārasubhagetyutpātaparamparā keyam || 484 ||’

atra kamalamanambhaṃsi kamale kuvalayametāni kanakalatikāyām ityanyadharmāṇāmanyatrāropaṇaṃ samādhiḥ, sā ca sukumārasubhagetyutpātaparamparā keyamityaślīlāmaṅa‍galārthau doṣaguṇāvapi, ślādhyaviśeṣaguṇayoga udātta-[page 724]tvam, vikaṭabandhatvamudāratā, upakramābhedo rītiḥ, *arthaprākaṭyaṃ prasādaḥ, aniṣṭhuratā saukumāryam, *abhīṣṭatamatā preyaḥ, dīptarasatvaṃ kāntiriti guṇā daśa, rasāstu ratyutkarṣaharṣadhṛtyutkaṇṭhāvegavismaya*mativitarkacintācapalatāhāsotsāhastambhagadgadonmāda*vrīḍāvahitthabhayaśaṅa‍kāḥ viṃśatirvāgārambhānubhāve śrṛṅa‍gāriṇaḥ priyācāṭukārasya kasyacitpratīyanta iti rasādhikaḥ ||

rasālaṃkārasaṃkaro 'pyetena vyākhyātaḥ |

rasavanti hi vastūni sālaṃkārāṇi kānicit | ekenaiva prayatnena *nirvartyante mahākaveḥ || 173 ||
rasākṣiptatayā yasya bandhaḥ śakyakriyo bhavet | apṛthagyatnanirvartyaḥ *so 'laṃkāraḥ prakṛṣyate || 174 ||
rasābhāvādiviṣayavivakṣāvirahe sati | alaṃkāranibandho yaḥ sa kavibhyo na rocate || 175 ||

tatra rasālaṃkārasaṃkaro dvidhā—rasapradhāno 'laṃkārapradhānaśca | *tayoryonubhavitraiva varṇyate sa rasapradhānaḥ | tatra hyalaṃkāravato vākyasya vāgārambhānubhāvatvaṃ bhavati ||

tatra ratāvupamāyāḥ saṃkaro yathā—

‘tīe daṃsaṇasuhae *paṇaakkhalaṇajaṇio muhammi maṇahare | roso vi haraï hiaaṃ *maapaṃko vva mialaṃchaṇammi* ṇisaṇṇo 485’
[tasyā darśanasubhage praṇayaskhalanajanito mukhe manohare | roṣo 'pi harati hṛdayaṃ madapaṅa‍ka iva mṛgalāñchane niṣaṇṇaḥ ||]
[page 725]

atropamātiraskāreṇa rasavato harervacasi vāgārambharūpe rukmiṇīpradattapārijātamañjarīvilokanaprabhavaṃ satyabhāmāyā *roṣarāmaṇīyakaṃ prādhānyataḥ pratīyate ||

ratāveva viparītopamā yathā—

‘yattvannetrasamānakānti salile magnaṃ tadindīvaraṃ meghairantaritaḥ priye tava *mukhacchāyānukārī śaśī | *ye 'pi *tvadgamanānukārigatayaste rājahaṃsā gatā- stvatsādṛśyavinodamātramapi me daivena na kṣamyate || 486 ||’

atra virahiṇo rāmasya priyāvayavasādṛśyadarśanenātmānaṃ vinodayata *upāyabhraṃśādaratipramavaviṣādavāgārambhe svarūpābhidhāne prakṣīṇaśaktiraprāghānyenopamā pratīyate ||

ratāveva *paryāyasya yathā—

‘kiṃ gurujahaṇaṃ *aha thaṇabharo tti *bhāakaraalaggatuliāe* | vihiṇo *khuttaṃgulimaggavibbhamaṃ* vahaï se* tivalī || 487 ||’
[kiṃ gurujadhanamatha stanabhara iti bhāgakaratalāgratulitāyāḥ | vidheḥ khātāṅa‍gulimārgavibhramaṃ vahatyasyāstrivalī ||]

atra yadyapi ratiprabhavebhyo vismayādibhyaḥ saṃśayahetūtprekṣopamā*dibhyaśca paryāyālaṃkāraḥ prādhānyena pratīyate tathāpyasau vāgārambhānubhāva iti *ratāvaprādhānyamevānubhavati ||

[page 726]

ratāveva samādhiryathā |

‘kṛcchreṇoruyugaṃ vyatītya suciraṃ bhrāntvā nitambasthale madhye 'syāstrivalītaraṅa‍gaviṣame *nisyandatāmāgatā | maddṛṣṭistṛṣiteva saṃprati śanairāruhya tuṅa‍gau stanau sākāṅa‍kṣaṃ muhurīkṣate *jalalavaprasyandinī locaneṃ || 488 ||’

atra vatsarājena svadṛṣṭau prāṇidharmāḥ samādhīyamānāḥ sāgarikā*darśanottha*rativāgārambhe nyagbhavanti ||

ratāvevārthaśleṣasya yathā—

‘kapole pattrālī karatalanirodhena mṛditā nipīto *niḥśvāsairayamamṛtahṛdyo 'dhararasaḥ | muhurlagnaḥ kaṇṭhe taralayati *bāṣpaḥ stanataṭīṃ priyo manyurjātastava niranurodhe na tu vayam || 489 ||’

atra yadyapyākṣepeṇa vākyopasaṃhārastathāpi priya ityādibhiḥ prādhānyenābhidhīyamānaḥ śleṣa eva śrṛṅa‍gāriṇo vāgārambhānubhāvā*ṅa‍gatāmaṅa‍gīkaroti ||

ratāveva paryāyokteryathā—

‘muktāḥ kandharayā *dhṛtā stanataṭenottuṅa‍gutā kumbhayorūrubhyāṃ pariṇāhitā kramavatī hastasya pabhdyāṃ gatiḥ | etadvaḥ karighātinastu kaṭhinaṃ carmaiva ko 'yaṃ haṭhaścaṇḍīti tripurārikelivacanairā*ryāsmitaṃ pātu vaḥ || 490 ||’

atra bhagavataścāṭūktivāgārambhe devyāḥ paryāyavarṇanā *śeṣabhāvaṃ labhate-[page 727]ya* udāsīnena varṇyate so 'laṃkārapradhānaḥ sa hi rasabhāvādeḥ saṃkaraprakāramabhidhitsuḥ svabhāboktiṃ vakroktiṃ vāvalambate ||

tatra svabhāvoktipakṣe jātiḥ ||

sā vidhimukhena yathā—

‘*thoosaraṃtarosaṃ *thoatthoaparivaḍḍhamāṇapaharisam | hoi a dūrapaāsaṃ *uhaarasāaṃtavibbhamaṃ* tīa mukham || 491 ||’
[stokāpasaradroṣaṃ stokastokaparivardhamānapraharṣam | bhavati ca dūraprakāśamubhayarasāyattavibhramaṃ tasyā mukham ||]

atra satyabhāmāyā roṣasyāpasarpataḥ* praharṣasya ca prasarpato ye 'nubhāvā jihnāvalokanamukhaprasādādayasta iha saṃkīryamāṇāḥ kavinobhayarasāyattavibhramamityanena* yathāvadavasthitā bhavantīti vidhimukhenābhidhīyante ||

jātireva niṣedhamukhena yathā—

‘dhīreṇa māṇabhaṃgo *māṇaksvalaṇeṇa garua dhīrārambho | *ullalaï tulijjaṃte ekammi vi se thiraṃ ṇa laggaï hiaaṃ 492’
[dhairyeṇa mānabhaṅa‍go mānaskhalanena gurukadhairyārambhaḥ | ullalati tolyamāne ekasminnapyasyāḥ sthiraṃ na lagati hṛdayam ||]

atra yadyapi hetūpanyāso vartate tathāpi tasya *svabhāvākhyānaparikaratvenāprādhānyena hṛdayakriyāsvarūpameveha* niṣedhamukhenābhidhīyata itīyaṃ jātireva bhavati ||

[page 728]

saiva vidhiniṣedhābhyāṃ yathā—

‘helodastamahīdharasya tanutāmālokya doṣṇo hare- rhastenāṃsataṭe 'valambya* caraṇāvāropya tatpādayoḥ | śailoddhārasahāyatāṃ jigamiṣoraspṛṣṭagovardhanā rādhāyāḥ suciraṃ jayanti gagane vandhyāḥ karabhrāntayaḥ 493’

atra rādhāyāḥ preyasi harau *yathāvadastitodbhūtavṛttisnehaśaṅa‍kotsāhā mithaḥ saṃkīryamāṇā bhayāvegasmṛtimativitarkādibhirvyabhicāribhāvairālambanacaraṇākramaṇasahakṛtāyāṃ karabhrāntau śarīrārambhānubhāve pratīyamānā aspṛṣṭagovardhanā vandhyā iti niṣedhamukhena jayantīti vidhimukhena cābhidhīyante ||

vakroktipakṣa upamādayaḥ |

teṣūpamā yathā—

‘*corā sabhaasataṇhaṃ puṇo puṇo pesaaṃti diṭṭhīo | ahirakkhiaṇihikalase vva *poḍhamahilāthaṇucchaṃge || 494 ||’
[corāḥ sabhayasatṛṣṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ preṣayanti dṛṣṭīḥ | abhirakṣitanidhikalaśa iva prauḍhamahilāstanotsaṅa‍ge ||]

atra *﻿cauragatabhayānurāgayoḥ saṃkarasvabhāvoktimatibhūyottarārdhāgatamaupamyaṃ prādhānyena pratīyate ||

[page 729]

upamaiva rasābhāsasaṃkaraviṣayā yathā—

‘ekenārkaṃ pravitataruṣā pāṭalenāsta*saṃsthaṃ *paśyatyakṣṇā sajalataralenāpareṇātmakāntam | ahnaśchede dayitavirahāśaṅkinī cakravākī tau saṃkīrṇau racayati rasau nartakīva pragalbhā || 495 ||’

atra nigadenaiva *vyākhyāte spaṣṭatayaivopamāyāḥ *pradhānatvena pratītiḥ ||

rasapraśamayorupamāsahoktiryathā—

‘dṛṣṭe locanavanmanāṅmukulitaṃ pārśvasthite cakravannyagbhūtaṃ bahirāsitaṃ pulakavatsparśaṃ samātanvati* | nīvībandhavadāgataṃ śithilatāmābhāṣamāṇe tato mānenāpasṛtaṃ hriyeva sudṛśaḥ pādaspṛśi preyasi || 496 ||’

atra kasyāścitsakhīvikhyātamānasaṃvidhānakopānmānavatyāḥ priyasaṃdarśanādālambanavibhāvādutpannaprakṛṣṭaratiprabhave* praharṣasthāyibhāve *tatpārśvopasarpaṇādibhiruddīpanavibhāvairuddīpyamāne* samutpadyamāneṣu* *pulakādiṣu mukhātmakeṣu vyabhicāriṣu nayananimīlanādhomukhyanīvīvisraṃsa*nādibhiranubhāvaiḥ prakarṣaṇāropaṇādānandarasa*tāmāpādyamāne sthāyini prabalavirodhibhāvāntarodayādetebhya eva kāraṇebhyaḥ pratikṣaṇamapacīyamānayorlajjāroṣayoḥ praśamasaṃkarābhibhūya prādhānyenopamāsahoktiḥ *prakāśate ||

[page 730]

śleṣādyalaṃkārasāmarthyāttu kvacidavāstavamapi rasābhāsasaṃkaraṃ kavayaḥ prakalpayanti* ||

sa rūpakaśleṣeṇa yathā—

‘rāmamanmathaśareṇa tāḍitā duḥsahena hṛdaye niśācarī | gandhavadrudhiracandanokṣitā jīviteśavasatiṃ jagāma sā || 497 ||’

atra bībhatso rasaḥ śleṣarūpakasāmarthyādavidyamānenāpi śrṛṅa‍gārarasena saṃkīrṇa iva pratīyate ||

śleṣānuviddhārthāntaranyāsena yathā—

‘*daṭṭhoṭṭha ho asilaaghāo* devi maülāvaï loaṇabhaüho* ve | supaohara*kuvala apattalacchi *kaha moha ṇa jaṇaï ṇa laggavacchi ||’
[daṣṭauṣṭha ho asilatādhāto devi mukalayati locanabhruvau dve api | supayodharakuvalayapattralakṣmīḥ kathaṃ mohaṃ na janayati na lagnā vakṣasi ||]

atra vīro rasaḥ śleṣasāmarthyādavidyamānenāpi vipralambhaśrṛṅa‍gāreṇa saṃkīryate ||

[page 731]

śleṣopamā yathā—

‘kṣipto hastāvalagnaḥ prasabhamabhihato 'pyādadānoṃ 'śukāntaṃ gṛhṇankeśeṣvapāstaścaraṇanipatito nekṣitaḥ saṃkrameṇa | āliṅa‍ganyo 'vadhūtastripurayuvatibhiḥ sāśrunetrotpalābhiḥ kāmīvārdrāparādhaḥ sa *dahatu duritaṃ śāmbhabo vaḥ śarāgniḥ 499’

atra karuṇo rasaḥ śleṣopamāsāmarthyenāvidyamānenāpi vipralambhaśṛṅa‍gāreṇa saṃkīryate ||

śleṣavyatirekeṇa yathā—

‘padbhyāmūruyugaṃ vibhajya bhujayorbhadhyaṃ nipīḍyorasā pārśveṣu prasabhaṃ prahṛtya nakharairdantairvilūyādharam* | suptānapyavabodhya yuṣmadahitānbhūyo 'pi *bhuṅke vane kiṃ kāntā surataiṣiṇī nahi nahi vyāghrī karālānanā || 500 ||’

*atra śleṣasāmarthyādapāramārthikī śṛṅgāra*pratītiḥ pāramārthikena bībhatsarasena vyāvartamānā taddharmāṇāṃ mithaḥ *saṃsargabuddhimutpādayati ||

śleṣarūpakeṇa yathā—

‘antraiḥ kalpitamaṅa‍galapratisarāḥ strīhastaraktotpalavyaktottaṃsabhṛtaḥ pinahya śirasā hṛtpuṇḍarīkastrajaḥ | etāḥ śoṇitapaṅa‍kakuṅa‍kumajuṣaḥ saṃbhūya kāntaiḥ pibantyasthisnehasurāḥ kapālacaṣakaiḥ prītāḥ piśācāṅa‍ganāḥ || 501 ||’

atra vībhatso rasaḥ śabdasāmarthyākṣiptena śṛṅa‍garābhāsena saṃkīryate ||

[page 732]

samādhirūpakeṇa yathā—

‘śikhaṇḍe khaṇḍenduḥ śaśidinakarau karṇayugale dṛśastārāstārāścalamuḍupacakraṃ ca kucayoḥ | taḍitkāñcī sandhyā sicayarucayaḥ kāli tadayaṃ tavākalpaḥ kalpavyuparamavidheyo vijayate || 502 ||’

atra bhayānako rasaḥ samādhirūpakādyupakalpitākalparāmaṇīyakākṣiptena śṛṅa‍gārābhāsena saṃkīryamāṇaḥ śrotuḥ preyorasāṅa‍gatāṃ gacchansaṃgacchate | evamiyamama*nekaprakārasaṃsṛṣṭirguṇālaṃkārasaṃkaraprabhavābhimantavyā tatrāpi pradhānāṅa‍gabhāvena samakakṣatayā ca vyaktāvyaktobhayātmakarūpāstilatandula*kṣīrajalācchāyādarśakādayo bhedā *yathāyogamavagantavyāḥ | te kiṃ vaktavyā na vaktavyāḥ | kathamanuktā gamyante | ukteṣvevāntarbhāvāt | tadyadhā--arthobhayālaṃkārābhidhāne ‘khaṃ vaste’ iti ‘carcāṃ pārayati’ iti vibhaktimudrā, kalaviṅa‍kaṇṭhamalinaṃ kādambinīkambalam iti padamudrā ca śabdālaṃkārāvapi saṃkīryamāṇau pratīyete |

evamanyatrāpi |

aṅa‍gāṅgibhāvāvasthānaṃ sarveṣāṃ samakakṣatā | ityalaṃkāra*saṃsṛṣṭerlakṣaṇīyā dvayī gatiḥ || 176 ||

tatrāṅa‍gāṅgibhāvenāvasthānaṃ yathā—

‘ākṣipantyaravindāni mugdhe tava mukhaśriyam | koṣadaṇḍasamagrāṇāṃ kimeṣāmasti duṣkaram* || 503 ||’

*atrāravindāni ‘mugdhe tava mukhaśriyamākṣipantīti’ upamā, ‘koṣa-[page 733]daṇḍasamagrāṇāṃ kimeṣāmasti duṣkaram’ iti śleṣopasarjanārthāntaranyāsaḥ | *bhavanti cāravindāni koṣadaṇḍasamagrāṇi *tena teṣāṃ na kiṃcidaśakyamasti koṣadaṇḍayorvijayasādhanatvāt | etena śleṣasya *sādhanabhūtārthasamarthakatvādupamāyāstu prastutasādhyavastuviśeṣakatvādarthāntaranyāsaṃ pratyaṅa‍gabhāvo vijñāyate |

sarveṣāṃ samakakṣatāṃ yathā—

‘limpatīva tamo 'ṅa‍gāni varṣatīvāñjanaṃ nabhaḥ | asatpuruṣaseveva dṛṣṭirni*ṣphalatāṃ gatā || 504 ||’

*nanu cābandhaḥ samatvātsyāditi kathaṃ sarveṣāṃ tulyakakṣatayā saṃbandhotpattiḥ evaṃ manyate ye utprekṣopamādayo 'laṃkārā vibhāvānubhāvavyabhi*cāryādivarṇanāparatayā rasāderaṅa‍gatāṃ pratipadyante tadā bhavatyeva teṣāṃ tulyakakṣateti | tatra ‘limpatīva tamo 'ṅa‍gāni varṣatīvāñjanaṃ nabhaḥ’ iti dve* utprekṣe, ‘asatpuruṣaseveva dṛṣṭirniṣphalatāṃ gatā’ ityupamā ca varṇanīyasya tamasa uddīpanavibhāvabhūtasya samatayaivotkarṣapratipādakatvenā*ṅa‍gabhāvamupagateti nāsti lakṣaṇānupapattiriti | nanūpamā imāstisro 'pi kasmānnocyante | ivo hi vākyāntareṣūpamāyā eva dṛśyate | *maivam | upamānopameyaśabdapratipannasya* sādṛśyārthasya dyotanamivena kriyate na ca limpatītyādāvupamānamupameyaṃ vāsti yatsādṛśyadyotanaya ivaḥ *prayujyet | na ca tiṅantenopamānamasti tasya sādhyārthābhidhāyitvenāsattvārthatvāt* ||

[page 734]

tadāha—

‘siddhasya hi samānārthamupamānaṃ vidhīyate | tiṅantārthasya sādhyatvādupamārtho na vidyate ||’

na copamāyāmevevaśabdo bhavati | tadyathā kathamivaitadbhaviṣyati | astu vā limpatitamasorupamānopameyabhāvastathāpi tulyadharmo na dṛśyate ya upamānopameyabhāvāya prabhavati | kimanyaina lepanameva bhavati tarhi limpatinā* kena bhāvyam | na hi lepanaṃ limpeḥ pṛthagmavitumīṣṭe | nanu ceha dvayaṃ cakāsti thāturlimpati tadarthaśca* lepanam | maivam | evaṃ sati limpatiriveti syāt na tu limpatīveti | atha yathā rāhoḥ śiraḥ iti bhedābhāve 'pyavayavāvayavibhāvastatheha dharmadharmibhāvo bhaviṣyati | maivam | upamānopameyabhāvasya bhedasādṛśyapratipattinibandhanatvāt tadabhāve 'pi yastanmanute sa kathaṃ nonmattaḥ syāt |

taduktam—‘sa eva dharmo dharmī cetyunmatto 'pi na bhāṣate |’ astu tarhi tiṅa‍vācyaḥ* kartā upamānamiti cet nyagbhūto 'sau kriyāpade | kathaṃ punarasau kriyāpade* nyagbhūto bhavati | śrūyatāṃ, ṣaḍarthāstiṅantena pratīyante kriyā kālaḥ upagrahaḥ sādhanaṃ saṅkhyā puruṣaśceti | teṣu kriyākālātmanepadaparasmaipadanimittāni prakṛtirabhidhatte pratyayaḥ sādhanaṃ, saṅkhyāṃ puruṣaṃ ca | eteṣāṃ tu kriyārthatvātkriyā pradhānaṃ, kālātmanepadanimitte kriyāviśeṣaṇatvena, saṅkhyāpuruṣau sādhanaviśeṣaṇatvena tayoreva nyagbhavataḥ | sādhanaṃ punaḥ ‘prakṛtipratyayau* *svārthaṃ saha brūtaḥ’ iti nyāyāt ‘pradhānabhūtamapi bhūtaṃ bhavyāyopadiśyata’ iti nyāyena kriyāsiddhāvutpa-[page 735]nnavyāpāraṃ parārthaṃ tasyāṃ kriyāyāṃ nyagmavati | tenāyaṃ kartā svakriyāsidbhābākulaḥ* kathamupamānatvenopameyatvena *vānyadapekṣituṃ kṣamate | evaṃ tarhi yo 'ṅa‍gāni limpati tena kriyopalakṣitena kartrā tulyaṃ tama ityarthaḥ pratipatsyate | maivam | kriyopalakṣitasya karturupamānabhūtasya śabdanvāyabalāpratipattiḥ | śabdo hi mukhyāgauṇīlakṣaṇābhirarthaprakaraṇādisaṃpāditasācivyādā*bhistisṛbhireva vṛttibhirarthaviśeṣapratipattinimittaṃ bhavati | tadyathā—gaurityayaṃ śabdo mukhyayā vṛttyā sāsnādimantamarthaṃ pratipādayati sa eva tiṣṭhanmūtratvādiguṇasaṃpadamapekṣya vāhīkādau prayujyamāno gauṇīṃ vṛttimanubhavati | yadā tu mukhyayā gauṇyā vopāttakriyāsiddhau sādhanabhāvaṃ gantumasamarthastadā lakṣaṇayā svārthāvinābhūtamarthāntaraṃ lakṣayati yathā gaṅa‍gāyāṃ ghoṣaḥ prativasatīti gaṅa‍gāśabdo viśiṣṭodakapravāhe nirụ̄dhābhidhānaśaktirghoṣakartṛkāyāḥ prativasanakriyāyā adhikaraṇabhāvaṃ gantumasamarthaḥ svārthāvinābhūtaṃ taṭaṃ* lakṣayatīti | na caitāsāmihānyatamāpi vṛttiḥ saṃgacchate | tathā hi limpateḥ kriyāvacanatvānna mukhyā* | nāpi kriyākartrorasādṛśyena śuktikādau rajatādivattadbhāvāpattiḥ kriyāguṇānāṃ kartaryasaṃbhavāt | sākṣādiva prayogācca na gauṇī kriyāyāśca svayameva dharmarūpatvāt | buddhiḥ paśyatītivadanyadharmāṇāmanyatrādhiropaṇamupacāra iti na gauṇībheda upacāritā* | ivaśabdasya cāsādṛśye 'pi darśanānna lakṣyeta | yadi hīvaśabdaḥ sādṛśyameva vidyotayati tadā limpatikriyāyāḥ sattvabhūtena tamasā sādṛśyaṃ na saṃbhavatīti svārthāvinābhūte kartāra-[page 736]mākṣipati | na ceha lakṣitalakṣaṇāviruddha*lakṣaṇādayo 'pi vartante, yathā ‘priye jane nāsti punaruktaṃ’, ‘svalpairasāvapi na dṛśyata eva kālaiḥ’ iti | na ca *śabdanyāyavilaṅghinī padārthavyutpattiḥ prekṣāvadbhirādriyate | yadyapyadhyāhārādibhiridamapi syāttathāpi tulyadharmo mārgaṇīyastadvadeva vipratipatteḥ || na cendumukhādivadanabhidhīyamānasyāpi tulyaguṇasya pratyayo bhavatīti vācyam |

yathenduriva te vakramiti kāntiḥ pratīyate | *na tathā limpaterlepādanyadatra pratīyate || 177 ||
tadupaśleṣaṇārtho 'yaṃ limpatirdhvāntakartṛkaḥ | varṣaṇārthaśca vidvadbhirutprekṣyata itīkṣyatām || 178 ||
manye-śaṅa‍ke-dhruvaṃ-prāyo-nūnamityevamādibhiḥ | utprekṣā vyajyate śabdairivaśabdo 'pi tādṛśaḥ || 179 ||

vākyavadeva prabandheṣvanaucityaparihāreṇa guṇālaṃkārasaṃkaraniveśo bhavati | tatrānaucityaparihāro yathā—māyayā kaikeyīdaśarathābhyāṃ rāmaḥ pralambhito na mātāpitṛbhyāmiti nirdoṣadaśarathe; rāmameva yodhayan rāmeṇa vālī nihato na sugrīveṇeti mahāvīracarite; rudhirapriyarākṣasena duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ pītaṃ na bhīmaseneneti veṇīsaṃhāre; durvāsaso 'padhyānādduṣyantaḥ śakuntalāsvīkāraṃ visasmāra, *nānāvasthititānurāgatayeti śākuntale; lavaṇaprayuktarākṣasābhyāṃ vā sopaskareṇa *tadabhidhāya sītā parityājitā na kaikeyīmantharābhyāmiti chalitarāme; kiṃca dagdhāyāmapi [page 737]vāsavadattāyāṃ vairapraticikīrṣayā padmāvatī mayọdhā, avasite ca samīhite tathā vinā kṣaṇamapi na jīvāmītyavijñātavāsavadattāsaṃnighervatsarājasyāgnipraveśādhyavasāyaḥ priyāhṛdayato vyalīkaśalyamuccakhāneti tāpasavatsarāje; *nīcākṣaḥ svāmikāryaṃ sādhayāmīti prabhubhaktyā niraparādhāmapi preyasīṃ hitvā svāmikāryāpekṣayāhamevaitāvanti dināni jīvitaḥ, adya tu kṛtasvāmikāryastāmevānugacchāmīti śivagaṇaḥ śūdrakanimittāṃ māyāmayīṃ citāṃ priyāsamakṣaṃ praviveśa, sāpi tatpremāvadānadarśanāpahnutapriyabyalīkā* tadviyogakātarā tatraivātmānaṃ praticikṣepeti vikrāntaśūdrake, iti tadetaddoṣahānam || guṇopādānaṃ tu samyag guṇayogena saṃvidhāne susūtratā, api ca caturvṛttyaṅa‍gasaṃpannamiti catasro vṛttayo bhāratī ārabhaṭī kaiśikī sāttvatī ceti | tatra—

yā vākpradhānā nṛpatiprayojyā strīvarjitā *saṃskṛtayātha yuktā | svanāmadheyairbharataprayojyā sā bhāratī nāma bhavettu vṛttiḥ ||
yatrāvapātakṣutalaṅghitāni chedyāni māyākṛtamindrajālam | citrāṇi yuddhāni ca tatra vṛttimetādṛśīmārabhaṭīṃ vadanti ||
yā ślakṣṇanepathyaviśeṣayuktā strīsaṃgatā yā bahugītavṛttā | kāmopabhogapracuropacārā tāṃ kaiśikīṃ vṛttimudāharanti ||
yā sāttvikenātmaguṇena yuktā tyāgena vṛttena samanvitā ca | harṣotkaṭā saṃhṛtaśokabhārā sā sāttvatīti prathiteha vṛttiḥ ||

āsāmaṅa‍gāni ṣoḍaśa—teṣu prarocanā, vīthī, prastāvanā, prahasanamiti catvāri bhāratyaṅa‍gāni ||

[page 738]

tatra vaktavyārthapraśaṃsāparaṃ vacaḥ prarocanā; yathā—

‘jayati bhuvanakāraṇaṃ svayambhurjayati purandaranandano murāriḥ | jayati girisutāniruddhadeho duritabhayāpaharo haraśca devaḥ 505

prastutavastūpapādanāvasarasūcakaṃ vacaḥ prastāvanā; yathā ratnāvalyām |

‘dvīpādanyasmādapi madhyādapi jalanidherdiśo 'pyantāt | ānīya jhaṭiti ghaṭayati vidhirabhimatamabhimukhībhūtaḥ 506’

uddhātyakādīnāmaṅa‍gānāṃ pravṛttiḥ vīthī uddhātyakaḥ kathoddhātaḥ prayogātiśayaḥ pravartako 'valagitamiti |

tatroddhātyako yathā—

‘ko jayati jayati śarvaḥ kena jitaṃ jitamanaṅa‍gadahanena | tripurāriṇā bhagavatā bālaśaśāṅa‍kāṅkitajaṭena || 507 ||’

kathoddhāto yathā—

‘sākaṃ paṅa‍kajajanmanā surapaterabhyarthanāyā vaśā- dikṣvākoḥ śaradindubimbavimale vaṃśe 'vatīrya svayam | niḥśeṣāttapadaṃ *trayīpathajuṣāṃ vidveṣiṇaṃ rākṣasaṃ yaḥ paulastyamahan sa pātu bhavato rāmābhidhāno hariḥ 508

prayogātiśayo yathā—

‘*yūthāyitamavatu hareḥ kṣmāmuddharato varāhavapuṣo vaḥ | *śeṣaphaṇaratnadarpaṇasahasrasaṃkrāntabimbasya || 509 ||’
[page 739]

pravartako yathā—

‘āsāditaprakaṭanirmalacandrahāsaḥ prāptaḥ śaratsamaya *eṣa viśuddhakāntaḥ* | utkhāya gāḍhatamasaṃ ghanakālamugraṃ rāmo daśāsyamiva saṃbhṛtabandhujīvaḥ || 510 ||’

avalagitaṃ yathā,—amumeva śaratsamayamāśritya gīyatām, tathā hyasyām*

‘satpakṣā madhuragiraḥ prasādhitāśā madoddhatārambhāḥ | nipatanti dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kālavaśānmedinīpṛṣṭhe || 511 ||’

*svadharmātpracalitānāṃ tāpasādīnāmupahāsaparaṃ vacaḥ prahasanam | yathā—

‘śramaṇaḥ śrāvakavadhvāḥ suratavidhau daśati nādharaṃ dattam | madirākṣi māṃsabhakṣaṇamasmatsamaye niṣiddhamiti || 512 ||’

saṃkṣiptikā, avapātaḥ, vastūtthāpanam, saṃsphoṭaḥ, iti catvāri ārabhaṭyaṅa‍gāni ||

teṣu māhendrajālanepathyādibhirvastusaṃkṣepaḥ saṃkṣiptikā | yathā—

‘rakṣasā mṛgarūpeṇa vañcayitvā sarāghavau | jahāra sītāṃ pakṣīndraprayāsakṣaṇavighnitaḥ || 513 ||’

bhayādibhirvidravādikarmānupraveśanirgamanamavapātaḥ | yathā—

‘mṛgarūpaṃ parityajya vidhāya vikaṭaṃ vapuḥ | nīyate rakṣasā tena lakṣmaṇo yudhi saṃśayam || 514 ||’
[page 740]

avidravaḥ savidravo vā sarvarasabhāvasamāso vastūtthāpanam | yathā—

‘rāhoścandrakalāmivānanacarīṃ daivātsamāsādya me dasyorasya kṛpāṇapātaviṣayādācchindataḥ preyasīm | ātaṅa‍kādvikalaṃ drutaṃ karuṇayā vikṣobhitaṃ vismayā- tkrodhena jvalitaṃ mudā vikasitaṃ cetaḥ kathaṃ vartatām 515’

nānāstrayuddhaniyuddhādibhiḥ sasaṃrambhasaṃprahāraḥ saṃsphoṭaḥ | yathā—

‘kṛṣṭā yena śiroruheṣu paśunā pāñcālarājātmajā yenāsyāḥ paridhānamapyapahṛtaṃ rājñāṃ gurūṇāṃ puraḥ | yasyoraḥsthalaśoṇitāsavamahaṃ pātuṃ pratijñātavā- nso 'yaṃ madbhujapañjare nipatitaḥ saṃrakṣyatāṃ kauravāḥ || 516 ||’

narma, narmasphijaḥ, narmasphoṭaḥ, narmagarbha, iti catvāri kaiśikyaṅa‍gāni ||

teṣu sthāpitaśṛṅa‍gāraṃ vaco viceṣṭitaṃ vā saparihāsaṃ narma | yathā—

‘vayaṃ tathā nāma yathāttha kiṃ vadāmyayaṃ tvakasmādvikalaḥ kathāntare | kadambagolākṛtimāśritaḥ kathaṃ viśuddhamugdhaḥ kulakanyakājanaḥ 517’

prathamasaṃbhoge navāvasthānaṃ saṃbhogāśrayavākyādi karma narmasphijaḥ | yathā—

‘prāptāsau vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ priyasutā saṅa‍ketakhaṇḍe nave vṛṣṭiḥ seyamanambudā 'mṛtamayī yātrāṇi me siñcati | kiṃ jānāsi vinodayiṣyati manaḥ saṃtaptamevādya me durvātyeva nivartayiṣyati na bhostāṃ devayānīṃ prati || 518 ||’

āvirbhūtābhilāṣānubhāvayorakāṇḍasaṃbhogabhaṅa‍go narmasphoṭaḥ | yathā—

‘itaḥ parānarbhakahāryaśastrānvaidarbhi paśyānumatā mayāsi | evaṃvighenāhavaceṣṭitena, tvaṃ prārthyase hastagatā mamaibhiḥ 519’
﻿ [page 741]

kāryahetoḥ svarūpavijñānādipracchādanaṃ narmagarbhaḥ | yathā—

‘athājināṣāḍhadharaḥ pragalbhavāgjvalanniva brahmamayena tejasā | viveśa kaścijjaṭilastapovanaṃ śarīrabaddhaḥ prathamāśramo yathā || 520 ||’

utthāpakaḥ, parivartakaḥ, saṃlāpakaḥ, saṃghātyakaḥ, iti catvāri sātvatyaṅa‍gāni |

teṣu parasparībhūtārtheṣūtthāpanamutthāpakaḥ | yathā—

‘prahara mama tu kāyaṃ prākprahārapriyo 'haṃ *mayi tu kṛtavighāte kiṃ vidadhyāḥ parasmāt | jhaṭiti vitatabahvaṅa‍gārabhāsvatkuṭhāra- pravighaṭitakaṭhauraskandhabandhaḥ kabandhaḥ || 521 ||

prastutārthatyagādanyārthabhajanaṃ, parivartakaḥ | yathā—

‘munimabhimukhatāṃ ninīṣavo yāḥ samupayayuḥ kamanīyatāṃ guṇena | madanamupadadhe sa eva tābhyo duradhighamā hi gatiḥ prayojanānām || 522 ||

sadasi nānāvākyairmitho 'dhikṣepaḥ saṃlāpakaḥ | yathā—

‘kathamapi na niṣiddho duḥkhinā bhīruṇā vā drupadatanayapāṇistena pitrā mamādya | tava bhujabaladarpādhdyāyamānasya vāmaḥ śirasi caraṇa eṣa nyasyate dhārayainam || 523 ||’

kāryamantrānubhāvadaivādibhiḥ saṃghātabhedaḥ saṃghātyakaḥ | yathā—

‘apaśyadbhiriveśānaṃ raṇānnivavṛte gaṇaiḥ | muhyatyeva hi kṛcchreṣu saṃbhramādhigataṃ manaḥ || 524 ||’
[page 742]

‘catura’ ityanena śāstrīyalaukikavyavahāravedino nāyakasya dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu vaicakṣaṇyamucyate | ‘udātta’ ityanena āśayavibhūtyorābhijātyayauvanādīnāṃ cotkarṣaḥ prakāśyate | caturvargaphalaṃ *prabandhaṃ ko vā na bāndhavīyatītyanena śrotṝṇāṃ rāmādivadvartitavyam, na rāvaṇādivaditi vidhiniṣedhanibandhanasya* prabandhasyābhīṣṭatamatvamākhyāyate | ‘mukhaṃ pratimukham' ityādinā pañcāṅa‍gaṃ prabandhaśarīramabhidhīyate | tadaṅa‍gāni copakṣepaparikarādīni catuḥṣaṣṭirapi mukhādiṣvevāntarbhavanti | atastadvadeva pañcasaṃdhyekamapi vākyaṃ prabandhavyapadeśamāsādayati | tadyathā—

‘kathamapi kṛtapratyāsattau priye’ iti mukham, ‘skhalitottare’ iti pratimukham, ‘virahakṛśayā kṛtvā vyājaṃ prajalpitamaśrutam’ iti garbhaḥ, ‘asahanasakhīśrotraprāptiprasādasasaṃbhramaṃ vivalitadṛśā’ iti vimarśaḥ, 'śūnye gehe samucchvasitaṃ *sametam’ iti nibarhaṇam | etena prācīnaprabandhārthe 'pi ekavākyoktena prabandhatvamityākhyātaṃ na bhavati | tadyathā—

‘turaganicayavyagrānūrvībhidaḥ sagarādhvare kapilamahasā roṣātpluṣṭānapi prapitāmahān | agaṇitatanūtāpastaptvā tapāṃsi bhagīratho bhagavati tava spṛṣṭānadbhiścirādudadīdharat || 525 ||’

‘avistṛtamasaṃkṣiptam’ ityanena vistārabhīrūṇāṃ kathārasavicchedaśaṅkināṃ ca cittamāvarjyate | ‘*śravyavṛttam’ ityanena vṛttāntarairāśvāsakādi-[page 743]parisamāptiriti pariśrāntāḥ śrotāra aśvāsyante, sragādisaṃniveśādivatsaṃdarbhe cāśvādayo vibhāvyante | ‘puropavane’ ityādinā ca deśakālapātrasaṃpadupavarṇanādālambanoddīpanavibhāvāḥ kathyante | udyānasalilakrīḍādyupalakṣaṇena kāminīnāṃ divāceṣṭāḥ, madhupānaratotsava ityanena ca rātriceṣṭā ucyante | vipralambhā ityanena catvāro 'pi prathamānurāgādayaḥ parāmṛśyante | ‘vivāha*’ ityupalakṣaṇena prathamānurāgo vivāhāntaḥ, mānaḥ premāntaḥ, pravāsaḥ, saṃgamāntaḥ, karuṇaḥ, pratyujjīvanāntaḥ, *prabandhe kartavya ityupadiśyate | ‘mantradūta’ ityādipuruṣakārāyatta*siddhi*sūcanenādyūnatādinirāsānnāyakasya sattvotkarṣaḥ prakāśyate | ‘nāvarṇanaṃ nagaryāderdoṣāya’ ityādinā tu puruṣārthāsattvopakāritvena* śailartūdyānacandrodayamadhupānaratotsavādīnāṃ mantradūtaprayogājināyakābhyudapādīnāṃ* ca niyamena prayogaḥ, śeṣāṇāṃ tu prabandhaśarīrānurodheneti pratipādyate | ‘guṇataḥ’ prāgupanyasya nāyakaṃ tena vidviṣām | nirākaraṇam’ ityanena guṇavatā bhāvyaṃ na guṇadveṣiṇeti jñāpyate | ‘vaṃśavīryaśrutādīni’ ityādinā punarābhijātyauddhatyaśauṇḍīryavīryādaya* eva śatrorvarṇanīyā na tvavacchedahetavo nyāyyācaraṇabinayādaya iti pratyāyyate | ‘dhinoti naḥ’ iti tvayameva pakṣaḥ śreyāniti granthakāreṇa svābhiprāyaḥ prakāśyate ||

iti nigaditabhaṅa‍gyānaṅa‍gasarvasvametad vividhamapi manobhirbhāvayanto 'sya bhedam* | [page 744] tadanubhavasamutthānandasaṃmīlitākṣāḥ pariṣadi paritoṣaṃ hanta santaḥ prayāntu || 526 ||
yāvanmūrdhni himāṃśukandalabhṛti svarvāhinī dhūrjaṭeryāvadvakṣasi kaustubhastabakitā lakṣmīrmuradveṣiṇaḥ | yāvaccittabhuvastrilokavijayaprauḍhaṃ dhanuḥ kausumaṃ bhūyāttāvadiyaṃ kṛtiḥ kṛtadhiyāṃ karṇāvataṃsotpalam || 527 ||

iti śrīmahārājādhirājaśrībhojadevaviracite sarasvatīkaṇṭhābharaṇālaṃkāre rasavivecano nāma pañcamaḥ paricchedaḥ |

samāpto 'yaṃ granthaḥ |

śubhamastu |
